paribhāṣāvṛtteḥ prathamādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ sphuradabhinavarāgā bhāskarābhā pragalbhā prasabhaśamitadoṣā sphītasallokacakrā vihitahitavicārā jāḍyajātopaśāntyai prabhavatu paribhāṣāvṛttirāsevitaiṣā   vyākhyānato viśeṣapratipattirna hi sandehādalakṣaṇam   vyākhyānādācāryapāramparyopadeśātsandehepi viśeṣāvagamo bhavati na tu lakṣaṇābhāva iti tena ṣaṣṭho sthāneyogenetyasya pratyākhyāne ṣaṣṭhonirdeśeṣvanekasabandhasabhavepi sthāneyogaiva bhavati tadukta vyākhyānato viśeṣapratipattirna hi sandehādalakṣaṇamiti sthāneyogeti vyākhyāsyāmaiti tathā catvāryaṇagrahaṇāni pūrveṇa ṇakāreṇa aṇaditsarvarṇasya cāpratyaya ityeka pareṇa iṇgrahaṇāni tu pareṇaiveti atra yuktayopi yathāsabhavamabhidhīyante tatra keṇaḥ dralope pūrvasya dīrghoṇa ityatrāṇagrahaṇasāmarthādavasīyate pūveṇeti yadi pareṇa syāt acāmeva hrasvadīrghābhyā bhāvyam etaccācaśca iti paribhāṣayaiva siddha tatkimaṇagrahaṇeneti saiṣā yuktiḥ śakyate vyabhicārayitum  acaścetyeva siddhayo hrasvadīrghayoryadaṇgrahaṇa karoti tasyaitatprayojanamanacopyaṇo dīrghahrasvau yathā syātām agīṣkaḥ adhūṣkaḥ śvaliṅkaḥ  madhuliṅkaḥ vaḍhā varḍhumiti  eva ca laṇityatra yannyāsakṛtokta ke pare halāmaṇāmasabhavādityāditathā dīrghaśrutyācaśceti sanidhāpiteca eva dīrghatvena bhavitavyamityādi taccintyam atra ke ciccintayanti agīṣka ityādau visarjanīyādiṣu kṛteṣu hakāroṇ rephaśca nāsti na cāstyasiddhatvam na mune iti yogavibhāgena niṣiddhatvāt anabhidhāna tu na vaktavyam roḥ supi ityatrāgīṣkādīnā nyāse vyākhyātatvāt dīrghavidhau ca varḍhā varḍhumityādau pareṇa ṇakāreṇa pratyāhāragrahaṇādanacopi rephasya yaddīrghatvamuktam tanna yadyetatprayojana syāt tadā hayavarataṣṭakāreṇa pratyāhāra kuryāt dralope pūrvasya dīrghoṭa iti  atha vāstu varḍhā varḍhumityādau dīrgha eva ṝkāraḥ tathāpi kṛte tasminnādguṇa ityakāraṛkārayorguṇenākāre raparatve ca kṛte tadeva rūpa varḍhā  varḍhumiti  atocaśca iti siddhi yadaṇgrahaṇa tatpūrveṇa ṇakāreṇa pratyāhārārtham na ca pareṇa ṇakāreṇa pratyāhāragrahaṇe rephasya dīrghavaiyarthyātpunarādguṇabādhaḥ kalpanīyaḥ eva hi sāmarthyadvaya syāt savarṇavidhau pareṇa ṇakāreṇa pratyāhāragrahaṇe urṛt iti taparakaraṇa jñāpakam  yadi tatrāpi pūrveṇa syāt eva ca sūtropāttasya mātrikasya sthāne sūtropātte ṛkāre vidhīyamāne sāvarṇyābhāvād dvimātrikasya prāptireva nāstīti  taparakaraṇamanarthaka syāt   yacca laṇityatra nyāsakṛtokta dīrghasyāpi sthānino yathāśrutena hrasvenaiva bhavitavyamiti taparakaraṇamanarthaka syād vyāvarttyābhāvāditi tatra dvimātrikasya sthānitva yaduktam tadasaṅgatam ādeśavatsthāninopi dvimātrasyābhāvāt atha jātau dvimātrasya sthānitvamiti cenna evamādeśepi dvimātratvaprasaṅgaḥ atha sthānina prati jātirādeśa prati vyaktiretacca na hṛdayagrāhi eva tarhi ṛkāraṝkārayoḥ samāhāradvandvaikatvena napusakahrasvatvena ca urṛditi nirddeśe dīrghasyāpi sthānitvam numabhāvastvāgamaśāsanasyānityatvāt idamatha yuktam vyaktirekeṇapratyāhāre ṝkārasyānantarbhāvāt sāvarṇyen ṛkāreṇa ṝkārasyāgrahaṇāddṛkārasyāctva nāsti atoco hrasvatva vidhīyamānamṝkārasya katha syāt ucyate hrasvo napusake prātipadikasya ityanenāco hrasvatva vidhīyate  acpratyāhāre ca ṛkārosti tatra ṛkāreṇa ṛtvajāterāśrayaṇād dvimātrikasyāpi ṝkārasya hrasvatvena bhāvyameveti yukta dīrghasyāpi sthānina ityādi iya ca paribhāṣā laṇityatra bhāṣyakāreṇa jñāpitā taduktam  ki punaraya varṇotsattāvibra ṇakārassandehaheturanubaddhopi punaranubadhyate yasmādanenāṇgrahaṇeyviṇgrahaṇeṣu ca sadehaḥ ki pūrveṇa pareṇa  veti eva tarhi jñāpayatyācāryo bhavatyeṣā paribhāṣā vyākhyānata ityādi   atha katha viśeṣapratipattirityatra ṣaṣṭhīsamāsaḥ yāvatā karmaṇi ca ityanena pratiṣedhena bhāvyam na ca kṛdyogalakṣaṇā ṣaṣṭhī samasyata ityanena samāsaḥ śakyate karttum tadviṣaye eva karmaṇi cetyasyārambhāt ucyate karmaṇi cetyanenobhayaprāptau karmaṇi ityanena niyamena yā ṣaṣṭhī tasyā eva samāsapratiṣedho vijñāyate atra cārthe karttari ca iti sūtra pramāṇam anyathā apā sraṣṭā odanasya bhojaka ityādau karmaṇi cetyanenaiva pratiṣedhasya siddhatvāt karttari cetyanarthaka syāt na ca praiṣyasya hārayitā praiṣyasya kārayitā ityatra hṛkroranyatarasyām iti karttari ṣaṣṭhīsamāsapratiṣedhārthamidamiti tṛjakābhyā karttari ityanenaiva tatsiddhiḥ yattu tṛjakābhyā karttarītyatra vṛttāvukta tṛjgrahaṇamuttarārthamiti tatkarttari ceti sūtre sthite iti aṇyantāpekṣayoktamuttarārthamityeke  ubhayaprāptāviti niyamena ca ṣaṣṭhī ṣaṣṭhī hetuprayoge ityataḥ prayogagrahaṇānuvṛtteryatra sāmarthyaprāpta kartṛkarmaṇorubhayorupādāna tatraiva  yathā syāt  yathā āścaryo gavā dohogopālakeneti  tathā hyatrāścarya pratipādya tacca durdohānā gavā karmaṇāmasuśikṣitasyāgopālakasya ca karttuḥ sāmarthyaprāpte upādāne ṣaṣṭhī bhavati nānyathā viśeṣapratipattirityatra tu śiṣyādeḥ karturakicitkaratvānna sāmarthyaprāpta kartturupādānam eva ca sati antarddhau yenādarśanamicchati ityatra yeneti tṛtīyā na yuktā kartṛkarmaṇoḥ kṛti iti karttari ṣaṣṭhīvidhānāt ucyate nirddeśādeva tṛtīyetyadoṣaḥ anyastvācaṣṭe gamyamānepi karmaṇi ubhayaprāptāviti niyamo bhavatyeva  tathā cāntarddhau yenādarśanamicchatītyatra nyāsakṛtā ubhayaprāptau karmaṇi ityatra rakṣitena ca gamyamānepi karmaṇi niyamātṣaṣṭhyabhāvena  antarddhau yeneti nirddeśasiddhiruktā  ki tvevamaiuṇityatra tasya grahaṇa bhavatyekeneti tatra tasyeti karttari ṣaṣṭhīti nyāse yadukta tanna śobhanam tathā hyatrāpi gamyamāne grāhye karmaṇi ubhayaprāptāviti niyamātṣaṣṭyā na bhavitavyam etacca śabdānuśāsane nyāsakṛtā vyākhyātam yattu tatra svamatimahimaprāgalbhyādanunyāsakāro vyājahāra yatra sāmarthyaprāptamubhayorupādāna sa ubhayaprāptau karmaṇītyasya viṣayaḥ anyathā kartṛkarmaṇoḥ kṛtītyasya vidherubhayaprāptāvityādeśca viṣayavibhāgo na syāt na cākartṛka karmāstīti nyāyāditi tadayuktam purā bhettā devadatta ityādau abhihite kartari niyamāprasaṅgāt atrocyate  ṣaṣthī hetuprayoge ityatonuvarttamānamapi prayogagrahaṇamanaṅgīkṛtya yathā yuṣmābhirgamyamāne karmaṇi ubhayaprāptāviti niyama ucyate tathāsmābhirapyanabhihitādhikāramanaṅgīkṛtya  vibhāgābhāva uktaḥ  etaccāyuktam akākārayīḥ pratiṣedhoḥ vaktavya ityanyena yatra niyamo bādhyate tatra vidheḥ kṛtārthatvāt cikīrṣāraverālokānāmiti tathā kāryaḥ kaṭo devadattasyetyatrābhihite karmaṇi ṣaṣṭhīprasaṅgācca ucyate kartṛkarmaṇoḥ kṛtītyasya vidherubhayaprāptāvityādeśca vidheriti naite samānādhikaraṇe ṣaṣṭyau ki tarhi vaiyadhikaraṇye tadayamarthaḥ kartṛkaraṇoḥ kṛtītyasya sabandhī yo vidhiḥ karttari ca ititathobhayaprāptau karmaṇītyasya yo vidhiḥ karmaṇi ca iti etayorviṣayavibhāgo na syādityayamabhiprāyaḥ  yadi gamyamānepi karttari ubhayaprāptāviti karmaṇi niyamaḥ syāt tadā idhmavraścana ityādāvapi karaṇe lyuṭi karmaṇi ceti niṣedhaḥ syāt kartṛlyuṭyapi  idhmapravraścano devadatta ityatrāpi ātmanā devadattenetyasya karturgamyamānatvādubhayaprāptiravyāhataiva  eva ca karmaṇi yā kā citṣaṣṭhī tasyā eva sarvasyāḥ karmaṇi cetyanena samāsapratiṣedhe siddhe kartari cetyanārambhaṇīya syāt ārabdha cāto yuktamukta viṣayavibhāgo na syāditi etacca na ātmanetyasya kartturgasyamānatve pramāṇābhāvāt eva tarhi purāmbhettā devadatta ityādau yathā kartturabhihitatvānniyamo na bhavati tathā śabdānuśāsanamityatrāpi karturaprayogāt tatra yathā karttṛṣaṣṭhīprāptyā vināpi gamyamāne karttari niyama ucyate tathābihitepi karttari niyamamuttkā niyamamuktāviṣayavibhāga uktaḥ eva ca vidhiniyamavākyayoreva viṣayavibhāgābhāvaḥ etaccākākārayoḥ prayoge vidheḥ kṛtārthatvānāśrayaṇenocyate   na hi kāryī nimittatvenāśīyate   yatkāryabhāk tatkarya prati nimitta na bhavatītyarthaḥ tenādhyetā adhyāpakaḥ śayitā śāyaka ityatra iṅśīṅorṅitvāt kṅiti ca iti guṇavṛddhipratiṣedho na bhavati tathāririṣatītyatra dvirvacaneci iti sthānivadbhāvo na bhavati yadi syāt iso dvirvacane kṛterīṣatīti syāt jñāpaka cātra dīdhīvevīṭām ityatra ṅitorapi dīdhīṅvevīṅorguṇavṛddhipratiṣedhārthamupādānam na ca kṅiti cetyanena iglakṣaṇāyā eva vṛddheḥ pratiṣedhaḥ kriyateatojlakṣaṇāyā api vṛddheḥ pratiṣedhārtha dīdhīvevyorubhayorupādāna syāditi vācyam indhibhavatibhyā ca ityatra bhavatigrahaṇenājlakṣaṇāyā api vṛddheḥ pratiṣedho bhavatītyasyārthasya jñāpitatvāt nanu ca bhāṣye vuko nityatvādindheścchāndasatvādindhibhavativyā ceti sūtra pratyākhyāta tathā dīdhīvevīṭāmityapi yadāha dīdhīvevyorgrahaṇamanarthaka anayośchāndasatvāt ādīdhet ādīdhayurityatra guṇadarśanācca iṭaścāpi grahaṇamanarthaka neḍvaśi kṛti ityata iḍgrahaṇānuvṛttau ārddhadhātukasyeḍvalādeḥ ityatra yadiḍgahaṇa tadiṭo vikārābhāvārtham tato laghūpadhaguṇābhāvāt siddha kaṇitā śvo raṇitā śva iti na caiva pipaṭhīrapāṭhīdityādāvapi dīrghatva na syāditi vaktavyam yataḥ samānajātīyatayāṅgakāryameva vyāvarttyate grahītetyatra tu graholiṭi ityādisūtrārambhād dīrghatvam tarhi pipaṭhīṣi brāhmaṇakulānītyatra sāntamahataḥ sayogasya iti dīrghatva na syāditi cenna numevātra nāsti numi karttavyellopasya sthānivattvenājhalantatvāt na ca kvau lupte na sthānivadityasti kvau vidha prati na sthānivaditīda vārttikamiti kaiyaṭena vyākhyātam eva ca kvau nātra num api tu sarvanāmasthāne vāmanastu kvau lupta ityeva manyate tathā ca maparyantasya ityatra tena parigrahaṇa varjanīyārthamityuktam tena yatraiva varjanīyamasti tatraivādeśa iti tena yuṣmadasmadorṇici ṭilopaḥ yuṣmayateḥ kvip tataḥ svādayaḥ atra varjanīyābhāvādādeśā na bhavanti na cāsti ṇilopasya sthānivattvam kvau lupte na sthānivaditi vacanāt tadeva sthitametat bhāṣyamate na hi kāryītyasyā liṅga nāsti sthaṇḍilācchayitari ityatra śayitarīti nirddeśosyā liṅga kuṭādiṣu kuṅ śabde ityasya pāṭho vā anye tu vyācakṣate iglakṣaṇavṛddhipratiṣedhastāvat kṅitpratyayanimittaka eva sabhavati na tu kṅiddhātunimittakaḥ  ato mṛṣṭaḥ mṛṣṭavān nyanuvīt nyaghuvīt ityādau kṅinnimittakaḥ pratyaya eva parato vṛddhipratiṣedhastatsāhacaryād guṇapratiṣedhopi bhūyate  bobhūyate ityādau kaṅinnimittakaḥ pratyaya eva kartavyaḥ  ata evādhyetā śayitetyatra kṅiddhātunimittakena pratiṣedhena na bhavitavyam  aririṣātītyatrāpi dvirvacaneci ityajādeśa prati nimittabhāvokāryitvenaiva niyataḥ tadevamajādeśasabandhecītyasyākāryitva tatsāhacaryād  dvirvacanavidhānepi yadyakāryitvamevācītyasya tadā sthānivattva yathā cakruturiti  aririṣatītyatra tu dvitīyasyakāco dvirvacanādikārasya dvirvacanabhāktamiti dvirvacanavidhānecītyasya kāryitva na punarakāryitvamiti tasmātparibhāṣā prayojanābhāvānna svīkarttavyā yukta caitat anyathā asyā satyā prorṇunaviṣatītyatra guṇāvādeśayoḥ kṛtayordvicanecīti sthānivattva na syāt sannantasya kāryitvāt  tathā dvirvacanecītyatrācīti kimityuktā heghrīyate dedhmīyate iti yatpratyudāhṛta tannopapadyate dvyaṅgavaikalyāt yathaiva yaṅ ajādirna bhavati  tathā dvirvacananimittamapīti  tatra tahīrda vaktavyam kāryamanubhavanneva kāryo nimittatvena nāśīyatejeghrīyata ityatra kāryamananubhavan nimittatvenāśrīyate anyanstu nāśrita eva tathā hi aririṣatītyatra sthānivattvena iso dvirvacanaprasaṅgādajādereva sanaḥ kāryitva nimittatva ca prorṇunaviṣatītyatra tu ajādeḥ sano nimittatva kāryitva ca dhātornuśabdasyaiva tasyaiva dvirvacanavidhānāt atotra sanaḥ sākṣāt kāryitva nāstīti yuktameva nimittatvenāśrayaṇamiti evamapi śādhītyatra śāhau ityasya śādeśasya dhibhāva prati samānāśraye hāvasiddhatvanna syāditi dhibhāvasya sthānino hiśabdasyānimittatvena samānanimittatvābhāvāt tatra vaktavya prāyikametat lakṣyavaśāt kva cidāśrīyate   itaretarāśrayāṇyapi kāryāṇi śāstre prakalpante   itaretarāśrayāṇi kāryāṇi viroddhānna pravarttanta iti nyāyaḥ yaduktamitaretarāśrayatvādaprasiddhiriti tadapavādoyamārabhyate apiśabdaḥ kva cidarthe tadayamarthaḥ kva ciditaretarāśrayāṇi pravarttanta iti yathā vanasihayoḥ parasparāśrayāpi rakṣā pravarttate tathā śāstre gārgīya ityādau vṛddhisajñayā bhāvitasyāpi vṛddhisajñā prakliptiḥ anyathā śālārairauprabhṛtiṣu sāvakāśā vṛddhisajñā itaretarāśrayatvānna syāt jñāpaka cātra igyaṇaḥ saprasāraṇam ityatra saprasāraṇena yaṇaḥ sthāne iko bhāvyante yaṇsthānikānā cekā saprasāraṇasajñeti itaretarāśrayatvam kathametadanyathā prakalpate yadītaretarāśrayatva kva cinna syāditi bhāgavṛttikārastvāha nityaśabdānāmanvākhyānamātramidamiti tato netaretarāśrayadoṣaḥ yadukta sarvāṇītaretarāśrayāṇi bhāṣye parihṛtāni siddha tu nityaśabdatvāditīti athaitatsyāt yaṇaḥ sthāne igvidhīyate sthānyādeśabhāvaśca pauruṣeyaḥ tatkṛto nityatvamiti naiṣa doṣāḥ  loke hi iṣṭa yaṣṭetyādayo nityāḥ tatra yajerarthe ijirviśiṣṭaviṣaye sādhurityetāvati puruṣāśrayatva svabhāvata eva yajeḥ sthāne ijisiddhiḥ āgamāstaṅguṇībhūtāstadgrahaṇena gṛhyante    ādyantau ṭākitau ityatrādyantaśabdayoravayavavacanatvāt ṭitkitorāgamayorādyantāvayavatvamatidiṣṭa midacontyātpara ityatrāpi antagrahaṇanuvṛttyā  mitopyantāvayavatvam  avayavāścāvayavigrahaṇena gṛhyante ityuktamataḥ siddheya paribhāṣā āgamāstadguṇībhūtā iti sukhapratipattyartha ca jñāpakamapi kecidāhaḥ ṇeraniṭi ityatrāniṭīti pratiṣedhaḥ yadyāgamigrahaṇenāgamo na gṛhyeta tadā kārayitavyamityādau itā vyavahitatvādeva ṇilopo na prāpnotīti kimaniṭītyaneneti jñāpakam tena sarveṣāmityatra suṭaḥ subgrahaṇena grahaṇājjhalādau supi etva siddhyati nanu asyā satyā cicchidatuḥ cicchiduḥ ityādau halādiḥ śeṣeṇa tuko nivṛttiḥ prāpnoti ucyate halādiḥ śeṣa ityatrāṭaturāṭurittyādisiddhyartha jātipakṣa āśritaḥ tatracaikameveda lakṣaṇa sakṛdeva papāṭhetyādau anāderhalo nivṛtti karoti tadeva cicchidaturityādau halādiḥ śeṣānantara yastuk tasya nivṛttirna prāpnoti lakṣaṇābhāvāt avaśya caitat anyathājāderdvitīyasyetyatra bhāṣyakāreṇa ca maitreyeṇa ca yadudāhṛtam oṇeruvoṇiṣatīti syāditi sāvakāśameva dvitīyadvirvacanamiti tadasaṅgata syāt halādiḥ śeṣeṇa vakāralopaprasaṅgāt yadyeva vavṛte ityādau urattve raparatve ca kṛte rephasya lopo na syāt ucyate halādiḥ śeṣa ityatra urat ityanuvarttiṣyate tena uraditi kṛte rephasya nivṛttirbhaviṣyati eva tarhi uñcheraiñcicchadityatra tuki kṛte halādiḥ śeṣeṇa tasya nivṛttiḥ syādeva ucyate checa ityatra hrasvagrahaṇenuvarttamāne punaryaccakāreṇa tasyānuvarttana tatsāmarthyāt hrasva āgamī svīkriyate na tu hrasvāntaḥ samudāyaḥeva cābhyāsāvayavasyaiva bhaktastuk kriyate tatsāmarthyādihāvayavāvayavopi avayavigrahaṇena na gṛhyate anyatra tu gṛhyata eva ataeva śerata ityatrāvayavāvayavaḥ samudāyāvayavo bhavatītyuktā śīṅo ruṭ ityatra śīṅaḥ sārvadhātuke guṇa uktaḥ eva tu śobhanacchāya ityatra tukā uttarapadasya vyavadhānātpuvadbhāvo na syāditi dūṣaṇam ucyate hrasva pratīda jñāpaka padāntādvā ityatra tu nāsti dadhi chādayatītyatra svaravidhau vyañjanamavidyamānavaditi tiṅñatiṅa iti nighātaḥ śakyate karttum asyā satyā prātipadikāntanum vibhaktiṣu ca ityatra numgrahaṇasya prayojana na dṛśyate bhartṛhariṇā tūktam yaḥ prātipadikānto nakāro na bhavati tadartha numgrahaṇa prāhiṇvaditi atra hi hiverlaṅi numo ṇatvamiti tatra ca pūvapadādhikāraḥ samāse ca pūvottarapadavyavahāraḥ tatkathamiha ṇatvamiti na vyaktīkṛtamiti bhāgavṛttikṛtoktam yadyeva prahiṇvannityetadartha tarhi numgrahaṇa syāt ucyate  alpāctaramityanena prātipadikānta ityādau numaḥ pūrvanipāte karttavye yatprātipadikavibhaktimadhyastha numgrahaṇa karoti tadeva bodhayati  yonayoreva madhyastho numnakārastasya ṇatva bhavatīti   aṭkughāṅnumvyavāsepi ityatra bhāgavṛttikṛtā pratipādita numaḥ pūvanipātalakṣaṇavyabhicāracihnāt prenvamityatra ṇatvābhāvaḥ kṣubhnādityādvā  tena saha samānam  nanu mitvānnumaḥ pūrvāntatve niṣkauśāmvinī kule ityatra paratvānnumi kṛte napusakahrasvatva na prāpnoti ajantatvābhāvāt yathā suvāk brāhmaṇakulamiti naiṣa doṣaḥ vibhaktyāśrayaṇād bahiraṅgo num hrasvatamantaraṅga vibhaktyanāśrayatvāt tatprathama bhaviṣyati taduktam na vā bahiraṅgalaṇatvāditi   nirddiśyamānasyādeśa bhavanti   ṣaṣṭhyā nirddiṣṭasya samudāyasya tadekadeśasya vādeśā bhavanti tadyathā pādaḥ pat iti ṣaṣṭhyā nirddhiṣṭasyaiva pādaḥ sthāne padbhavati dvipadaḥ paśyeti nāṅgādhikāraparibhāṣayā tadantasya tathā bhavetāmityatra tasaḥ sthāne tāmādeśo bhavati na sayāsuṭaḥ tadekadeśasya yathā udaḥ sthāstambhoḥ pūrvasya iti tiṣṭhaterādideśasya pūrvasavarṇo vidhīyamāna udasthādityatrāṭo na bhavati tathā ṣyaṅaḥ samprasāraṇam iti ṣyaṅekadeśasya samprasāraṇe vārāhīputra ityatrānayā rephavakārayoḥ samprasāraṇābhāvo vyākhyātaḥ iya paribhāṣā ṣaṣṭhī sthāne yogā ityasyārthe paṭhyate tathā hi tatra bhāṣyam yadyapyekaśata ṣaṣdyarthāḥ yāvantaste tāvantaḥ ṣaṣṭhyāmuccāritāyā sarve prāpnuvanti arthā ye punaḥ samīpāntaravikārādyāḥśabdasya tu konyo bhavitumarhati anyadataḥ sthānāt nanu śabdasyāpyanantarādayaḥ sambandhāḥ sambhavanti astebhūrbhavatīti sandehaḥ ki sthāne samīpe vā tatra samīpe na bhaviṣyati dvayorekārthayorekatra prayogānupapatteḥ ki ca sandehamātramatat sarvasandeṣvidamupatiṣṭhate bhavati hi vyākhyānato viśeṣapratipattirna hi sandehādalakṣaṇamiti sthāne iti vyākhyāsyāmaḥ na tarhīdānīmaya yogo vaktavyaḥ vaktavyaḥ ki prayojana ṣaṣṭhyanta sthāne yathā prasajyeta yataḥ ṣaṣṭhī uccāritā tadeva kāryopayogi yathā syāt tadetenaitatpratipādita nirddiśyamānasyādeśā bhavantīti  asyā satyā śīṅo ruṭ ityatra yannyāsakṛtokta yadi ruḍāgamo jhakārasyaiva syāt tadādādeśo jhakārasya na syāt tasyaiva ruṭaḥ syāt ādeḥ parasyeti  vacanāt  tathā maparyantasya ityatra yadudāhṛta yuvakāmiti sākackasya syāditi etadanapekṣya tatsamādheyam   nānubandhakṛtamanekāltvam   anubandhakṛtamanekāltva nāśrīyate tenārvaṇastrasāvanaña iti arvantau arvanta ityatra trādeśontyasyaiva bhavati na sarvasya ke cittu dyubhyā dyubhirityudāharanti tanna śobhanam diva ut ityanena ukārasyaiva vidhānāt tathā hi taparastatkālasya iti udityeṣā sajñā ukāramātrasyaiva vidhīyate eva ca diva udityanena ukāra eva kevalo vidhīyate na tūcchabdaḥ avaśya caitat anyathātobhisa aisa ityatra kā gatiḥ syāt na hyatrāta ādeśo vidhīyate ki tarhi atsajñayā akāraḥ sajñī nirddiśyate yattu sthāghvoricca ityatrokta icca kasya takārettvamiti tatpratipādakaikadeśānā pratipādyaikadeśatvamabhyupagamya tatmatenaiva titsvaritam ityatra tiditi pratyayagrahaṇamiti bhāṣye uktam taparastatkālasya ityatra tu varṇa eva sajñītyukta na punastaparaḥ samudāyaḥ yukta caitat anyathā taparastatkālasyetyatra svagrahaṇānuvṛttyā bhavadbhirityatrāpyais syāt iya ca paribhāṣā anubandhā avayavā ityatra pakṣe jñāpaka cātrānekālśitsarvasya ityatra śidgrahaṇam yadyanubandhenāpyanekāltva syāt tadā sarve ityādau śībhāvasyānekāltvādeva sarvādeśe jasaḥ siddhe śidgrahaṇamanarthaka syāt  nanu dhvasoreddhāvabhyāsalopaśca iti lopaḥ śidvaktavya iti yaḥ śidabhyupagamyate tatra sarvādeśārtha śidgrahaṇa syāt dehi dhehīti sarvasyaiva  lopo bhavati  ucyate yadetallopasya śittvamāśrita tatsāmarthyādeva sarvādeśo bhaviṣyati atha vā lopaḥ śidvaktavya iti nāśrayaṇīyam nānarthakelontyavidhiriti survasyaiva lopo bhaviṣyati yattūcyate tatrānabhyāsavikāreṣviti tallakṣyasthityā na sarvatreti nanu yadi iya paribhāṣāsti ṇal tarhi sarvādeśo na prāpnoti ucyate ānupūrvyāt siddhamidam tathā hi sarvādeśe sati ṇalo ṇakārasyopadeśe pratyayāditvamiti tataścuṭū itītsajñā tatastasyānubandhatvam tadeva sarvādeśapūrvakamanubandhatva sarvādeśatā vihantu na kṣamate sarvādeśatāyāḥ pūrvameva niṣpannatvāt   varṇāśraye vidhau pratyayalakṣaṇa na bhavati tena gave hita gohita rāyaḥ kula raikulamityatra pratyayalakṣaṇenācīti avāyādeśau na bhavataḥ lavaṇā yavāgūrityatra lavaṇāllugiti ṭhako lukikṛte pratyayalakṣaṇena ṭhagantāṭṭiḍḍhāṇañ iti ṅībna bhavati ṅīpo varṇamātrāśrayatva yathā syādityevamarthamakārastatrānuvṛttaṣṭidādibhirviśeṣyate na tvakāreṇa ṭidādayaḥ ata eva kvarapkhyunāmiti ṣaṣṭhyā nirddeśaḥ kṛtaḥ aya cārthaḥ pratyayalope pratyayalakṣaṇam ityatra dvitīyena pratyayagrahaṇena sādhitaḥ tathāhi tatroktam  tallakṣaṇamiti vaktavye pratyayalakṣaṇamityatra yatpunaḥ pratyayagrahaṇa pratyayāśritameva kārya pratyayalakṣaṇena yathā syāt yathā suptiṅanga  padam iti acītyetadvarṇamātrāśrita mābhūditi jñāpaka cātra śravaṇākārttikīcaitrībhya iti śravaṇeti ṭabanto nirddeśaḥ nanu yadi varṇāśraye pratyayalakṣaṇa nāsti tarhi atṛṇeḍityatra tṛṇahaim iti im na prāpnoti imāgamasya halvarṇāśrayatvāt ucyate nāya varṇāśrayopi tvaṅgādhikāreṇa pratyayākṣepāddhalādipratyayāśrayaḥ  etadukta bhavati pratyaye dvividha kārya pratyayanimittamapratyayanimitta ca tatra pratyayanimitta yattadeva pratyayalopalakṣaṇena yathā  syāditaranmābhūdityevamartha pratyayalope pratyayalakṣaṇamityatra dvitīya pratyayagrahaṇam   tenaicoyavāyāva ityavādirvaṇāśrayatvātparibhāṣayā khaṇḍyate imāgamastu pratyayanimitta eva aṅgādhikāreṇa pratyayākṣepāttadbhavane ko virodhaḥ na caiva śriyai ida śryarthamityatrājādipratyaye iyaṅṅāśaṅkanīyaḥ na lumatāṅgasya iti pratiṣedhāt yattu śāsa idaṅhaloḥ ityatrāsyāḥ prāyikatvamuktā nyāsakāreṇātṛṇeḍityatra varṇāśrayepīmāgamo bhavatītyuktam tadupāyāntaram nanu gohitamityādau luko vidhāna na tu lopasya tadeva pratyayalakṣaṇasya prasaṅga eva nāsti tatki paribhāsāśrayaṇena ucyate lukyapi pratyayalakṣaṇa bhavati lopasyādarśanārthatvāt pramāṇa cātra na lumatāṅgasyeti pratiṣedhaḥ   kva cetyatra ṭita ātmanepadānā ṭere ityatra ca bhāṣyakhyākhyāna rakṣitenoktam ki tvevamiṭodityatrāpi dvayorāgamapratyayayorgrahaṇa prāpnoti tatheḍvahimahiṅityatra pratyāhārtha varṇāntare karttavye ghusajñāyā nergadādi sūtreṇa ṇatva nāsti dādhāśabdau prati nerūpasargasajñāyā abhāvāttathā ca bhāṣyam na cetau dādhau prati kriyāyoga iti sani mīmāghu ityādau cāṅgasya ghorgrahaṇādasakārāditvācca pratyākhyātam yadyeva nipātatvād yadavyayatva tatsāmarthyādeva subluk siddhaḥ naitat nipātatvasya svarārthatvamātreṇopapannatvāt anarthakatva tu praśabdasya prakarṣārthasya prakarṇādināvagatatvāt ityatra bhāṣye jñāpitā tatra hyukta rūpagrahaṇa na karttavyam sva śabdasyetyucyamāne yadyapi śabdasya rūpamarthaśca sva bhavati tathāpi rūpameva grāhya nārthaḥ yataḥ śabdoccāraṇe rūpapratipattirādau siddhe vyākaraṇaśāstre rūpavadarthopyaṅgīkriyata iti labhyate atha vā vraścādi sūtre bhrājagrahaṇamasyāstitve jñāpakam yadi hyanarthakasyāpi grahaṇa syāttadā rājagrahaṇenaiva bhrājaikadeśasyāpi grahaṇe siddhe rājabhrājeti bhrājagrahaṇa na kuryāt kṛta cāto jñāpakamarthavata eva grahaṇa nānarthakasyeti   na varṇagrahaṇeṣu   pūrvāpavādoyam varṇā akārādayaḥ tadgrahaṇerthavarparibhāṣā nāsti yatheko yaṇaci iti nirarthakasyāpīko nirarthakepi yaṇ bhavati bhavatyatra bhavatviti anyathā ṅībādisabandhina eva sārthakasyekaḥ sārthake evāci yaṇ syāt kumāryauśvaśvāviti tathāsya ghvau iti nirarthakasyāpi bhavati śklīkarotīti anyathārthavata eva viṣṇuvācakākārasya syāt  iko jhal ityatregiti yoya varṇasamudāyaḥ sa ki sārthakaḥ pratyāhāro gṛhyatā nirarthako vā dhāturiti vicāre yuktameva ānarthakyamuktam  kathamiḍgrahaṇerthavatparibhāṣābhidhīyate yāvatā āto lopa iṭi ca ityatroktamiḍvahimahiṅityatra ṭhe karttavye ṭitkaraṇamāgamapratyayayorubhayorapi  grahaṇārthamiti  tadeva yaṇaci ityatrāpyanubandhopādānādanayā nopasthātavyam naitadasti kakārādīnā samudāyānubandhatvādigiti nekārādīnā sānubandhānāmupādānam samudāyānubandhānāmavayavānubandhatā na svīkriyate karmeṇiṅ iti samudāyānubandhatvepyavayavānubandhatvamiti yastu svādi sūtre auḍasiti kṛte ḍitvāṭṭilopo doṣa uktaḥ sonuparābhyā kṛña ityasya sāmānyajñāpakatvamabhyupagamya boddhavyaḥ yadapyukta sāgamakasyaivārthavattvamiṇmātra tvanarthakamiti tadapi na prakriyākrameṇāgamāstadguṇībhūtāstadgrahaṇena gṛhyante ityāśrayaṇāt bhindyuḥprastāve tvanāgamakānā sāgamakā ādeśā bhavantītyāśritam yaccāpyukta ṭhe karttavye ṭittvātsāmānyagrahaṇamityādi tadapi na sati prayojane jñāpakāt pratyayāgamayorgrahaṇamucyate vija iṭ ityitra na ki cidāgamasya ṅittve prayojanam atannimittatvād guṇasya iṭot ityatra ca prākaraṇikasyeṭodādeśavidhānātkuta āgamaprasaṅgāśaṅketi jñāpaka cātroña iti sūtram  yadyarthavatparibhāṣā varṇagrahaṇepi syāttadā u itītyatretiśabdekārenarthakerthavatparibhāṣayaiva yaṇādeśāprasaṅgaḥ siddha ityuña iti pragṛhyasajñā  na kṛtā syāt  kṛtā cāto jñāpakam atha vā bhakṣyeṇa miśrīkaraṇam iti nirddeśe jñāpakaḥ   bhāvyamānoṇ savarṇānna gṛhṇāti   vidhīyamānoṇ savarṇānā grāhako na bhavati tenehetidama iś iti trimātrasya sthānina āntaratamyāt trimātra ādeśo na bhavati tathā he anaḍvan ityatrāmsabuddhau iti dīrgho na bhavati lavitā lavitumityatra vṝto vā itīṭo vikalpena dīrghavidhānādiṭo na sarvarṇagrahaṇamityāhaḥ iya ca paribhāṣā aṇuditsarvaṇasya cāpratyaya ityatrāpratyaya ityasyaivārthaḥ paṭhyate tathā hi pratyāyyate vidhīyate bhāvyate iti pratyayaḥ na pratyayopratyayaḥabhāvyamāna ityarthaḥ apratyayoṇ sarvarṇān gṛhṇātītyasminnarthe bhāvyamānoṇ savarṇānna gṛhṇātīti vyaktamavatiṣṭhate sukhapratipattyartha jñāpakamapi ke cidāhaḥ īhalyaghoḥ iti dīrghekāravidhānam anyathā dīrghasya sthāne sāvarṇyārddirgha eva syāt anityā ceya paribhāṣā tenāmū ityatra dvimātrasyaukārasya dvimātra evokāro bhavati atra cārthe diva ut iti taparakaraṇa jñāpakam  yadi bhāvyamānoṇ sarvathaiva savarṇānna hṛhṇāti tadā dyubhyāmityatra cchroḥ śūḍanunāsike ca ityūdyapi kṛte dīrghasya sthāne hrasvaḥ siddhaḥ  syāt ki tapakaraṇena  tatkṛta jñāpayati kva cidbhāvyamānoṇ sarkṇan gṛhṇātīti śāsa idaṅ haloḥ iti taparakaraṇa vā jñāpakamiti   yasminvidhistadādāvalgrahaṇe   yasminniti saptamnirdiṣṭe algrahaṇe varṇagrahaṇe yo vidhiḥ sa tadādau samudāye bhavati na tadante tena pivatereśi pape ityatra pāghrādi sūtreṇa pivādeśo na bhavati tathācīti iyaṅṅuvaṅāvajādau bhavataḥśriyo luluvartululuvuriti śriyau luluva ityatrāpi vyapadeśavadbhāvāt yadi hyatra tadantavidhiḥ syāt śriyo luluvaturityatra na syāt halantatvāt aya cārtho yena vidhi sūtre tadantavidyapavādastadādividhirupasakhyātaḥ paribhāṣārūpeṇa padyata iti vāmanena tu guṇopṛkta ityatrāpṛktagrahaṇādiya varṇitā taduktam  uto vṛddhirluki halītyanuvarttamāne halādau guṇe prāptepṛktagrahaṇa halmātra eva yathā syāddhalādau mābhūdityevamartha kriyamāṇa jñāpayatyastīya  paribhāṣā yasminvidhirityādi  tena halītyanuvṛttau halādau syāt apṛktagrahaṇe tu varṇamātra eva bhavati praurṇoditi yadyeva kṅiti saprasāraṇa kṅādāveva syād gṛhīto gṛhītiriti yagādau na syād gṛhyata iti ucyate kṅitīti neda varṇagrahaṇamiti kṅāvitau yasyeti bahubrīhiṇā varṇasamudāyasya parigrahāt   vidhividhānavidhibhājā trayāṇā sanidhāne tadantavidhirbhavati   tena erac itīvarṇāntādattpratyayo bhavati iya paribhāṣā yena vidhi sūtrasyaiva sāmarthyāllabdhorthaḥ padyate tathāhi yeneti karaṇe tṛtīyā na cākartṛka karaṇamastīti karttāpyāśritaḥ sa punariha sabandhiśabdatvādantaśabdenāvayavavācinā sannidhāpitaḥ samudāyo vijñāyate sa ca karttā tribhiḥ prakāraiḥ sannihito bhavati kva cinnirddeśāt yathā īdūdeddvivacanam iti dvivacana karttṛbhūta nirdiṣṭa yattadīdādibhiḥ karaṇaiḥ pragṛhyasajñā vidadhāti kva citprakaraṇāt yathā erac ityatra dhātorityadhikārāt prakaraṇāddhātuḥ karttā sanidhāpitaḥ sa ikāreṇa karaṇenāca vidadhāti kva citsāmarthyāt yathā iko jhal ityatra dhātoreva ca san vidhīyate iti sāmarthyāddhātuḥ karttā sanidhāpita ikā karaṇena sanaḥ kittva vidadhāti  tadevamīdūdeddvivacanamityādau pragṛhyasajñāyā vidhīyamānasya karmaṇo vidherīdūdetaḥ karaṇasya vidhānasya dvivacanasya ca kartturvidhibhājaḥ  sabhavādyena vidhistadantasyeti tadantavidhirvidhīyate  tadeva yena vidhiḥ ityasya sūtrasyārtha evāyamevavidho vidhividhānavidhibhājā trayāṇā sannidhāne tadantavidhirbhavati ecoyavāyāva ityādau vidhibhājosabhavānna pravarttate nanu śabdānuśāsanaprastāvācchabdarūpa karttṛ vidhibhāk syāt tatkatha kartturabhāvobhidhīyate ucyate śabdarūpa kartṛtvena nāśrīyate atiprasaṅgāditi suptiṅanta padam ityatra rakṣitena vyākhyātam tenaicoyavāyāva ityādau śabdarūpasyāsvīkāradejmātrasyaiva sthānitvamajmātrasya paratva naijantasyājādāviti tasya sthānitve vṛkṣāvatretyādāvāvādayonekālatvātsarvādeśāḥ syuḥ nanu nirddiśyamānasyādeśā bhavantītyeca eva sthāne ādeśena bhavitavya naijantasya satyametadvyaktau jātau tu doṣaḥ anyastvāha varnavidhitvamalvidhīnā na syāt tathā na yena vidhi sūtre bhāgavṛttikṛtoktam  iko yaṇaci itīkā acāvayavenāvayavinaḥ samudāyasya sanidhāpitatvādigantasyājādau yaṇādeśa iti varṇavidhireva na syāt tiṣṭhatu dadhyaśāna tva  śākeneti   ki tu satyapogantasyājādau yaṇādeśe padavidhitva na bhavatyeva padasya padāt supsupetyādyanuccāraṇena ṣaṇādeśādikāryāṇā vidhānāditi   iti mahāmahopādhyāyaśrīsīradevakṛtāyā paribhāṣāvṛttau prathamaḥ pādaḥ   ekayoganirddiṣṭānā saha vā pravṛttiḥ saha vā nivṛttiḥ   ekayoganirddiṣṭānā padānā pravṛttirvā nivṛttirvā sahaiva syāt na tvekasya pravṛttiraparasya nivṛttiḥ tena uśca ityatra liṅsicāvātmanepadeṣvityetatsarvamanuvarttate tadayamarthaḥ ṛvarṇāntāddhātoḥ parau liṅsicāvātmanepadeṣu kitau bhavata iti tatra hi ṛ iti ṛvarṇānto dhāturgṛhyate na ṛ gatāviti atra nyāsakāraḥ kāraṇamāha śailīyamācāryasya yatrāsya dhātorgrahaṇamicchati tatrāvaśya śtipā nirddeśa karoti yathārttipiparttyīśca sarttiśāstyarttibhyaśca iti atra ca nyāse sandehavicchedāyetyadhyāhāryam tenāyamarthaḥ yatrāsya dhātorgrahaṇamicchati tatra sandehavicchedāyāvaśya śtipā nirdeśa karoti yatra na sandehastatra karoti na karoti ca eva ca smipūṅrañjvaśā sani ityatra ṛgatāvityasya grahaṇepi na śtipā nirddeśaḥ tatra hi kiraśca pañcabhya ityatra dṛṅdhṛṅorgrahaṇānna sandehaḥ anyathā didiriṣate didhariṣate ityatra smipūṅrañjvaśā sani ityeveṭaḥ siddhatvāṭḍhṛṅdhṛṅorgrahaṇamanarthaka syāt yattu tatra rakṣitenoktam sadehavicchedāyetyatrādhyāhāryam tataśca śmipūṅrañjvaśā sani ityatrāvirodhaḥ kiraśca pañcabhya ityatra kṛgṛsvīkāra eva viccheda heturiti tadayuktam yato vṝto vā ityanuvṛtto iṭ sani vā iti vikalpeneṭi prāpte nityamiṭo vidhānārtha kṛgṝgrahaṇa syāt ucyate yadi nityamiṭo vidhānārtha kṝgṝgrahaṇa syāt tadā kiraśca pañcabhya iti sūtramakṛtvā smipūṅrañjvaśkṛgṛpracchā sanītyeva kuryāt na cottaratra rudādibhyaḥ sārvadhātuke ityatra pañcabhya ityasya prayojanamastīti vācyam rudādipañcadhātuparigrahārtha tatra vṛtkaraṇa karttavya tata eva vyavasthā bhaviṣyati  atha vā kṛgṛsvīkāra iti bahubrīhiraya kṛgroḥ svīkāro yasminniti kṛgṛsvīkāraḥ kiraśca pañcabhya iti yogastasminkṛgṛsvīkāre kiraśca pañcabhya  iti sūtra evāntarbhūtayorddaṅdhṛñorgrahaṇa vicchedaheturityarthaḥ  atha vā smipūṅrañjvaśā sani ityatra ṛgrahaṇa hrasvāntārtha tāvanna bhavati dṛṅdhṛṅgrahaṇāt dīrghantādapi yadi iṭ sani vā iti vikalpaḥ syād dīrghārthamapi na syānnityavikalpayorvirodhāt  eva ca ṛgrahaṇamanarthaka tasmādiṭ sani vā ityatra ṛgrahaṇa nānuvarttate vṛṅvṛñāvevānuvarttate vṛṅvṛñoreveḍvikalpaḥ ṛtā tu smipūṅrañjvaśā  sani ityanenaiva nityamiṭ siddha iti kṛgṛgrahaṇameva vicchedaheturiti  jñāpaka cātra hanaḥ sic iti sijgrahaṇam  yadyekasūtranirddiṣṭayorapi padayorekamanuvarttate nāparamiti tadā liṅsicāvātmanepadeṣu ityato liṅgrahaṇa nānuvarttiṣyate sijgrahaṇamevānuvarttiṣyata  iti sijgrahaṇamanarthaka syāt  aya ca svaritatvalabdhorthaḥ paribhāṣārūpeṇa paṭhyate ata evopadeśejanunāsika it ityato laśakvataddhita ityatra idgrahaṇānuvṛttāvapi anunāsikagrahaṇa nānuvarttate upadeśagrahaṇānuvarttana prati rakṣitānunyāsayorvivāda eva tathāhi gāṅkuṭādi sūtrenunyāsakāreṇoktamādeśapakṣe idgrahaṇamanarthakamāderhi bhavato laśakvataddhita ityanenaivetsajñāyāḥ siddhatvādityādi  rakṣitena tūktamādibhūto ṅakāro laśakvataddhita ityatropadeśagrahaṇānuvṛtterasatīdityetasminnetsajñaka iti na jñāpakamidityetadādeśābhāvasyeti tatrāya rakṣitābhiprāyaḥ laśakvataddhita ityatrāsatyupadeśādhikāre niśśabdātsaptamībahuvacane nicśvityatra śakārasyetsajñ syāt na cetsajñāyā karttavyāyāmasiddhatvamasti sasajuṣoruḥ ityatra rorukārasyānunāsikyapratijñānasamarthyātriṅśayagliṅkṣu iti nirddeśācca sāmānyenetsañjñāyā karttavyāyāmasiddhatvāpravarttanasya jñāpitatvāt tathā bhiyaḥ kruklukanau iti bholuka ityatra klukanaḥ kakāre lupte lakārasyetsañjñā syāt naitadasti prayojanābhāvādevetsañjñāyā apravṛttiḥ svarastu na prayojana nittvādeva tasya siddhatvāt eva tarhi yaṅluki bebhīluka ityatra svaraḥ prayojanam tathāhi nittvādekāra udātto bhavati littvādīkāraḥ syāditi anunyāsakārasyāyamabhiprāyaḥ nicśvityatretsañjñā na bhavivyatyasiddhatvāt yattūkta rorukārasyānunāsikyapratijñānasāmarthyālliṅkṣviti nirddeśāccāsiddhatva na bhavatīti tadupadeśejanunāsika ithalantyam ityetsūtradvayakarttavyatāyāmevāsiddhatva na bhavati tatraiva pramāṇasambhavāt anyatra tvasiddhatvameva bebhīluka ityatra yaṅlukaśchāndasatvāditsañjñā na bhaviṣyatīti yadi vā lakārasyetsañjñāyā yaṇādeśe kṛte bebhyuka ityeka evājiti kva litsvaraḥ syāt nicśviti jastvena śakārasya jakāraḥ ścutvena sakārasya śakāraḥ svari ca iti cartva jakārasya cakāraḥ nanu stoścunā ścuḥ ityatra rakṣitenokta jhalā jaś jhaśi iti nirddeśāt śakārasya jaśtva nāsti  ata eva masjinaśorjhali ityatra majjatisiddhaye jaśtvena sakārasya dakārastasya bhṛjjati iti nirdeśādasiddhatvābhāvāt ścutvena jakāro nyāse  uktaḥ  anyathā ścutvena sakārasya śakāre kṛte jastvena jakāre siddhe bhṛjjati iti nirddeśādasiddhatvābhāvapravarttanamayuktam eva ca kathamatra jaśtvena śakārasya jakāraḥ ucyate  jhalā jaś jhaśi ityatra cavargaparasya śakārasya jaśtvābhāvādanyatrāpi cavargaparasyaiva jaśtvābhāvastulyajātīyatvāditi yathā katha cit jñāpakasiddha  na sarvatreti vā    uṇādayovyutpannāni prātipadikāni   aya cārthorthavat sūtrapraṇayanādastītyāhuḥ anyathā sarveṣāmuṇādīnā dhātujatvena kṛdantatvāt prātipadikasajñāsiddhau tanna kuryāt anye tvataḥ kṛkami ityatra kamigrahaṇa kṛttvā kasagrahaṇādetāmāhuḥ  tena kṛgṛkuṭividibhidibhyaśca iḥ kiditīkārapratyayāntayoḥ kirigiriśabdayorosi yaṇādeśe kṛte dhātutvābhāvāddhali ca iti dīrghatvanna bhavati  kiryoḥ giryoriti  etacca na samyak acaḥ parasmin iti sthānivatvāddīrghatvāprasaṅgāt na cāsti dīrghavidhi prati na sthānivaditi svaradīrghayalopeṣu lopājādeśo na sthāvaditi vacanāt yathā pratidīvneti  eva tarhi jīryaterdhātorjīyateḥ krin raśca va iti krin pratyaye ittve raparatve ca rephasya vakāre kṛte jivririti dhātutvābhāvāddīrgho na sarvo dvandvo vibhāṣayaikavadbhavati   tena bābhravāśca śālaṅkāyanāśca bābhravaśālaṅkāyana bābhravaśālaṅkāyanā ityekavacana bahuvacana copapanna bhavati yadyeva samāhāhāradvandvepi vāktvaca śrīsrajam ityatrāpi dvivacana prāpnoti paśce tathetaretarayogadvandvepi pakṣe ekavacana syāt ucyate sarvo dvandva ityanena samāhāradvandvastathetaretarayogadvandvaśca nāpūrvatayā vibhāṣaikavat kriyate ki tarhi nyāyasiddhonūdyate tathāhi  cārthe dvandva ityanena cārthe dvandvaḥ kriyate cārthaścetaretarayogaḥ sa eva yadodriktāvayavabhedo bhavati tadāvayavabhedānugamād dvivacanabahuvacane  siddhe eva yadā tu tirohitāvayavavivakṣā sahatiḥ pradhānamiti yāvat tadā samāhāra iti tatra sahatipradhānatvādekavacanamiti  tadeva cārthe eva sarvo dvandvo vibhāṣayaikavadbhavatīti paribhāṣārūpeṇa paṭhyate nanu cārthaḥ samuccayo netaretarayogaḥ caśabdaprayoge samuccayasyaiva pratīteḥ satyametat ki tu tatprabheda evetaretarayogo na tu samuccayādayaḥ tathāhi samuccaya eva yadā yugapadarthābhidhāyinā parasparāpekṣāṇā padānā bhavati tadā dvandvaḥ kriyate etāvataivetaretarayogaścārtha evetyucyate  nanu yadi cārtha evāya sarvo dvandva ityādi kimartha tarhi tiṣyapunarvasvoḥ ityatrāsya bahuvacanagrahaṇa jñāpanārtha nyāsakṛtābhidhīyate tiṣya ekaḥ punarvasū ca dvau iti bahutvādbahuvacana siddhameva ekavacanasya prasaṅga eva nāsti bahuvacanaprsaṅge eva dvivacana bhaviṣyati ki bahuvacanasyetyanena tatkṛta jñāpayati astīya paribhāṣā sarvo dvandva ityādi ucyate jñāpayati bodhayati jñāpaka bodhakam kasya bodhakam abhimatasya niyamasyeti kvābhimataniyamaḥ dvandvaśca prāṇitūryasenāṅgānām ityatra samāhāre eva prāṇyaṅgādīnāmiti prāṇyaṅgādīnāmeva samāhāre nānyeṣāmiti viparītaniyame hi tiṣyapunarvasūnā sarvadā itaretarayoga eva dvandvaḥ syānnasamāhāre eva ca bahuvacanaprasaṅga eva dvivacanamiti gahuvacanagrahaṇamanarthaka syāt  etacca dvandvaśca prāṇitūrya ityatra prāṇyaṅgādīnāmeva samāhāra ityeva viparītaniyamo nāśrīyate tiṣyapunarvasvornakṣatradvandve bahuvacanasya  iti bahuvacanagrahaṇādityādina granthena rakṣitena vyākhyātam  nanveva dvandvaśca prāṇitūrya iti sūtramanarthaka syāditi tena hi samāhāre evaikavadbhāvo vidhīyate tatra samāhāradvandvaikatvādekatvādekavacana siddhameva ucyate prāṇyaṅgādīnā samāhāra eva dvandvo yathā syāditaretarayogo mābhūditi sūtraprayojanam nanu kimartha samāhāra ekavattva kriyate netaretarayoga evaikavadbhāvaḥ kriyatām eva ca samāhāradvandvagrahaṇa prayatnapratipādya na bhavati karya ca vidhimukhenaiva pravarttate ucyate itaretarayoga evaikavadbhāve satyasthitvacamityatra samāhāralakṣaṇo dvandvāccudaṣahāntātsamāhāra iti ṭac syāt nanvevamapi pūrvoktaprakāreṇa samāhāra evaikavadvacana bhavati samāhāraścaika eva eva caikavaditi vatirnopapadyate na hyeka evaikavadbhabhavati ucyate buddhyānekatvamāropya vatirbhaviṣyati ukta ca buddhirhi bhagavatyabhedepi bheda janayati yathā rāhoḥ śira iti atha vā nāya vatiḥ ki tarhi vadervijantoyamekavaditi nanu ca tathāpyaśeṣadvandva ekatvāvidhānāt sarvaśabdārthoghaṭamānaḥ syāt ucyate sarvo dvandva iti korthaḥ itaretarayogasamāhārātmaka ityarthaḥ nanvevamapi vibhāṣā vṛkṣamṛgādi sūtramanarthakam anayaiva paribhāṣayā bābhravaśālaṅkāyana bābhravaśālaṅkāyanā itivat plakṣanyagrodha plakṣanyagrodhā ityevamādīnā siddhatvāt ucyate siddhe paribhāṣayaikatve vṛkṣādīnā sajātīyaireva dvandva ekavadyathā syātna vijātīyairiti vyatikaranirāsārtha vibhāṣayaikavadvidhānamiti tena paśvādīnā vijātīyairdvandva ekavanna bhavatītītaretarayogosau dvandvao bhavati tathā ca bhaṭṭiḥ naravānararakṣāsāmiti   iti mahāmahopādhyāyasīradevakṛtāyā paribhāṣāvṛttau gāṅkuṭādipādaḥ   ūditsavarṇa gṛhṇāti na savarṇamātram   udidvarṇoṇuditsavarṇasya iti sthānaprayatnābhyā viśiṣṭameva savarṇa gṛhṇāti na savarṇamātram tena coḥ kuḥ iti kugrahaṇe hakārasya grahaṇa na bhavati jñāpaka cātra na vibhaktau tusmā ityatra tugrahaṇa kṛtvā sakāragrahaṇamiti aya ca nyāyasiddha evārthaḥ sukhapratipattyartha jñāpakenokaḥ tathāhi sthānaprayatnābhyā sadṛśasya savarṇasajñā vidhīyamānā takārasakārayoḥ sparśovāṇoḥ prayatnabhedādeva sāvarṇya nāstīti tat kuto jñāpakam yata eva sthānaprayatnābhyā sādṛśyāt sāvarṇyamata evāi uṇiti sūtre vṛttikṛtoktam hrasvamavarṇa prayoge savṛtam dīrghaplutayostu vivṛtatvam teṣā sāvarṇyaprasiddyarthamakāra iha śāstre vivṛtaḥ pratijñāyata iti tatraika nyāsakāreṇoktam vivṛtataraḥ pratijñāyata iti draṣṭavyam anunyāsakāreṇa tu vivṛtatamaḥ pratijñāyata iti draṣṭavyamityuktam anyathā ākārasya vivṛtatamatvādakārasya vivṛtataratvapratijñāne satyapi sāvarṇya na syāt nyūnādhikaprayatnatvāt nyūnādhikaprayatnānā ca sāvarṇya nāstyeva tathā ca jājjhalau iti sūtre śakārasya sāvarṇyenāctvābhāvārtha bhāṣyakāreṇoktam spṛṣṭa karaṇa sparśānāmīṣatspṛṣṭamantasthānāmvivṛta karaṇamuṣmaṇāmīṣadityanuvartatesvarāṇā cavivṛtamityanuvarttate īṣaditi nivṛttamiti etenekāraśakārayorvivṛteṣadvivṛtayoḥ sāvarṇyābhāva ukto bhavati eva ca nājhalau ityasyāpi prayojana na dṛśyate dadhi śītamityādau nyūnādhikaguṇatvādeva sāvarṇyābhāvāt nyūnādhikaguṇānā ca sāvarṇyābhāvovaśyamevāṅgīkarttavyaḥ anyathā eṅaḥ padāntādati ityādau ekāraukārābhyā sāvarṇyādaikāraukārayorapi grahaṇa syāt rakṣitena tu eṅa ityatra eoṅṅakāreṇa praṭyāhāragrahaṇasāmarthyāt sāvarṇyābhāva uktaḥ anyathā aikāraukārayorapi grahaṇe eca iti cakāreṇa pratyāhāragrahaṇa kuryāt ki tveva yatra svarūpeṇaikāra upādīyate tatra sāvarṇya syāt īdūdeddivacanam iti atra ekāreṇa aikārasya grahaṇe sāvarṇyabhāvātkaravāvahāyitītyatrāpi pragṛhyasajñā syāt na cātra taparakaraṇātsāvarṇyābhāvo vācyaḥ taparakaraṇasya prayojanāntarābhāvena vṛttinyāsayornirdeśārthatvena vyākhyātatvāt  yadyevamiṇkoḥ ityatra katha nyāsakāreṇa dāsyatītyatra ākārahakārayornyūnādhikaguṇayoḥ sāvarṇyāt ṣatvaprāptimuktā vayasyāsu iti nirddeśād vyavasthoktā tathāhi hakārasya vivṛtvam ākārasya vivṛtatamatvam yadāha śikṣākāraḥ vivṛta karaṇamūṣmaṇā svarāṇā catebhya eṅau vivṛtatarautābhyāmapyeautābhyāmapyākāra iti atrāhuḥ  vivṛta karanamūṣmasvarāṇāmityekapade karttavye yadvivṛta karaṇamūṣmaṇā svarāṇā ceti pṛthak pada kṛta tataḥ svarāṇāmityasyaivottaratra  sūtre sambandha iti   tena svarāpekṣamevākārasya vivṛtatamatva noṣmāpekṣamata ākārahakārayoṣtulyaprayatnatvād dāsyatītyatra nirddeśāt ṣatvābhāvo yukta evābhihitaḥ rakṣitena tu iṇkoḥ ityatra nyūnādhikaguṇasyāpi sāvarṇyamuktam nanu dāsyatītyādāvākārahakārayorajjhaltvānnājjhalau iti sāvarṇyapratiṣedhādeva mūrddhanyo nāsti tatkimiti nirddeśena vyavasthocyate ucyate nājjhalau ityagṛhītasavarṇānā pratiṣedho vaktavya iti vacanāt ākārastu gṛtasavarṇaḥ tatkatotra pratiṣedhaḥ  nanu kimarthamagṛhītasavarṇanā pratiṣedha ucyate na sāmānyenaiva pratiṣedhostu tena dāsyatītyādau sāvarṇyābhāvo nājjhalau iti niṣedhādeva  sidhyati  tathā khaṭvā hastaḥ kumārī śete ityādāvakaḥ savarṇe dīrghatvābhāvārthamacītyanuvarttanīya na bhavati ucyate yadi gṛhītasavarṇānāmapi nājjhalau iti pratiṣedhaḥ syāt tat nissa ityatra jharo jhari savarṇa iti pakṣe sakāralopo nasyāt nṛkāreṇācā savarṇasya sakārasya grahaṇāt tasyācthalyupadeśāddhaltvamajjhalornājjhalau iti pratiṣedhāt na ca lṛkārasakārayornājjhalau iti savarṇasajñāniṣedhaḥ śakyate karttum ātmani kriyāvirodhāt tathāhi lṛkārasakārayornājjhalau iti pratiṣedhena sakārasyāctvābhāvāt lṛkārasakārayornājjhalau iti niṣedhī nopapadyate eva cātmana eva ātmanā pratiṣedhaḥ kṛtaḥ syāditi  agṛhītasavarṇānā pratiṣedhaśca nājjhalau ityatra savarṇasajñāpratiṣedhavākye savarṇasajñāyā anabhinirvṛttatvena grahaṇakaśāstrasyānabhinirvṛttatvāt eva hyukta pūrva hyapavādāḥ pravarttante paścādutsargā iti   prakṛtivadanukaraṇa bhavati   tena kaścidāha dviḥ paṭatīti tamanyonukaroti dviḥ paṭatītyāheti tatra prakṛtivadbhāvātpadatve tiṅṅatiṅa iti nighātaḥ siddho bhavati padatvābhāve sa na syāt tathā vṛṣaṇvasvaśvayorityatra nalopābhāvaṇatve bhavataḥ  jñāpaka cātra parivyavebhyaḥ kriya ityādau nirddeśe kriāderanukaraṇaśabdasya vibhaktyutpattyartha prātipadikasajñābhyupagamepi dhātutvāśrayasyeyaṅādeśasya  karaṇam  yadyeva katha viparābhya jeḥ ityādinirddeśaḥ na cātra vidyamānopīyaṅādeśaḥ paratvād gherṅiti iti guṇena bādhyate iti śakyate vaktum kṣiya iti nirddeśātparamapi guṇa bādhitvā iyaṅeva bhavati pūrvavipratiṣedheneti rakṣitena vyākhyātatvāt eva ca kṣiyo ḍhīrghāt ityatra dīghagrahaṇamupapadyate anyathā hi kṣiya itīyaṅā nirddeśādeva dīrghaparigrahe siddhe dīrghagrahaṇamanarthaka syāt ucyate dvividhamanukaranam sārthakasya nirarthakasya ca śabdamātrasya tadeva kriya ityādau sārthakasyaiva labdhadhātuvyapadeśasya krītyasyānukaraṇam tatra dhātukāryasyeyaṅo vidyamānatvādanukaraṇepi tadbhavati viparābhyā jeḥ ityādau nirarthakasya varṇasamudāyamātrasyānukaraṇa tatra ca kriyārūpasyārthasyābhāvāddhātusajñaiva nāsti eva cānukārye eva dhātusajñāyā abhāvādiyaṅādeśo nāsti tadanukaraṇe kā punaḥ kathā tadeva dvividhamanukaraṇamiyaṅaḥ karaṇākaraṇābhyāmavadhāryate ata eva paṭhanti sārthakānukaraṇe prakṛtivadanukaraṇa bhavatīti nanu yadi jeriti nirarthakasyānukaraṇa katha tarhi jayaterdhātorātmane pada bodhyate ucyate sāmānyasya viśeṣagrahitayā dhātorapi pratipādanāt nanu yadi prakṛtivadbhāvād dhātukāryamiyaṅ tadādhāturiti prātipadikasajñāpratiṣedhaḥ prāpnoti ucyate adhāturiti nāya prasajyapratiṣedho dhātorna bhavatīti ki tarhi paryudāsaḥ dhātoranyatra bhavatīti krīprabhṛtayaśca śabdā anukaraṇatvenādhātavaḥ prakṛtivattayā ca dhātava iti dhātvadhātutvāddhātoranya eva bhavanti tathā ca kṣiyo dīrghāt ityatra kṣiyaḥ svāśrayā prātipadikasajñā bhaviṣyatīti nyā vyākhyātam atha vā paryudāsedhāturiti neda śāstrīya kāryam tastatkarttavyatāyā na prakṛtivadityatideśaḥ paryudāse nañityeta ccārthavadadhāturapratyayaḥ prātipadikam ityatra kṣiye dīrghāt ityatra ca rakṣitenoktam nanvevamapyanarthaka tvādanukaraṇaśabdasya prātipadikasajñā na prāpnoti na cānukā evārthaḥ bhedābhāvāt bhede hi sati vācyavācakasabandhaḥ cānukaraṇaśabdasyānukāryaśabdātkopi bhedovadhāryate tathāpi bauddho bhedaḥ syāt evamapi anukāryasya vācyasya śabdātmakatvādanukaraṇasya vācakasya na tadabhidheyatvamupapadyate na hi śabdasya śabdāntara vācya ki tarhyartha eva naidasti śabdopi śabdasya vācyo dṛśyo yathā bhūvādiśabdo dhātuśabdasyeti nanu yukta tat ācāryeṇa sajñāvidhānāt eva tarhi anukaraṇamapyanukāryasya vācaka yuktam ācāryasya tathā vyavahārāt vācyavācakabhāve vyavahāra eva hi nibandhanam nanvevamapi satyapyarthavattvenukaraṇādvibhaktirna prāpnoti sakhyāyā sāvidhīyate na cānukāryeṣu śabdeṣu dravyasamavāyinī sakhyā sabhavati teṣā śabdātmakatvenāvaraguṇatve satyadravyatvāt sakhyāpi guṇa eveti na tatrāsāvasti nirguṇā guṇā iti vacanāt ucyate śabdasyeda taditi sarvanāmaparāmarśayogyatvād dravyatvamiṣyate tasmātsiddhānukaraṇaśabdādvibhaktiḥ   vikaraṇebhyo niyamo balīyān   śabādivikaraṇāt prāganudāttaṅita ātmane padam ityādīni niyamaśāstrāṇi tāvadbhavanti tato vikaraṇāḥ tena nerviśa ityādau vṛttau yaduktamaḍāgamastadbhaktastadgrahaṇena gṛhyata iti tadupapanna bhavati tathāhi vikaraṇānnityāt parasmādapi niyamaḥ karttavyaḥ niyamakāle ca tadaivāḍāgamaḥ prāpnoti nāsāvaḍāgamo niyamenāpasāryate vikaraṇādeva niyamasya balīyastvāt nāpi vikaraṇenāpasārayitu śakyate niyamapravṛttikāle tasyāvidyamānatvāt tadeva niyamāḍāgamayoryugapatprāptau paratvādaḍāgamastato yuktamuktamaḍāgamastadbhaktastadgrahaṇena gṛhyata iti nanu ca niyamena pravarttamānena vikaraṇo bādhyeta tadbādhakakāḍāgamapravṛttikāle vikaraṇo nityoḍāgamāt prāk kasmānna bhavati ucyate yadi vikaraṇīḍāgama bādheta tato niṣpratidvandvī kimiti niyamo vikaraṇa na bādheteti tathā edhiṣyate aidhiṣṭetyatrānudāttaṅita ātmanepadameva bhavati na parasmaipadamiti anyathā paratvānnityatvācca vikaraṇeṣu kṛteṣu syādiṣu tairvyavadhānādanudāttaṅidbhya evātmanepada śeṣādeva parasmaipadamiti niyamo na syāteva ca sāmānyena tibādayaḥ syuḥ niyamastvāste śete ityādiṣu kṛtārthaḥ yadyeva syādīnā lāvasthāyāmutpattirna prāpnoti lādeśe tu kṛte edhiṣyate ityatra dvaya prāpnoti yak pratyayaḥ syapratyayaśca tatra paratvādyakaiva bhāvyam ucyate kartṛvācini sārvadhātuke śapi prāpte bhāvakarmaṇostu yaki syādayo vidhīyamānāḥ sāmānyena sarveṣāmapavādatvādbādhakā bhavanti  aya cārtho vṛdbhyaḥ syasanoḥ ityatra parasmaipadabidhā nena jñāpitaḥ anyathā vṛtu varttana ityevamādīnā syena vyadhāna cādanudāttaṅita ātmanepadam  iti niyamo nāstīti sāmānyavihiteṣu tibādiṣu siddhamubhaya vartsyati varttiṣyatai iti kimanena vidhānena  tatkṛtamasyārthasya jñāpakam anye tvasmāj jñāpakāt kṛtepi vikaraṇe niyamaḥ pravarttate iti paribhāṣāmāhuḥ asmin darśane edhiṣyata ityatra lāvasthāyāmevāntaraṅgatvātsyapratyayena bhavitavyam tathāsminneva darśane aupyata auhyata ityatrājāditvādāḍajādīnām ityāḍ bhavati anyathā hi vikaraṇānniyamasya balīyastve niyamāḍāgamayoḥ sapradhāraṇāyā paratvādaḍāgamena bhavitavyam na cāḍāgamapravṛttikāle nityo vikaraṇaḥ śakyate pravarttayitum pūrvameva niyamenāpasāritatvāt āḍāgamastu niyamena nāpasāryat iti paratvādasau bādhakaḥ prāpnotyeva tadeva halāditvādaḍāgame kṛte āṭaśca iti vṛddyabhāvādauhyata ityavamādi na sidhyati tathāsminneva darśane ṛccheranādeśasya grahaṇam atyārdeśasya carttītyeva siddheriti samo gamyādi sūtre vṛttgrantha upapadyate na hi vikaraṇānniyamabalīyastve śeti vikaraṇe vidhīyamāna ṛcchādeśa ātmanepadātprāgeva bhavate tathāsminneva darśane nergadādi sūtre vikaraṇāttasyāḍāgama uktaḥ anyathā vikaraṇānniyamabalīyastve tatopi paratvādaḍāgame kṛte katha vikaraṇāntasyāḍāgama upapadyate  atha vikaraṇebhya ityatra nirddeśe bhyasaḥ sakārasya rutve kṛte rukārasyopadeśejanunāsika it itītsajñā na prāpnoti pūrvatrāsiddham ityasiddhatvāt ucyate rorukārasyānunāsikapratijñānasāmarthyādasiddhatva na bhavati tathā copadeśejanunāsika ityatra rakṣitaḥ itsajñāyāmasiddhatva nāsti sasajuṣo ruḥ ityatrokārasyetsajñārthamanunāsikatvapratijñānasāmarthyāditi atrocyate haśi ca ityatrānunāsikaviśiṣṭasya rorgrahaṇa yathā syādityevamartha rorukārasyānunāsikatvapratijñāna syāt tena taruvanamityatra haśi ca ityutva na bhavati tatkutastatsāmarthyāditsajñābhidhīyate na ca vācya kṛtrimākṛtrimanyāyena sasajuṣo ruḥ ityasyaivottvena bhavitavyam na taruvanādau kṛtrimākṛtamayorubhayorhi sabhave kṛtrimaparibhāṣāpravṛtteḥ tathāhi utvaśāstre sasajuṣo ruḥ ityasyāsiddhatvāttaruvanasyaiva sambhavo netarasya eva tarhi rephasyaivānunāsikatva pratijñāyatā svaritatvapratijñānavat tathā cottvavidhāvanunāsikaviśiṣṭasya rephasyottve vidhīyamāne punarbhavādau kathamuttvaprāptiḥ tadeva rephasyānunāsikatve pratijñātavye yadukārasya pratijñāna tatsāmarthyāditsajñā bhaviṣyati etadapi na eva sthita eva śāstre rorukāramakṛtvaiva punaranantaroktaprakāreṇeṣṭasiddherukāronubandho vyarthaḥ syāt eva tarhi vyaktipadārthāśrayaṇena sāmarthyam etacca sasajuṣo ruḥ ityatrokārasyetsajñārthamanunāsikatva pratijñātamiti vadatā maitreyeṇa pratipāditam anyaḥ punarāha anunāsikaviśiṣṭasya yadroruttva tadapyasiddhabādhanamantareṇa na sambhavati tathetsajñāpi tatra yathāsiddhatva bādhitvānunāsikapratijñānamuttva pravarttayati tathetsajñāmapi pravarttayati na cottvamāśrayātsiddhamiti vacanātpravarttate vipakṣe pramāṇābhāvāt   iti paribhāṣāvṛttau bhūpādaḥ   sakṛḍgatau vipratiṣedhe yadbādhita tadbādhitameva   punaḥ prasaṅgavijñānātsiddham   vacanadvayamida vipratiṣedha sūtre vyaktijātipakṣayo phalabhūta paribhāṣārūpeṇa paṭhyate tathāhi vyaktau padārthe pratilakṣya lakṣaṇasya vyāpārabhedātparyāyeṇa dvāvapi vidhī prāptau yathā devadattayajñadattābhyāmekatra bhājane krameṇa bhujyate tatra vipratiṣedhe param ityanena vipratiṣedhaviṣayo niyamyate vipratiṣedhe parameva na pūrvamiti na caitena pūrvavākyānarthakyam vipratiṣedhasūtreṇa tasyāsattvākhyāpanāt tadidamucyate sakṛdgatau vipratiṣedhe yadbādhita tadbādhitameveti tasyāyamarthaḥ sakṛdekavāra yadbādhita tadbādhitameveti gatau vipratiṣedhe tenājjaserasuk ityanena paratvādasuki kṛte punaḥ śībhāvo na bhavati ye pūrvāsa iti tathā stāt tvamityatra tātaṅaḥ sthānivattvāḍvibhāvo na bhavati ghvasoreddhāvabhyāsalopaśca iti sasyaittva ca etacca sthānivat sūtre bhāṣye vyākhyātam jātau tu padārthe sakṛdekavāra lakṣaṇa pravarttate viṣayāntare cobhaya caritārthamiti vipratiṣedhaviṣayepravṛtirevobhayoḥ prāpnoti yathobhayostulyabalayorekaḥ preṣyo virodhādekasyāpi kāryena pravarttate tatra vipratiṣedhe para kāryam ityasya paravidhau vyāpārātpūrvanivṛttāvavyāpāra iti nanu pūrvavākyasya prāgevoktā nivṛttistatkathamidānī tadvidhānam ucyate yugapadvirodhādapravṛttirityuktam paratvātparavidhau kṛte virodhābhāvādyukta eva pūrvidhiḥ tadidamucyate punaḥprasaṅgavijñānātsiddhamiti tena bhinddhakītyatra paratvāddhibhāve kṛte punarakac kriyate ījaturityatra paratvātsaprasāraṇe kṛte punardvirvacanam yatra pūrveṇa pravarttamānena parasya bādhā tatra sakṛdgatiparibhāṣā yatra tu pūrva pravarttamāna para na bādhate tatra punaḥ prasaṅgavijñānātsiddhamiti keṣā cinmatam tadayuktam eva hyakṣī ityatra paratvādī ca dvivacane itīkāre kṛte punarnum syādeva tasmāllakṣyasthityaiva hyetayorvyavastheti atha punaḥprasaṅgavijñānādityatra nirddeśe punaḥśabde padatvāśrayaḥ katha visarjanīyaḥ yāvataikavākyatāyā karmādīnāmekatvādau svādibhirbhavitavyam punaḥ śabdaścāvyayam avyayāni ca liṅgasakhyārahitāni ucyate pañcakapakṣe sāmānyena svādividhānam tato bahuṣu bahuvacanam ityanena bahuṣvartheṣu bahuvacanamevetyarthaniyamena pratyayasyāniyatatvādavyayebhyaḥ svādayo vidyanta eva athāpi bahuṣvartheṣveva bahuvacanamiti pratyayaniyamaḥ tathāpi tulyajātīyāpekṣayā niyamasya yatra sakhyāsti sakhyāntara ca vyāvarttya tatraiva niyamena bhavitavyam  eva ca sakhyāśabdebhyo devadattayajñadattaviti dvandvasamāsācca tathā vanasyāgregrevaṇa prācīna grāmādāmrā ityatrānabhidhānāt sarvasubādyabhāvo  vācyaḥ  ata eva hi trikapakṣepyanekavākyatā svādi sūtre vakṣyati nyāsakāraḥ bahuṣu bahuvacanam ityanenānekavākyatāpīhākhyāyata iti atha yadā trika ekavākyatāpakṣastaḍhā katha svādayaḥ katha ca na syuḥ ekatvādyabhāvāt  yadyeva vṛkṣādibhyopi na prāpnuvanti tatra yathā vṛkṣādibhyo bahuṣu bahuvacanam ityādinā svādibhiravidyamānā eva sakhyādayobhidhīyante tathāvyayebhyopyabhidhāsyante naitat pratyāsattyā prātipadikārtha eva yatra sakhyādayaḥ prātipadikenānuktāstatra svādibhiḥ sakhyādayobhidhīyante nānyatra yathā ajādyataṣṭāp iti striyāmabhidheyāyā vidhīyamānaṣṭāb vṛkṣādibhyo na bhavati eva tarhyavyayādāpsupaḥ iti jñāpakātsakhyākarmādirahitebhyovyayebhyopi svādayo bhavanti tathā ca bahuvacanamityatra nyāsakṛtoktam avyayādāpsupaḥ iti jñāpakādavyayebhyastu nitsakhyebhyaḥ sāmānyavihitāḥ svādayo vidyanta eveti tatra rakṣitenoktam avyayādāpsupaḥ iti jñāpaka vyaktau astyeva hi tasya viṣayaḥ pralambate svarityādiravakāśaḥ  pralambate svarityatra hi pralambanakriyāpekṣayā svaḥśabdādavaśyamevāpādāne pañcamyā bhavitavyamatastasyā lugartha saj jñāpaka katha syāt tarhi vyaktāvaliṅgasakhya yadavyaya nīcairityādi tadartha yatkṛta taj jñāpakam nanvatrāpi prātipadikārtha ityādinā prātipadikārthamātre vihitāyāḥ prathāmāyā lugartha syāt tatkatha jñāpakam ucyate dvitīyādyartha yat kṛta taj jñāpakam etaccāsamyak avyayād dvitīyādividhānasya na ki citprayojanam sapūrvāyāḥ prathamāyā vibhāṣā iti vikalpitatemayādividdyabhāvaḥ prayojanamiti cet  na prathamāvidhānapakṣe teṣāmavaśyabhāvāt eva tarhi dvitīyādyantānā dvitīyādisamāsaḥ prayojanamiti cet etadapi na yataḥ pratyāsattyā tatra śritādinimittā dvitīyā samasyate eva ṣaṣṭhītyādāvapi supsupetyadhikārāttannimittā vibhaktirgrahītavyā ucyate prātipadikārtha sūtre arthagrahaṇamanabhisadhāya jñāpakamidam tadabhisadhāne jñāpakasya prayojana nāsti arthagrahaṇādevāvyayebhyaḥ prathamāyāḥ siddhatvāt ata eva prātipadikārtha sūtre rakṣitaḥ arthagrahaṇamaliṅgārtham taccāvyayam ata eva sakhyārahitebhyopi prathamā siddhetyavyayādāpsupaḥ iti sūtra jñāpaka prapañcatayoktam   antaraṅgabahiraṅgayorantaraṅga balavat   iya paribhāṣā vipratiṣedha sūtre bhāṣye nyāse ca paṭhitā tena dyaukāmiḥ sautthitirityādau vibhajyānvākhyānapakṣe bahiraṅgāyā vṛddherdaurbalyādantaraṅgau yaṇekādeśau bhavataḥ tadetadudāharaṇa diṅmātram samarthānā prathamādvā ityatra samarthagrahaṇātsamarthitasarvakāryāttadvitena bhavitavyamityeva yaṇekādeśayoḥ siddhatvāt ida tūdāharaṇa vṛkṣāi ihetyādau bahiraṅgādakaḥ savarṇadīrghādantaraṅgo guṇaḥ na caitadasiddha bahiraṅgaḥ mantaraṅgaḥ ityanayā paribhāṣayā sidhyati acorānantarye nājānantarye bahiṣṭvapraklṛptiriti tasyāḥ pratiṣiddhatvāt nanveva kṛtepyatra savarṇadīrghatvecaḥ parasminpūvavidhau iti sthānijadbhāvādāṅguṇena siddha vṛkṣa iheti naitadasti ekādeśasya pūrvagrahaṇena grahaṇāt padāntavidhitvena sthānivattvapratiṣedhāt parādigrahaṇa tu na vācyam parāditvena na padāntādi sūtrāvyāpārasyāyuktatvāt nanvantaraṅgaparibhāṣāpi na prāpnoti nājānantarye iti niṣedhādeva tathāhi yathā asiddhaparibhāṣayā ṣatvatukorasiddha ityasyānarthakatva tathāntaraṅgaparibhāṣayāpi ucyate naivāntaraṅgaparibhāṣayā ṣatvatukorasiddha ityasyānarthakyam yatastukontaraṅgatvātprāptiḥ dīrghasya nityatvāt tatra paratvāddīrgha eva prāpnoti yattūcyate nityādapyantaraṅga balīya iti tatparatvaphala na tvapūrvamiti atha vāstvantaraṅgatvāttuk dīrghatve kṛte nimittāpāyaparibhāṣayā tannivṛttiḥ syādeva tadeva bahiraṅgaparibhāṣayaivānarthakya ṣātvatukorasiddha ityasya atastasyā eva nājānantarya iti pratiṣedhaḥ ki ca yadyatrāntaraṅgaparibhāṣāyāḥ pratiṣedhaḥ syāttadāntaraṅgaparibhāṣā nirviṣayā syāt iya ca paribhāṣā bahiraṅgaparibhāṣayaiva sarvakāryasya siddhatvād bhāgavṛttikṛtā nābhyupagamyate tanmate vṛkṣa ihetyādāvacorānantarye yadyapi bahiraṅgaparibhāṣā nāsti tathāpi padasaskārapakṣe doṣapratikṣepo vyākhyeyaḥ yadāhuḥ suvicārya padasyārtha vākya gṛhṇanti sūraya iti yukta caitat anyathā vākyasaskāre vṛkṣai ihetyādau śabdaparavipratiṣedhenāntaraṅgamādguṇa bādhitvā sarvaṇadīrghatvameva syāt yathā diva ut ityatra divokamo devā ityatra ukārasya yṇādeśo rakṣitenotkaḥ na cāntaraṅgaparibhāṣāsāmarthyād vṛkṣai ihetyādāvābguṇenaiva bhavityam eva hi divokasa ityatrāpi ikārasya yaṇādeśaḥ syāt athāsyā udāharaṇāntara kaścāya ṛtviya iti atra ghas tasya iyādeśe kṛte siti ca iti padasajñāntaraṅgatvādajādau vidhīyamānā bahiraṅgā yaci bham iti bhasajñā bādhate samāveśastu nāsti ekasajñādhikārāt etaccāyuktam siti ca iti sūtrārambhādeva bhasajñābādhakatvasya siddhatvāt ata evaitadarthataikasajñādhikārasya na ghaṭate tathāhi  svādiṣviti padasajñayā yaci bham iti bhasajñāyāḥ samāveśe siddhe siti ca iti kṛta yadi punaḥ samāveśaḥ syāttadā siti ca ityanarthakameva  syāt  athaitatsyāt yaci bham ityatraikasajñādhikārābhyupagamād bhapadasajñayoḥ samāveśo nāsti eva ca siti ca ityatrāsatyekasajñādhikāre ṛtviya ityatra bhapadasajñayoḥ samāveśaḥ syādeva nanvemapi siti ca ityanarthakamtasya hyetatprayojanam ṛtviya ityatra sittvātpadatvenaurguṇo mābhūditi bhasajñāsamāveśe tu syādevaurguṇaḥ iti eva cākaḍārāt ityatra yadetadanunyāsakāreṇoktam anavakāśāyāstvidamucyate aya te yonirṛtviya ityatra padasajñā bhasajñā bādhata iti tadayuktam nāyuktam padatvasyāvagrahārthatvāt   ubhayanirddeśe pañcamīnirddeśo balīyān   yatra pañcamīnirddeśosti saptamīnirddeśaścopāttonuvṛtto vā tatra pañcamīnirddeśasya balīyastvāttasmādityuttarasya iti pravarttate  tenāmi sarvanāmnaḥ suṭ ityatrāt ityanuvṛttau avarṇāntātsarvanāmna ityanayā pañcamyā āmītyasyāḥ saptamyāḥ ṣaṣṭhyā parikalpitāmāma eva suḍāgamo  bhavati  aya ca vipratiṣedhe para kāryam ityasyārthaḥ paribhāṣārūpeṇa paṭhyate tathāhi tasminniti nirddiṣṭe pūrvasya iti saptamīnirddeśa iko yaṇaci iti dadhyatra madhvantretyatra sāvakāśaḥ tasmādityuttarasya iti pañcamīnirddeśo raṣābhyā no ṇa ityatra kṛtārthaḥ āstīrṇamiti yatra tu saptamīnirddeśaḥ pañcamīnirddeśaścobhaya kṛtārtha tatrobhayaprāptau paratvāttasmādityuttarasya iti pravarttate tathāhi āmi sarvanāmnaḥ suṭ ityatrāt iti pañcamī ājjaserasuk ityatrāsugvidhau kṛtārthā amīti saptamī trestraya ityatra kṛtārthā ubhayostulyabalayorvirodhe paratvātpañcamī saptamyāḥ ṣaṣṭhītva kalpayati yatra tvanavakāśā saptamī tatra saptamīnirddeśa eva pañcamyāḥ ṣaṣṭītva kalpayati yathāne muk ityatrana iti saptamī niravakāśāto yeyaḥ ityatrāta iti kṛtārthāyāḥ pañcamyāḥ ṣaṣṭhītva kalpayati tataścāne paratokārāntasyaivāṅgasya mug bhavati yadyeva ḍaḥ si ghūṭ ityatra kathamanayā sakārādeḥ parasya dhuḍāgamaḥ na hi sītyasyāḥ saptamyāḥ kvāpi kṛtārthatvam ucyate yathā sītyasyāḥ saptamyā anavakāśatva tathā ḍa ityasyā api pañcamyāḥ eva cobhayoranavakāśayoryuktameva paratvam na ca yugapadanyonyaṣaṣṭhīkalpanā śaṅkyānāpi krameṇa ekaḥ pūrvaparayoḥ ityatra pūrvaparagrahaṇāt taduktam na ca yugapadabhaye prakalpike pūrvaparagrahaṇāditi na caiva saptamīnirddeśasyānarthakyam lāghavārthatvāt sa iti nirddeśe gaurava syāditi etacca ḍaḥ si dhuṭ ityatra nyāse uktam iha tu dīrghātpadāntādvā ityatra yadyapi cha iti saptamī kṛtārthātathāpi tasyāḥ svaritāsaṅgādihānuvṛttāyā niravakāśatvāddīrghādityasyāḥ pañcamyāḥ ṣaṣṭhītva prakalpayati pañcamī tu paurvāparya prakalpya sāvakāśā nivarttate tenāyamartho bhavati dīrghāduttaro yaśchākārastasminparataḥ pūrvasyaiva dīrghasya tugbhavati tatrāsyā na vyāpāra iti tasmādityuttarasya ityatra nyāsaḥ dīrghāt ityatra tu nyāsakṛtā tasmādityuttarasyetyatra tasmāditi yogavibhāgaḥ karttavyaḥ pūvasūtrātpūrvasyetyanuvarttate tena dīghāt ityādau satyapi pañcamīnirddeśe pūrvasyaiva kārya bhavatītyuktam   sarve vidhayaśchandasi vikalpyante   tana dhuri dakṣiṇāyāmityatrārthe saptamyā vikalpitatvāccheṣe ṣāṣṭhīvidhānāddhuri dakṣiṇāyā iti sidhyati tathā ye yūpāya takṣatītyatra takṣatīti bahutve ekavacanam aya cārthaḥ ṣaṣṭhīyuktaśchandasi vā ityatra yogavibhāgena sādhitaḥ iya ca paribhāṣā vyatyayo bahulamityasyaiva prapañcaḥ   pratyayagrahaṇe yasmātsa vihitastadādestadantasya grahaṇam   pratyaye gṛhyemāṇe yasmādasau vihitastadādereva bhāgasya tatpratyayāntasya ca grahaṇa bhavati prayojana dhātupratyayaprātipadikataddhitāḍhyaḥ sanādyantā dhātavaḥ iti yasmātman vihitastadādestadantasyaiva dhātusajñā cikīrṣatīti na saghātasya prācikīrṣaditi kṛttaddhitasamāsāśca iti kṛttaddhitāntasya prātipadikasajñā tadādestadantasyaiva kārako gārgya iti na saghātasya vipraḥ kārako vipro gārgya iti supa ātmanaḥ kyac putramiccati putrīyati saghātānna bhavati mahāntamputramicchatīti taddhitavidhau yañiñośca iti pratyayayorgrahaṇa yatastau vihitau tadādereva phak pratyayo bhavati gārgyāyaṇa iti saghātānna bhavati vipro gārgyāyaṇa iti supsupā iti samāso na saghātasya ṛddhasya rājñaḥ puruṣa iti sa cāyamartho yasmātpratyayavidhi sūtre yogavibhāgena sādhitaḥ tathāhi yasmātpratyayavidhistadādi pratyaye iti vigṛhyate gṛhyamāṇe iti cādhyāharttavyam pratyaye gṛhyamāṇe yasmāt vihitastadādireva ghiyate na tu pratyayāntaḥ saghāta iti ata evāṅgapāde yasmādādi sūtra kṛtvā aṅgasya iti sūtra na khaṇḍyate nanu tatrāpi yogavibhāgena paribhāṣā sidhyati satya sidhyati ki tu na strīpratyaye cānuparjane iti dvitīyā na sidhyati tathāhi atra kṛte neyaṅuvaṅsthānāvastrī ityatostrīgrahaṇamanuvarttate tatrānuvṛttisāmarthyātstrīpratyayasya grahaṇam pradhāne ca kāryasapratyayānna strīpratyaye cānupasarjane iti labhyate tarhi prakaraṇamevedamaṅgapāde kriyatām nacaivamatatakṣadityatra laghusajñāgurusajñayoḥ samāveśaḥ syāditi vācyam laghusajñāpraṇayanavaiyarthyaprasaṅgāt anyathā laghupradeśe hrasvagrahaṇameva kuryāt ucyate yasmādādisūtrāttadādigrahaṇa suptiṅanta padam ityatrānuvarttate tadarthamiha prakaranam tena dviḥ prayogo dvirvacanamiti pakṣe tadādigrahaṇāt pacasipacasi iti samudāyasya suptiṅanta padam iti padasajñā sidhyati tathāhi  artharūpayoḥ sāmyāt sa eva pacśabdaḥ sa eva tiṅ yaḥ pūrvasmādvihitaḥ sa eva parasmādapi vihitaḥ yaḥ parasmādapavihitaḥ sa pūrvasmādapitī tadādigrahaṇāt  samudāyasya padatvam  tasya ca padatve āpacasipacasi devadattā ityatrāma ekāntaramāmantritamanantike ityekāntaratā siddhā bhavati etacca sarvasya dve ityatra bhāṣyavyākhyāna rakṣitenoktam atrocyate nanvekaikasmādapyatra tiṅ vihitastatoneka padam ucyate samudāyena vākyaparisamāptiriti samudāyasya padatvam yatha samudāyasyāvayavānā caikāctve samudāyasya dvirvacana bhavati nā vayavānā papāceti tathehāpi samudāyasya padatvam eva samudāyaśāstramanugṛhīta bhavati avayavayostu padasajñāyā samudāyasya tyāgāttadviṣaya śāstra hīna syāt tadādigrahaṇānuvṛttirapyapārthā syāt atra tu pakṣe andhondho duḥkhītyādau pratyeka padatvābhāve padakārya na syāt tadartha pratyeka vākyaparisamāptyā tatre padatve padakāryamanusandheyam anyastvāha gaurībhyāmityatra gurusajñāyā guroranuta iti plutaḥ syāt sthite tvekasajñādhikāre nadīsajñaivāpavādatvānna gurusajñeti nanu sthitepyekasajñādhikāre gurusajñānadīsajñayorbādhyabādhakabhāvo nāsti bhinnaviṣayatvāt tathāhi gurusajñā varṇamātrasya nadīsajñā tvīkārāntasya ucyate varṇamātrasyaiva keṣā cinmate nadīsajñā na cāsmin pakṣe lakṣmīprabhṛtiṣu strītvābhāvānnadīsajñā na prāpnotīti vācyam yatsamudāyagata strītvamavayave samāropya nadīsajñāvidhānāt jñāpaka cātra neyaṅavavaṅsthānāvastrī iti pratiṣedhaḥ tathā cācchīnadyornum ityatra śīnadyoḥ parata iti vṛttāvukta tadeva varṇapakṣe doṣaḥ tasmādyathānyāsamevāstu etattvanāgamam   na strīpratyaye cānupasarjane   yeya pratyayagrahaṇaparibhāṣā sā strīpratyayenupasarjane grāhikā na bhavati tena stryadhikārapratyayagrahaṇe saghātopi gṛhyate na tu yataḥ strīpratyayastadādireveti vākyārthaḥ tena strībhyo ḍhak iti yatoṇ tadantātkāraśabdān ṅīp na tadādestadantādeva ḍhak pratyayaḥ api tu samudāyādeva kaumbhakāreya iti anyathā hi avayavasya vṛddhisvarau syātām nanvaṇantān ṅīb vidhīyamānaḥ kṛdgrahaṇaparibhāṣayā kumbhakāraśabdādeva bhaviṣyati ucyate ṭiḍḍhāṇañ ityatrāṇiti na kṛdgrahaṇam api tu kṛdakṛdgrahaṇam  nanu pratyayagrahaṇaparibhāṣāyā abhāvādyathā strīpratyayāntāḍ ḍhagvidhīyamānaḥ kumbhakārītyasmātsamudāyaśabdādbhavati tathā kāraśabdādapi kva  citsyāt  naitat prādhānyātsamudāyādeva pravṛtteḥ tathā ṣyaṅaḥ saprasāraṇam ityatra ṣyaṅaḥ stryadhikāre vidhānāt strītvasthānivadbhāvena pratyayatvam atastadgrahaṇe pratyayagrahaṇaparibhāṣāyā niṣedhāt ṣyaṅmātrasya saprasārana paramakārīṣagandhīputra iti anupasarjana iti pratiṣedhādupasarjane strīpratyaye pratyayagrahaṇaparibhāṣā pravarttata eva tenātikārīṣagandhyaputrotikārīṣagandhyapatirityatra saprasāraṇa na bhavati nanvevamapi pradhāne kāryasapratyayātpradhānapratyayagrahaṇa eva pratyayagrahanaparibhāṣayā bhavityam eva cātikārīṣagandhyaputra ityatra saprasārana syādeva ucyate yadyatra saprasāraṇa syāttadānupasarjana iti pratiṣedhonarthakaḥ syāt nanvevamapyardhapippalītyatrāpi pratyayagrahaṇaparibhāṣayā halṅyādinā sulopo na prāpnoti strīpratyayāntasyopasarjanatvāt ucyate ekavibhakti cāpūrvanipāta ityatrānuvṛttavibhāṣāgrahaṇasya vyavasthitavibhāṣāvijñānādupasarjanasajñāyā abhāvaḥ kṛtaḥ ato na strīpratyaya iti tadāditadantaniyamaniṣedho bhavatyeva nanu śāstrīyopasajarnasajñāmābhūt laukika yadupasarjana tasminsati na strīpratyaya iti pravarttitu notsahate anupasarjana iti pratiṣedhāt tataśca pratyayagrahaṇaparibhāsayā tadādiniyamena bhavitavyameva upasarjanagrahaṇena laukikamupasarjana gṛhyata eva tathāhi  pañcakhaṭvītyatra samudāyibhyonyaḥ samudāya ityetasmindarśane śāstrīyopasarjanasajñābhāvepi laukikamupasarjanamāśritya gostriyorupasarjanasya  iti hrasvamuktā dvigoḥ iti ṅībuktaḥ  ucyate  ekavibhakti cāpūrvanipāte ityatrānuvṛttavibhāṣāgrahaṇasya vyavasthitavibhāṣāvijñād yathārdhapippalītyatra śāstrīyopasarjanābhāvena laukikopasarjanāśraya  hrasvatva na bhavati  tathānupasarjana iti pratiṣedhopi na bhavati atha vā halaṅyādi sūtre dīrghagrahaṇāt kva cidupasarjanastrīpratyayepi na strīpratyaye ityevātra varttata ityāhuḥ tenārdhapipyalītyatra halṅyādi lopaḥ sidhyati nanu katha jñapakam yāvatā vipakṣe he amba he nadi ityatra sulopo mābhūdityevamartha dīrghagrahaṇa karttavyam nanvatra bhavitavyamevaiṅhrasvātsabuddheḥ iti sulopena na ca dīrghagrahaṇātte nāpi na bhavitavyamiti vācyam anyathā hi halṅyādi sūtre dīrghagrahaṇameṅhrasvāt iti sūtra cākṛtvā hrasvaiṅoraṅyāpaḥ sabuddheriti kuryāt ata eveha he amba he nadi ityādau sulopo na bhaviṣyatīti  nanvevamapi badaryāḥ phala vikāra iti tasya vikāra ityarthenudāttādeśca ityañaḥ phale luk iti luki luk taddhitaluki iti ṅīpopi luki kṛtesati  dīrghagrahaṇe pratyayagrahaṇena badaramityatra sulopaḥ syāt sa mābhūditi sārthaka dīrghagrahanam  ucyate paratvādiha napusakādamā sulopo bādhanīyaḥ vyaktipadārthāśrayaṇāduktamiti vā   sajñāvidhau pratyayagrahaṇe tadantavidhirnāsti   tena taraptamapaughaḥ iti tarammātrasya ghasajñāyā gharūpakalpa iti ghe hrasva ucyamānastarapi bhavati na tu tarabante gaurī brāhmaṇitareti tathā ktaktavatū niṣṭhā iti ktaktavatvoreva niṣṭhāsajñā na tu tadantayoḥ tena dṛṣattīrṇetyatra dṛṣado dakārātparasya natvābhāvo dakārasya ca pūrvasyeti nanu sajñāvidhau pratyayagrahaṇaparibhāṣā mābhūt hrasvavidhau tu ghānte evottarapade hrasvatvena bhāvyam ucyate hṛdayasya hallekhayadaṇlāseṣu ityatrāṇgrahaṇa kṛtvā lekhagrahaṇāddhrasvavidhāvapi na tadantavidhiḥ radābhyām iti natva vidhāvapo sajñāvidhau tadantavidhipratiṣedhasāmarthyādeva na tadantavijñānam nanu hrasvavidhau tadantavidhiniṣedhasya kṛtārthatvāt sāmarthyamayuktam ucyate  yadi sajñāvidhau tadantavidhi pratiṣedhasya taraptabvidhāveva prayojana tadā suptiṅanta padam ityatrāntagrahaṇamakṛtvā sajñāvidhau pratyayagrahaṇe  tadantavidhirnāstītyapyajñāpayitvā taraptamapau pitau gha iti kriyatām  aya cārthaḥ pitau taraptamapau ghasajñau bhavata iti antagrahaṇāttu sajñāvidhāvityāderanopi viṣaya iti atha vā natvavidhau pratyayagrahaṇaparibhāṣā nāsti niṣṭhāśabdasya takāraviśeṣaṇatvenopādānāt kṛttaddhitasamāsāśca ityatra kṛttaddhitagrahaṇena tadantasyaiva sajñā na tatrayamupatiṣṭhate yatopratyaya iti pratiṣedhe prāpte kṛttaddhitayoḥ sajñārabhyate apratyaya iti ca pratyayāntasya pratiṣedha ityuktam tena tadantasya pratiṣedhe prāpte sajñārabhyamāṇā tadantasyaiva bhavati sātpadādyoḥ ityatra sādgrahaṇācca  yadi kevalasya taddhitasya sajñā syānna tadantasya tataḥ sāteḥ prātipadikatvāt tataḥ supi padāditvāt ṣatvapratiṣedhe siddhe sādgrahanamanarthaka  syāt  supi stha ityādau tu subgrahaṇe tadantasyopapadasajñārtho yatnaḥ karttavyaḥ jñāpaka tvasyāḥ suptiṅanta padamityatrāntagrahaṇam suptiṅoḥ pratyayatvāt pratyayagrahanaparibhāṣayaiva tadantatve sitdhe antagrahaṇamihānarthaka syāt   iti paribhāṣāvṛttau kārakapādaḥ   iti prathamodhyāyaḥ   prātipadikagrahaṇe liṅgaviśiṣṭasyāpi grahaṇam   yatra prātipadika gṛhyate tatra liṅgaviśiṣṭasya ṅyābantasyāpi grahaṇa bhavati liṅgagrahaṇenātra liṅgābhivyaktihetavaṣṭāvādayo gṛhyante abhidhāne abhidheyopacārāt tena yatheha bhavati lohitādiḍājbhyaḥ kyaṣ lohitāyate tathehāpi lohinīyate yathā sarvanāmnastṛtīyā ca iti yatheha bhavati bhavatā hetunā tathehāpi bhavatyā hetuneti ke cittvacittahastidheṣṭhak iti yathā hastinā samūho hāstikamiti bhavati tathā hastinīnā samūho hāstikamityāhuḥ taccāśobhanam ṭhagutpatteḥ prāgeva bhasyāḍhe taddhita iti puvadbhāvāt na ca jāteśca iti puvadbhāvapratiṣedhosti yata aupasakhyānikasya tena pratiṣedho na kriyate  etacca pravāhaṇeyībhārya ityatra jāteśca iti puvadbhāvapratiṣedhe siddhe vṛddhinimittasyeti punaḥ puvadbhāvapratiṣedhārtha pravāhanasya  ḍha iti yaduttarapadavriddhividhāna kṛtam  tena jāteśca ityasyānityatva jñāpitam tena jāteśca ityaupasakhyānikasya pratiṣedho na bhavatīti tatra nyāse vyākhyātam avaśya caitat anyathā sthitepi hāstikamityatra bhasyāḍha ityasya jāteśca iti pratiṣedhāt puvadbhāvo na syāt atha bhasyāḍha ityatra taddhita iti prasaptamī na viṣayasaptamīti cenna bhikṣādibhyoṇ ityatra viṣayasaptamyā vyākhyātatvāt tatra hyukta yuvatiśabdasya pāṭho bhyasyāḍhe taddhit iti puvadbhāvapratiṣedhārthaḥ yauvatamiti anyathā hi tipratyayāntasya yuvatiśabdasyānudāttāditvādanudāttāderañ ityañbādhanārthaḥ syāt tathāṇiñoranārṣayoḥ ityatra viṣayasaptamītvamasyā rakṣitenoktam ucyate ye parasaptamīmāśrityānudāttādeśca ityañbādhanārthameva bhikṣādibhyoṇ ityatra yuvatiśabdasya pāṭhamicchanti tanmatena draṣṭavyamidam ata eva bhāgavṛttikāro yuvatīnā samūho yauvanimityāha dṛśyate ca rūpalāvaṇyasapanna kalākuśalayauvanam yasya puṇyakṛtaḥ preṣya saphala tasya jīvita miti etasminneva darśane ṅyāp sūtre rakṣitenāsyāḥ paribhāṣāyā hastinīnā samūho hāstikamityudāharanamuktam jñāpaka cāsyā bhāṣyakāreṇa yuvā khalatipalitabalinajaratībhiḥ ityatra samānādhikaraṇādhikāre yuvajaratyoḥ samāsavidhānamuktam anyathā yadyeṣā na syāttadānayoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyānupapatteḥ samāsoghaṭamānaḥ syāt atrocyate nanu satyapi paribhāṣāyā astitve yuvatijaratyorbhinnārthatvādanupapanna eva samāsaḥ tathāhi yuvatirdvitīyavayāḥ jaratī tu vṛddhābhidhīyate ucyate yuvatirjaratīva cāñcalyavirahāt jaratī vā yuvatiriva cāñcalyāditi yuvatijaratyoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyamasti yadyeva yuvā jaratīva ucchūnastanatvāt śmaśruśūnyatvācceti tathā yuveva jaratī prāgalbhyāt tataścātrāpi sāmānādhikaraṇyamasti tatkatha paribhāṣā jñāpyate ucyate yuvajaratītyatra yūno jaratyā saha samāse kṛte tathopacarita sāmānādhikaraṇya na pratīyate svabhāvāt yathā pañcabhirbhuktamasyetyasyārthaḥ pañcabhuktaśabdena etacca bhāṣyakāradivarṇitaliṅgaviśiṣṭaparibhāṣāyā anyathānupapattyānumīyate nanu yadi sāmānādhikaraṇyānupapatteḥ paribhāṣājñāpanam tarhi viparītorthaḥ kimiti na jñapyate liṅgaviśiṣṭagrahaṇe prātipadikasyāpi grahaṇamiti prayojana cāpi revatījagatīhaviṣyābhyaḥ praśasye ityatra jagatīgrahaṇena jagatopi grahaṇamiti tathaiva eṇyā ḍhañ ityatra ṇīgrahaṇena ṇasyāpi grahaṇamiti ucyate yadi viparītortho jñapitaḥ syāttadā kumāraḥ śramaṇādibhiḥ ityatra śramaṇādīnā strīliñgānā nirddeśonarthakaḥ syāt nanvevamapi jaratyā samāsa ucyamāno jaratā na prāpnoti yuvajaranniti naitadasti vṛttyantare jaradbhiriti paṭhyate ubhayathā hyācāryeṇa śiṣyāḥ pratipāditā ityubhaya sidhyatīti yuvakhalatītyatra nyāsaḥ svarūpavidhiviṣayesvarūpavidhiviṣaye ca sāmānyena paribhāṣeyam jñāpakamapyāhuḥ roṇī iti kutsitoha nirddeśaḥ prathamāntatvāt pratyayavidhau pañcamī nyāyyā tatra yathā prākaraṇikī pañcamyatikramyate tathā grahaṇavatā prātivadikena tadantavidhirnāstītyetadapi vacanam tena yathā rauṇa ityatrāṇ bhavati tathājakarauṇa ityatrāpi nanu grahaṇavatā prātipadekena tadantavidhirnāstīti tadantavidhirniṣidhyate naceda roṇīti prātipadika strīpratyayāntatvāt eva tarhi taj jñāpayatyasvarūpavidhiviṣaye paribhāsā pravarttata iti tena kumārīmācaṣṭe kumārayatītyasya siddhaye bahulavacana nātikliśyate anityā ceyam taccānityatva śaktilāṅgalāṅkuśayaṣṭitomaraghaṭaghaṭītyatra ghaṭīgrahaṇena jñāpitam tenānmahata ityādinā mahatīpriya ityatrāttva na bhavati dviṣatparayostāpeḥ ityatra tu dviṣatī tāpayatītyatra dvitakārakanirddeśāt khacpratyayābhāvo vṛttikṛtā vyākhyātaḥ rājāhaḥsakhibhyaṣṭac ityatrāpi rājaśabdasyāpi pūrvanipātakaraṇānmahārājñītyatra ṭacpratyayābhāvo vṛttāvuktaḥ prātipadikagrahaṇe ityatra ṣaṣṭhīsamāsaḥ sa ca samarthaḥ padavidhiḥ ityetatparibhāṣosthānād bhavati tasyāḥ paribhāṣāyā ayamarthaḥ padānā vidhiḥ samartho bhavatīti vidhiśabdaścāca karmasādhanaḥ vidhīyate iti vidhiḥ na bhāvasādhano vidhāna vidhiḥ nāpyadhikaraṇasādhanaḥ padāni vidhīyantesminniti padavidhiḥ karmaṇyadhikaraṇe ca iti lyuḍpavādaḥ kipratyayaḥ tatra karmasādhanagrahaṇe tatropapada saptamīstham ityatropapadamiti mahatyāḥ sajñāyāḥ karaṇa jñāpakam  tathāhi anvarthasajñeya mahatī uapapadamiti tena samarthaparibhāṣopasthānāt mahānta kumbha karotītyatra sāpekṣatvenāsāmarthyātkarmaṇyaṇpratyayo  na bhavati  etacca prajonam evamupapacyate yadyatra karmasādhanasya vidhiśabdasya grahana nānyatheti yattu tatra maitreyeṇokta vidhīyate vidhiḥ etena karmaṇi kipratyayāntatāmācaṣṭe karaṇādhikaraṇayorhi lyuṭā kipratyayo bādhyate na ca tatra vāsarūpa vidhirasti ktalyuṭtumunkhalartheṣu vāsurūpavidhirnāstīti vacanāt sapradānāpādāne ca niravatārevipūrvasya dhāñaḥ karotyarthatvāt bhāvasādhanastu sabhavannapi nyāsakāreṇa nirasta iti tatrādhikaraṇe kipratyayo nāstīti yadukta tadayukta yasmāt padaśabde karmaṇyupapade karmaṇyadhikaraṇe ca iti lyuḍapavādaḥ kipratyostyevaucyate yathā kevala vidhiśabdamupakramya nyāsakṛtokta maitreyeṇāpi tathā vidhānādadoṣaḥ tathāhi tatra karmopapadatvābhāvāt karmaṇyadhikaraṇe ca ityasya na prāptiḥ  nanu tathāpyuttarakāla padaśabdasya karmaṇobhisabandhāt kipratyayaviṣayoyamiti parihṛtyāpavādaviṣayamutsargobhiniviśata iti lyuṭ pravarttinu  notsahate  ucyate paḍhasaskārapakṣentaraṅgatvātpravartito lyuṭ kipratyayena bādhitu na śakyate śvaḥ kariṣyatītyatra yathā luṭā lṛṭ pratyayaḥ etaccāsamyak śvaḥ kariṣyatītyatra yuktā lṛṭā luṭo bādhā luṭpratyayasyopapadasabandhenāvidhānāt kipratyayasya tu karmopapadasabandhena vidhānāt sarvadā vākyasaskāra eva yukta ityāhuḥ   vibhaktau liṅgaviśiṣṭagrahaṇam   vibhaktyāśrayeṣu kāryeṣu liṅgaviśiṣṭaparibhāṣā na pravarttate tena gomatītyatrogidacām iti numna bhavati tathā supusītyatra pusosuṅ neti yuvatīḥ paśyetyatra śvayuvamaghonāmataddhhita iti saprasāraṇa na bhavati anye tvāhuḥ allopon ityatrān iti yogavibhāgādangrahaṇābhisabandhādannantānā śvayuvamaghonā saprasāraṇam yukta caitat anyathā yadyanayā paribhāṣayā saprasāraṇābhāvo vijñāyate tadā yuvatśabāt kṛdikārāditi ṅiṣi kṛte yuvatītyatra saprasāraṇa syādeva iya ca paribhāṣā yuvoranākau ityatra bhāṣye paṭhitā matuvasorityatra nyāsakāreṇa vyākhyātā etāvataiva pramāṇam   iti sīradevakṛtāyā paribhāṣāvṛttau samarthapādaḥ   sūtre liṅgavacanamatantram   tena karmaṇā yamabhipraiti ityatra yamiti pulliṅgenaikavacanena ca nirddeśasyātantratvāt liṅgāntare vacanāntare ca sajñā bhavati brāhmaṇyai dadāti brāhmaṇebhyo dadāti nyāyasiddhoyamarthaḥ sūtre dhānyapalālanyāyena liṅgavacanayorūpādānāt jñāpaka cātrārtha ākaḍārādekā sajñā ityatraikāgrahaṇam ardha napusakam ityatra napusakagrahaṇa ca dyadbhyo luṅi ityatra tvekavacanena nirddeśe karttavye yadbahuvacana tatsāmarthyānneya pravarttate   nañivayuktamanyatsadṛśādhikaraṇe tathāhyarthaḥ   tenāñceśchandasyasarvanāmasthānam iti sarvanāmasyānasadṛśamasarvanāmasthāna vibhaktirgṛhyate asyā bhāṣyertho vyākhyātaḥ nañivayuktamanyasminsadṛśādhikaraṇe varttana iti eva cānyaditi prathamāntapratirūpako nipātonyasminnityarthe varttata iti vijñeyam anyaḥ punarāha nañivayukta śabdarūpa sadṛśādhikaraṇe varttate kutaḥ yasmādanyacchabdarūpa mukhyārthavāciśabdarūpādityarthaḥ tadeva nañivaśabābhyā mukhyādarthādvyavacchidya gauṇa rthe śabdo vyavasthāpyate tathahyartha iti tādṛśa evārthaḥ pratīyata ityarthaḥ etenāsyārthasya pratītisiddhatva darśayati sā caiṣā pratītirnañsamāsa kurvatācāryeṇa vyaktīkṛtā tathāhi kṣiatriyārthe upacarito yo brāhmaṇaśabdastena saha nañ samasyate na brāhmaṇobrāhmaṇa iti ata eva tatra nañā mukhyādarthādvyavacchidya gauṇerthe vyavasthāpyate yathā nīla ca tadutpala ceti nīlotpalamiti nīlaguṇetaraguṇebhyo vyavacchidya nīlaguṇamutpala vyavasthāpyate iyāstu viśeṣaḥ kevalaḥ prayuktoya brāhmaṇaśabdo mukhyamevārtha gamayati prasiddhivaśāt gauna tu nañsanikarṣāt tatropacaritasya kṣatriyārthasyābhidhānāt tadeva paryudāse nañ vyākhyāto bhavati eva cābrāhmaṇa ityasya tatpuruṣasyottarapadārthapradhānatopapadyate tasyā ca satyāmanekamityatraikavacanāntatā sidhyati tathāhi bhramavaśād dvitvādāvarthe loke ekārthasyopacaritasya nañsanidhau gamyamānatva dṛśyate tathā cāropitaikatvasyārthasyābhidhāna ekaśabda upāttaḥ svasakhya eva yathā sākāśya catvāri yojanānītyupacāre ekavacanamupapadyate yadā tu yatrādvitvādāvarthe dvitvamāropita tadbhedaścāśrīyate tadā tadvacanabhedaḥ yathā dyudbhyo luṅi vṛdbhyaḥ syasanoḥ iti eva ca kṛtvā anekeṣāmityādayaḥ prayogāḥ sidhyanti yoyamatrottarapadārthaprādhānye nañuktastasya prāyikatvamāhuḥ akarttari ca kārake ityatra kārakagrahaṇāt nitye hyasminnañyuktakartṛsādṛśyādeva kārakapratītiḥ syāt tena prasajyapratiṣedhepi nañisaddho bhavati asūryapaśyā rājadārā iti tathābhidhānasāmarthyādadharmādayo nañsamāsā viruddhādāvarthe dṛśyante iti nanu nañsamāsavidhau ñakāro na karttavyo na hyanyo naśabdosti vyadvyavacchedāya ñakāropādānamiti atra pūrvapakṣe rakṣitena vyākhyātam atrāpīdamasti prayojana netyukte niṣedhasūtrametanmābhūditi naitat vidhivākyānarthakyaprasaṅgāt na ca vidhipratiṣedhayoḥ paryāyaḥ kalpanīyaḥ mahāvibhāṣayā vikalpasya siddhatvāt asati vā naño ñakāre svarūpanirddeśādanavyayatve vibhiktiśrutireva pratiṣedhavākyatā nirasyati na caivamasmadādeśasya ṣaṣṭhībahuvacanasya grahaṇaprasaṅgaḥ ṣaṣṭhyantasya ṣaṣṭhītyanenaiva samāsasya siddhatvāditi atrāhuḥ nanu katha ṣaṣṭhyantasya nañśabdasya ṣaṣṭhī ityanenaiva samāsobhidhīyate  yāvatā grāmo naḥ svamityatrāntaraṅgānapi vidhīn bahiraṅgo lug bādhate iti vacanānnasādeśātprāk samāse vibhakterluki ca kṛte ṣaṣṭhyantatvābhāvānnasādeśo  na prāpnoti  na cāsti pratyayalakṣaṇena ṣaṣṭhyantakāryam sāmānyātideśe viśeṣānatideśa iti ṣaṣṭhyantaviśeṣakāryātideśābhāvāt athāpyanalvidhāvityatra vidhigrahaṇādviśeṣopyatidiśyata evamapi tatra śrūyamāṇavibhaktyarthāt sthagrahaṇādvibhaktyabhāve nasādeśo nāstyevana iti tu samāsārthe sūtre kṛtentaraṅgāniti paribhāṣā nāstīti nasādeśasya samāsaśāstranimittatvāt tasmāccintyoya rakṣitaḥ atra ke ciccintayanti yādṛśotra pūrvapakṣastādṛśa eva siddhāntaḥ yathā hi  antaraṅgānapīti vacanāt ṣaṣṭhībahuvacanasya nasśabdasya grahaṇa śaṅkita tvayā tathā mayāpi ṣaṣṭhyantasya ṣaṣṭhī ityanenaiva samāsaḥ siddha  ityuktam    gatikārakepapadānā kṛdbhiḥ samāsavacana prāk subutpatteḥ    supsupā ityadhikārepi kugatiprādayaḥ kartṛkaraṇe kṛtā bahulam upapadamatiṅ iti ca gatīnā kārakāṇāmupapadānā ca yoya samāsaḥ sa subutpatte  prāgeva veditavyaḥ  tena praṣṭhītyatra praśabdasya gatisajñakasya sthaśabdenāsubantenaivātaścopasarga iti kapratyayāntena kugatiprādaya iti samāso bhavati yadi tu subantena samāsaḥ syāttadā supaḥ prāgantaraṅgatvāṭṭāpsyāt eva cādantatvābhāvātpuyogādākhyāyām iti ṅīṣ na syāt tathāśvadhanaśabdayośca labdhakaraṇavyapadeśayoḥ kṛdantenaiva krītaśabdena kartṛkaraṇe kṛtā bahulam iti samāsaḥ tathā cāśvakrītadhanakrītaśabdayoradantatvāt krītātkaranapūrvāt iti ṅīṣ bhavati tathā kacchaśabdasya kapratyayāntena paśabdenopapadamatiṅ iti samāsaḥ tathā ca kacchapaśabdasyādantatvāt kacchapīti jāteḥ iti ṅīṣ bhavati anyānyapi bahūni prayojanāni bhāṣye pratipāditāni  nanu kṛdantaiḥ samāsa kṛtvā strīpratyayaḥ kimartha pratipādyate yāvatā kṛtpratyayotpattyanantarakāla eva samāsāttannimittabhūtācca supastatopyantaraṅgatvāt  strīpratyayācca prāgeva puyogādākhyāyām ityādyairvākyaiḥ strīpratyaye kriyamāṇe praṣṭhī aśvakrītītyādi siddhyati  maivam eva hi praṣṭhādisamudāyasyākṛdantatvena prātipadikatvābhāvattatsamudāyāt strīpratyayo na śakyate kartum atrocyate  kṛttaddhitasamāsāśca ityatra kṛdgrahaṇena kṛdgrahaṇe gatikārakapūrvasyāpi grahaṇamiti kṛdgrahaṇaparibhāṣayā samudāyasya prātipadikatvamastyeva maivam arthavadadhāturapratyayaḥ prātipadikam ityatrāpratyaya iti pratyayagrahaṇaparibhāṣayā pratyāntasya prātipadikasajñā na prapnoti ata eva tadviṣaye kṛdgrahaṇena kṛdantasya sajñā na tu kṛdgrahaṇaparibhāṣayā gatikārakapūrvasyāpi yadi syāttadā mūlakenopadaśa bhuṅkte iti tṛtīyāprabhṛtīnyatarasyām iti samāsābhāvapakṣepi tṛtīyāyā luk syāt na ca vācyameva hi vikalpena samāsavacanamanarthaka syāt svarārthatvāt gatikārakopapadātkṛt ityeṣa tatpuruṣāśrayaḥ svaro mā bhūditi  ki ca yadi samāsātprāk strīpratyayaḥ syāt tadā prabhāvinī prabhaviṇītyatra ṅyantasyottarapadasyānto nakāro na bhavatīti prātipadikāntanumvibhaktiṣu  ca iti pakṣe ṇatva na syāt  iha yadyapi prāk subutpatteriti sāmānyenoktam tathāpi gatikārakopapapadānā subantānāmeva samāso bhavati tena carmakrīti carmakārītyatra subantatvātpadanibandhano nalopaḥ sidhyati vaiyākarana ityatra ca padatvādaijāgamaḥ pramāṇa cātra tatpuruṣe kṛti bahulam iti saptamyā alumvidhānam atra ca pakṣebhiprayaṇādeḥ śakandhvāditvātsamāsastena sādhutvam nanu yadyuttarapade vibhaktirna bhavati tarhi tasya padatva na syāt tataścottarapadavyapadeśābhavāduttarapade parato vidhīyamānoluk sarasijamityatra na syāt ucyate samāsāvayavasya hi parasya bhāgasya rūḍhyottarapadavyapadeśaḥ svīkriyate etaccottarapadādhikārādavasīyate avaśya caitat anyathā satyapi subantānā samāsa uttarapadatve cāpadādividhāviti vacanāt kvāpyuttarapadatva na syāt jñāpitā ceya paribhāṣā bhāṣyakāreṇopapadamatiṅ ityatiṅgrahaṇena taduktam supsupā ityadhikārāttiṅantena samāsasabhava eva nāsti kimatiṅgrahaṇena kṛta ca taj jñāpayatyetayoryogayoḥ supsupā iti nābhisambadhyate tena gatikārakopapadanā kṛdbhiḥ samāsavacana prāk subutpatterityupapanna bhavati nanu yadi gatyādīnā supaḥ prāk subantena śabdāntareṇa samāsastadā dhātūpasargasamudāyasyāpi syāt eva ca dhātūpasargasamudāyādvibhaktiḥ syāt ucyate pūrva dhātuḥ śādhanena yujyata ityetasmindarśana ida samādheyam etasyāśca dvāvarthau gatikārakopapadātkṛt ityatra nyāsakṛtā vyākhyātau gatikārakopapadānā kṛdbhireva samāso bhavati sa ca prāk subutpatterityekorthaḥ gatikārakopapadānāmaviśeṣeṇa samāso bhavati kṛdbhistu prāk subutpatteriti dvitīyaḥ tatra dvitīyerthe prapacatitarāmityatrāpi samāsaḥ ke cittu subantenaiva gatyādīnā kṛdbhiḥ kva citsamāsamāhuḥ tathā copapadamatiṅ ityatra rakṣitenoktam yathā dhanakrītetyatra subantena samāsastathoraḥkeṇetyatrāpi tena sopadādau iti satva na bhavati
