uraśśabdasya subantena kapratyayāntena samāse kṛte kakārasya padāditvāt sopadādau iti visarjanīyasya satva na bhavatīti tadetadayuktam tathāhi yadyapi subantena samāsastathāpi satvena bhavitavyam uttarapadatve cāpadādividhāviti pratyayalakṣaṇapratiṣedhāt kaśabdasyāmubantatvena padatvābhāvāt ucyate uttarapadatve cāpadādividhāviti yoya pratyayalakakṣaṇapratiṣedhaḥ sa sopadādā iti pratiṣedhe karttavye na pravarttate gatikārakopapadānāmityasya prāyikatva sopadādau ityatra pratyayalakṣaṇapratiṣedhāpravarttana ca bhāskārāntetyatra satvanipātanādavasitamtathāhi gatikārakopapadānāmiti kṛtvā yadi supaḥ prāk samāsaḥ tadā bhāskara ityatra uttarapadatvābhāvādeva sopadādau iti satva siddham  athāsyāḥ paribhāṣayāḥ prāyikatvādbhāskara ityatra subantayoreva samāsastathāpyuttarapadatve cāpadādividhāviti pratyayalakṣaṇapratiṣedhena padatvābhāvātsopadādau  iti satva siddha syāt  tatkṛtamuktārthasya jñāpakamiti jñāpakasya prayojanam uraḥkeṇetyādau sopadādau iti satvābhāvaḥ nanveva yadā supaḥ prāk samāsastadā kakārasyāpadāditvādayaḥkrītītyatra sopadādau iti satva syāt ucyate bhavitavyamevātra satveneti manyate atha vā sopadādau ityatra pāśakalpakakāmyeṣviti parigaṇanānna bhavati yadyeva pāśakalpakakāmyeṣviti parigaṇana na kriyatām bhāskārāntetyatra yatsatvanipātana tatsāmarthyāduttarapade satva na bhavatītyevāstu tata evāyaḥkrītītyādau satvābhāvaḥ siddha iti pāśakalpakakāmyeṣviti parigaṇanamanarthakameveti   iti paribhāṣāvṛttāvaparapādaḥ   kva cidapavādaviṣayepyusargobhiniviśate   tena kāñcanī vāsayaṣṭiriti nitya vṛddhaśarādibhya iti mayaṭo viṣayenudattādeśca ityañ bhavati tathā pradīyatā dāśarathāya maithilītyatrāta iñ ityasya viṣaye prāg dīvyatoṇ ityaṇ bhavati anyastvāha samarthānā prathamadvā ityato vanuvṛtteriñobhāvapakṣe tasyāpatyam ityaṇā dāśarathāyeti siddham etaccāyuktam yatrotsargo vibhāṣāpavādopi tatrāpavādenavinirmukte viṣaya utsargo na pravarttate pīlāyā vā iti jñāpakāt vāgrahaṇa tu vākyārtham  daśarathāpatyamityādisamāsārtha daivayajñiśaucivṛkṣisātyamugrikāṇḍeviddhibhyonyatarasyām ityate dvitīyānyatarasyā grahaṇanuvṛttiruktā nyāsakṛtā jñāpaka cātra kaṭa kārako vrajatītyatrākenorbhāviṣyaḍhādhamarṇyayoḥ iti bhaviṣyadakaprayoge karmaṇi ṣaṣṭhīniṣedhavidhānam taddhi yadyaṇ karmaṇi ca ityapavādaviṣaye tumunṇvalau kriyāyā kriyārthāyam ityutsargaḥ pravarttate tadopapadyate nānyathā nanu vāsarūpavidhināṇ karmaṇi ca ityapavādaviṣaye ṇvulapi siddha eva tatkuto jñāpakam ucyate kriyāyā kriyārthāyāmupapade vāsarūpavidhirna bhavati ṇvultṛcau iti ṇvuli siddhe punastumunṇvulau kriyāyām iti lṛṭ śeṣe ca iti viṣaye ṇvulo vidhānādavagamyate anyathā vāsarūpavidhinaiva lṛḍviṣaye ṇvulaḥ siddhatvātpunastanna kuryāt kṛta cātovasīyatesminviṣaye vāsarūpavidhinā tṛjādayo na bhavantīti nanvasati prayojane jñāpakam asti ca tumunṇvulau kriyāyām ityasya prayojana bhaviṣyatkāle ṇvul yathā syāt  tenākenorbhaviṣyadādharmaṇyayoḥ ityatra bhaviṣyadadhikāravihitasyākasya grahaṇād varṣaśatasya pūrakaḥ putrapautrāṇā darśaka ityatra ṣaṣṭhīniṣedho  na bhavati  ucyate bhaviṣyatkāle vihitasyākasya tatra gṛhaṇādiha doṣo nāstīti jñāpakavādinobhiprāyaḥ tathāhi varṣaśatasya pūraka ityatra pūraka iti pada na bhaviṣyatkāle prakaraṇādevaina sarvatrāpavādaviṣaya utsargāḥ pravarttante ata eva gatyarthakarmaṇi dvitīyācarturthyau ceṣṭāyāmanadhvani ityatra dvitīyāgrahaṇa kriyate anyathā caturthī cetyevocyeta cakārakaraṇasāmarthyātkṛdyogalakṣaṇā ṣaṣṭhī na bhaviṣyati grāma gantā grāmāya gantā bhāṣye tu sūtrameva pratyākhyātam taduktam kimarthamidamucyate caturthī yathā syāt dvitīyā tu siddhā karmaṇītyeva caturthyapi siddhā sapradāna ityeva na sidhyati karmaṇā yamabhipraiti sa sapradānam ityucyate na ca karmaṇātra grāmamabhipraiti ki tarhi kriyayā kayā kriyayā gatikriyayā kriyāgrahaṇa ca tatrātidiśyata iti tatraitasminbhāṣye rakṣitenoktam yathā bhāṣye sūtra pratyākhyātam tathā śobhana grāma gacchatīti kriyāviśeṣaṇasya karmatva na syāt grāmāya gamyata iti cākarmakatvādbhāve lakāraḥ syāt atrocyate nanu keya vāco yuktiḥ gatyārthādi sūtre sati kriyāviśeṣaṇasya karmatvāt śobhana grāma gacchatīti sidhyati tadaiva ca bhāve lakārābhāvādgrāmāya gamyata iti na bhavati grāmo gamyata ityeva bhavatīti ucyate  gatyārthādi sūtre sati prārthanādhyavasānādikriyābhedena karmabhūtāyā gatikriyāyā viśeṣaṇatvācchobhanasya karmatvena kriyāgrahaṇa karttavyamityasyāsarvaviṣayatvācchobhana  grāma gacchatīti bhavati  tathā gamikriyāvyāpyatvādgrāmasya karmatvena karmaṇi lakāreṇa karmaṇobhihitatvādgrāmo gamyata ityeva bhavati nākarmakatvādbhāve lakāreṇa grāmāya gamyata iti tatyarthādi sūtrābhāve tu grāmāya gacchatīti siddhaye kriyāgrahaṇa karttavyamityanena sapradānatva vaktavyam asya cārtha kriyayā karmaṇā yamabhipraiti sa sapradāna bhavatīti atra grāmāya gacchatītyatra yā gatikriyā tasyāḥ prārthanādhyavasānādikriyāvyāpyatvātkarmatvam tathāhi kaścitphalaprepsuḥ phala paśyatyetasyā etatphalamiti dṛṣṭvā prārthate tatastā karttumadhyavasyati gamamanā ca kriyā kāraṇā nimittamiti gamyamānayāpi prārthanādhyavasānādikriyāyayā gatikriyayāḥ karmatvam tathā ca karmabhūtayā gatikriyayā grāmasyābhisasambandhātsapradānatvam ata evātra pakṣe rakṣitena grāmāya gamyata iti cākarmakatvādbhāve lakāraḥ syādityuktam eva ca śobhana grāma gacchatītyatra karmaṇi dvitīyānurodhena prārthanādikriyābhedo vyākhyeyaḥ  tataśca gatikriyāyāḥ karmatvābhāvāttadviśeṣaṇasya kutaḥ karmatvamiti yuktamukta kriyāviśeṣaṇasya karmatva na syācchobhana grāma gacchatītyatra nanu prārthanādikriyābhedavivakṣāyāmapi grāmasya gatikriyāvyaptatvātkartturīpsitatama karma iti karmatva prāpnoti kriyāgrahaṇa ca karttavyamiti sapradānatva ca tatra paratvātkarmasajñayā siddha śobhana grāma gacchatīti dhātorapi sakarmakatve bhāve lakāro na bhaviṣyati ucyate eva hi śobhana grāmāya gacchatītyatrāpi karmatvena sapradānasya bādhanāccaturthī na syāt katha tarhi bhāṣye sūtra pratyākhyātam ucyate gramāya gacchatītyatra purvavipratiṣedhena sapradānasajñaiva  tathā grāmo gamyata iti karmaṇi lakārārtha prārthanādikriyābhedābhāvācchobhana grāma gacchatītyatra śobhanamityasya karmatvātha bheda eva  vyākhyeyo grāmamityasya tvabheda eveti bhāṣyakārābhiprayaḥ    iti paribhāṣāvṛttāvanabhihitapādaḥ   antaraṅgānapi vidhīn bahiraṅgo lyab bādhate   samāsasya dvipadāśrayatvād bahiraṅgo lyabantaraṅgānvidhīn bādhate tena pradhāyetyatra dadhāterhiḥ iti hyādeśo na bhavati pradāyetyatra cācaupasargātta iti jñāpaka cātrādau jagdhirlyapti kiti ityatra lyabgrahaṇam anyathā hi prajagdhyetyatrāntaraṅgatvāt tkāvasthāyā takārādau kitītyeva jagdhau siddhe lyapīti na kuryāt taduktam jagdhau siddhentaraṅgatvātti kitīti lyabucyate jñāpayatyantaraṅgāṇā lyapā bhavati bādhanamiti nanu yathā jagdhyādeśasyāntaraṅgatva tathā lyabādeśasyāpi nityatvam kṛtākṛtaprasaṅgitvāt tadeva nityāntarañgayoḥ paratvāllyapā bhavitavyam tato lyapi jagdhyādeśo yathā syādityevamartha lyagrahaṇa tatkuto jñāpakam ucyate jagdhyādeśasyāpi nityatvam lyabādeśe kṛtesiddhaparibhāṣayā tasya prāpteḥ atha prajagdhyetyatra katha lyapo lakārasyetsajñā yāvatā lyavādeśasya pratyayādhikārevidhānāt pratyayatva nāsti pratyayasyetyanuvṛttau pratyayāderitsajñā anyathā śīṅaḥ śakārasyetsajñāyā śīṅaḥ sārvadhātuke ityatra viśeṣaṇārthatā syāt īṅ iti hi kṛte īṅ gatāvityasyāpi grahaṇa syāt ṅī gatāviti divādau paṭhite śīṅo ṅakārpadeśavaiyarthyāyetsajñā tarhi śāseḥ śakārasyetsajñāyā śāsa idaṅhaloḥ ityatra viśeṣaṇārthaḥ syāt tadapi nāsti aṅgā sāhacaryādāsa upaveśana ityasyāgrahanāt sthita eva yathā āṅaḥ śāsu icchāyāmityasyāgrahaṇam ṅuṅ śabda ityatra tarhi āderṅakārasyetsajñā syāt etadapi na antaraṅgatvādantyaṅakārasyetsajñāyāmiṣṭasiddheḥ yadi vā ṅakāradvayamādau kṛtvā ṅaṅu śabda iti paṭhite ṅuvata ityatra na dūṣaṇam śā hau ityatra tarhi śādeśe śakārasyetsajñāyā sarvādeśārthaḥ syāt paramakhaṇḍaḥ paramakhaṅga ityādau prātipadikakhakārasyetsajñāyā khityanavyayasya iti mum syāt ucyate sthānivattvenāsya pratyayatvāditsajñā bhavati  yadyeva dvigurekavacanam ityatra yadukta rakṣitena pāribhāṣikaikavacanagrahaṇe pratyayādhikāresyāvidhānādasati pratyayatve pañcamyādyekavacanaṅakārasyetsajñā  na syāt iti tadayaktam   tathāhi pañcapalīśabdādanattyapakṣe bahvarthatvāt bhyasādiṣu kṛteṣu teṣā sthāne pañcamyādyekavacaneṣu kṛteṣu tatra pūrvavatsthānivattvamastyevetītsajñāprāpteḥ ucyate yathā tkāpratyayasthāne lyap vidhīyate na tathā bhyasādiṣu kṛteṣu ṅasyādayo vidhīyante ki tarhi bahuṣu bahuvacane prāpte ekavacana ṅasyādi vidhīyate kutotra sthānyādeśabhāvaḥ nanu tathāpi rakṣitoktiraktirasaṅgatā ṅasyādiṅkāravaccaturthīṅakārasyāpītsajñāprāpteḥ ucyate  pañcamyādiryasya sa pañcamyādiḥ pañcamyā ādiḥ pañcamyādiriti ca pañcamyādiśabdasya bahubrīhitatpuruṣayorekaśeṣeṇa caturthyāḥ sākṣādeva grahaṇamākhyātam nanvevamapi ṭakārasya cuṭū itītsajñā na syāt eva tarhi pañcamyāderityādiśabdaḥ prakāre yadyeva ṅakārasya na syādityayuktam ṭakārasyāpi na syāditi vaktavyam ucyate ṅakārasyeti doṣopalakṣaṇamidam tena pratyayatvābhāve paradeśe niyamena prayogo na syādityapi draṣṭavyam nanu tathāpi labdhapratyayaikavacanasajñakasya ṅasyādervidhānādastyevetsajñā ki caikavacanādisajñānubandharahitasyaiva vidhīyate na sānubandhakasya ekavacanādisajñāyāḥ prāgevetsajñakatvāllopapravṛtteḥ ucyate ekavacanādisajñā svādi sūtra eva vidhīyate atra pratyayatvābhāvāditsajñā nāsti ataḥ sanubandhakasyaivaikavacanādisajñā na ca svādi sūtra eva pratyayasajñā śakyate karttum arthavattvābhāvāt prayoga evārthavattvāt pratyayasajñā na cātra pratyayādhikāro nāstīti vācyam yatorthavataḥ pratyasajñāvidhānasāmarthyāt śāstradvāreṇa prayoga eva pratyayasajñā pravarttate yattu dvigu sūtre bhāgavṛttikāreṇoktam māharaṇa samāhāra iti bhāve ghañ iti sthite yadukta karmasādhane pañce kumāryaḥ samāhṛtāḥ pañcakumāri iti gostriyorupasarjanasya iti na prāpnoti eva tarhi bhāvasādhana iti tadayuktam yato gostriyorupasarjanasya ityasyābhāve hrasvo napusake prātipadikasya iti vidyata eva napusakatva tu sa napusakam ityanena ata eva svamornapusakāt iti lukā na vibhaktiśrutiḥ   iti paribhāṣāvṛttau dvigupādaḥ   iti dvitīyodhyāyaḥ   asati sabhave bādhana bhavati   asti ca sabhavo yadubhaya syāt   kāryayorvirodhādasati samāveśaśadbhāve balavataikenāparasya bādhana bhavati tadyathā goda iti kapratyayenāṇpratyayasya bādhana bhavati yathā vṛkṣebhya ityatraittvena dīrghasya yadi tvasti sambhavastadobhayamapi bhavati yaccabdo yadyarthe tadāśabdaścādhyāhāryaḥ yathā kekayamitrayupralayānā yāderiya ityatreyādeśepi kṛte vṛddhiḥ kaikeyaḥ prāleyaḥ  tathā yathājātīyastathājātīya ityatra prakāravacane jātīyar ityanena svabhāvāt prakāravati vidhīyamānena jātīyarā prakāravacane thāl ityanena  svabhāvāt prakāramātre vidhīyamanasthālpratyayo na bādhyate  tathā corayati dhārayati cikīrṣayatītyādāvārddhadhātukasajñā pratyayasajñā na bādhate tatra corayati cikīrṣayatītyādāvārddhadhātukatvena laghūpadhaguṇāllopau prayojanam dhārayatītyatrācoñṇiti iti vṛddhirārddhadhātukatvābhāvepi sidhyati tasyānārddhadhātukādhikārīyatvāt ata eva priyamācaṣṭe prāpayatītyādau vṛddhiḥ  yasmādeva tato yadukta satyāpapāśādi sūtrenunyāsakāreṇa corayati dhārayati cikīrṣayatītyādāvārddhadhātukatvābhāve guṇavṛddhyallopā na syuriti tatra dhārayatītyayuktam nayuktam dhārayatītyatra hetumiti ca ityanena dvitīyo ṇijvaktavyaḥ tathā ca corayatīti satyāpapāśādi sūtreṇa vihitasya prathamasya ṇica ārddhadhātukasajñā prayojanamuktam dhārayatītyatra hetumati ca ityasya yadi tasyārddhadhātukasajñā na syāttadā pūrvasyā ṇeraniṭi iti ṇilopo na syāt nanu vṛddhyabhāvo doṣa uktastatki ṇeraniṭi ityasyābhāvenokta syāt ucyate guṇavṛddhyallopā iti vṛddhiścācceti vṛddhyatau tayorlopau vṛddhyallopau atha vā lupyete iti lopau vṛddhyatau ca tau lopo ceti vṛddhyallopāviti karmadhārayaḥ tato guṇaśca vṛddhyallopau ceti dvandvaḥ tena guṇavṛddhyallopā na syurityasyāyamarthaḥ guṇo na syāt vṛddhilopo na syāt ato lopaśca na syāt nanu kathamatra vṛddherlopaḥ yāvatā ṇeraniṭi ityanena ṇereva lopaḥ ucyate paratvādvṛddhau kṛtāyā ṇeraniṭi iti vṛddereva lopaḥ atha vā lopaśabdenatrābhāvobhidhīyate tenāyamarthaḥ vṛddherabhāvo na syāt aikārasya śravaṇāt lope nu kṛte vṛddherabhāvo bhavati aikārasyāśravaṇāt jñapaka cātra nitya kauṭilye gatau ityatra nityagrahaṇam taddhi gatyarthebhyaḥ kauṭilye eva yaṅ yathā syāt kriyāsamābhihāre mā bhūdityevamartha kriyate yadi tu satyapi sabhave bādhana bhavet tadā nityagrahaṇamanarthaka syāt kauṭilyayaṅā kriyāsamabhihārayaṅo bādhasya siddhatvāt nanu kuṭila krāmatīti vākya mā bhūdityevamartha nityagrahaṇa kriyate tatkuto jñāpakam ucyate kuṭila kramatītyādika vākyamiṣyamāṇameva tathā ca rakṣitaḥ nityagrahana vākyanivṛttyartha na bhavati vākyasyeṣyamāṇatvāt   ktalyuṭtumunkhalartheṣu vāsarūpavidhirnāsti   tena napusake bhāve ktapratyayo lyuṭapratyayaśca nitya bhāve ghaña bādhate hasana hasitamiti hāsamiti na bhavati tathā samānakarttṛkeṣu tumun icchārtheṣūpapadeṣu liṅloṭāvitīmau nityameva bādhate icchati bhoktumiti tathāto yuc itīṣadduḥsuṣu iti khala nityameva bādhate īṣatpānaḥ somo bhavateti yatra tu ktādaya evāpodyā utsargā iti yāvat yonyojādipratyayopavādaḥ stryadhikārāt prāgbhūtastatra vāsarūpavidhirbhavatyeva yathā ajvidhau bhayādīnāmupasakhyānamityajviṣaye vāsarūpavidhinā lyuḍapi bhavati bhaya bhayanamiti varṣa varṣaṇamiti pramāṇa cātra vṛṣabho varṣaṇāditi bhāṣyakṛdvacanam ata evāśite bhuvaḥ karaṇabhāvayoḥ ityatra yadukta nyāsakṛtā ghaña sārūpyādbādhate khac lyuṭpratyayaḥ punarvāsarūpavidhinā bhavatyeva āśitabhavam āśitabhavanamiti tadupapadyate etasminvākya indumaitreyayoḥ śāśvatiko virodhaḥ tathāhi pratyayasūtrenunyāsakāra uktavān pratiyantyanenārthāniti pratyayaḥ erac pusi sajñāyā ghaḥ prāyeṇa iti vā gha iti maitreyaḥ punarāha pusi sajñāyām iti ghapratyaya eva erac ityacpratyayastu karaṇe lyuṭā bādhitatvānna śakyate karttum na ca vāsrūpavidhirasti ktalyuḍityādivacanāt tatrāya maitreyābhiprāyaḥ ktalyuṭtumunkhalartheṣvityatra ktagrahaṇena napusakakto gṛhyate lyuṭā sāhacaryāt lyuṭsahacaritasya ktapratyayasya grahaṇāt tadadhīte tadveda iti matibuddhipūjārthebhyaśca iti ktaviṣaye laṭo vidhānācca anyathā ñītaḥ ktaḥ ityanena laṭo bādhanānmedyatīti na syāt na caiva miderguṇaḥ ityasyānarthakya bhūte laṅyamedyadityatra kṛtārthatvāt eva ca matibuddhipūjārthebhyaśca ityatra najiṅbādhanārthaḥ suptaśabdasya pāṭhonarthakaḥ nānarthakaḥ syaṣṭārthatvāt avaśya caitat anyathā sāmānyagrahanepi svapeḥ kto bādhitu na śakyate ñisvapo ñītkaraṇasāmarthyāt ktādīnāmapodyāna vāsarūpavidheravasthāpitatvācca tadeva yadi bhāvavihitaktapratyayagrahaṇavijñānāllyuḍapi bhāvavihito gṛhyate tadā ktagrahaṇamakṛtvā lyuḍgrahaṇameva kuryāt ata eva hāsamiti na bhaviṣyati lyuḍgrahana tu na pratyākhyeya sakarmakebhyo bhāve ktapratyayasyābhāvāt tatrobhayorūpādānasāmarthyād sāmānyavihito lyuḍ gṛhyate ato yuktamukta karanalyuṭā vāsarūpavidherabhāvādacpratyayo nāstīti avaśya caitat anyathā vuñchaṇādi sūtre saptadaśa pratyayā iti vṛttigranthosādhuḥ syāt parimāṇākhyāyām ityanenāca bādhitvā ghaño vidhānāt nanveva vāsarūpostriyām ityatra yadukta rakṣitena lyuṭsahacarito napusakakto nitya bādhaka iṣyata iti tathā matibuddhipūjārthebhyaśca ityatra yadukta ktalyuṭtumunkhalartheṣviti lyuṭsahacarito napusakakto gṛhyata iti tadayukta syāt ucyate nātra napusakabhābārtha kṛta lyuṭsahacaritatva ki tarhi lyuṭā saha vidhānam napusake bhāve kto lyuṭ ca iti yāvat anunyāsakārasya tvayamabhiprāyaḥ ktalyuḍityatra lyuḍapi bhāvavihita eva gṛhyate tumunā sāhacaryāt ubhayopādāna tu spaṣṭārtham etacca tvayāpi vācyam yataḥ sāmānyagrahanapakṣepi ktagrahaṇamanarthakameva yathā karaṇādhikaraṇayorlyuṭā vāsarūpavidherabhāvadacpratyayo nāstītyuktam tathā bhāvalyuṭāpi saha vāsarūpavidherabhāvād ñagha nāstītyato hāsamiti na bhaviṣyati na ca vaktavya grahaṇopādānāt karaṇādhikaranalyuṭaiva vāsarūpavidherabhāva iti eva hi vijñāyamāne prayojanābhāyāt nanvidamasti prayojana sakarmakebhyo bhāve kto nāstīti kāramiti yathā syāt sāmanyalyuḍgrahaṇe tu kāramiti na syāt lyuṭā ghaño bhādhanāt ucyate na hi jñāpakādaniṣṭa kriyate jñāpakādācāryeṇeṣṭasūcanāt ata eva nātrobhayorupādānāt sāmānyavihitaḥ ktī gṛhyate tadeva karaṇe lyuṭā vāsarūpavidhināstyevācpratyayaḥ na cāsminvyākhyāne saptadaśa pratyayā iti vṛttigranthosaṅgataḥ syāt padasaskārapakṣe pratyayaśabda vyutpādyottarakāla parimāṇākhyāpratīteḥ ghapratyayena vā saptadaśa pratyayā iti bhaviṣyati atha vā pratyaya iti sūtrasādhane kāyabādhāpakṣeckārya lyuṭśāstreṇa bādhyate lyuṭśāstra ca śāstrabādhapakṣe ghaśāstreṇa bādhitam pratyayapravṛttau tvantaraṅgatvādac pratyayaḥ acpravṛttau lyuṇ nāsti lyuṭśāstrasya ghaśāstreṇa prāgeva bādhitatvāt eva ca na cakrakamiti etasyāḥ prāmāṇa vāsarūpostriyām ityatra vāgrahaṇasya vyavasthitavibhāṣāvijñāna nyāsakāreṇoktam jayādityena ta praiṣātisarga ityatra kṛtyagrahaṇamuktam ke cidvibhāsāgreprathamapūrveṣu ityatra vibhāṣāgrahaṇādityāhuḥ   sāpratikābhāve bhūtaprvagatiḥ   varttamānābhāve bhūtapūrvasyāśrayaṇa bhavati yathā vṛkṣairityatra bahuvacanae jhalyet ityettvepi kṛteto bhisa ais prapnoti taduktam kṛtepyettve bhautapūrvyādais tu nityastathā satīti  tathā āchi āyāma ityasmālliṭi dvirvacanebhyāsasya hrasvatve ca kṛte bhūtapūrvagatyā dvimātroyamākāra ityata ādeḥ iti taparakaraṇāddīrgho  na bhavati  tathā ca āñcha āñchatuḥ āñchuriti tasmānnuḍ dvihalaḥ iti nuḍāgamo na bhavati  na caiva pibateḥ sani dvirvacanebhyāsahrasvatve ca kṛte bhūtapūrvagatyā dvimātroyamākāra iti taparakaraṇāt pipāsatītyatrettva na prāpnotīti  vācyam  yaṅlugantātpāpaṭheḥ sani pāpaṭhiṣatītyatra sāpratikasya dvimātrasya vyāvṛttau taparakaraṇasya kṛtārthatvāt sāpratikābhābagrahaṇādve gaurityatra bhūtapūrvaiṅantādeṅhrasvātsabuddheḥ iti sabuddhilopo na bhavati he paṭo ityatra sāpratikasya vidyamānatvāt  jñāpaka cātrāco yat ityajgrahaṇa taddhi halantāṭṭahalorṇyat iti ṇyata vakṣyatīti pāriśeṣyādajantādeva yati siddhe dhitsya ditsyamityatrārddhadhātuka  iti viṣayasaptamyāmato lope kṛtejantabhūtapūrvādapi yathā syādityevamartha kriyate  etadarthatā ca tadā yadeha bhūtapūrvagatiḥ syāt   nānubandhakṛtamasārūpyam   anubandhakṛtamasarūpatva nāśrīyate tena goda iti kaviṣayeṇ na bhavati jñāpaka cātra dadātidadhātyovirbhāṣā iti ṇasya viṣaye vikalpena śavidhānam yadvyanubandhakṛtamasārūpya syāttadā vāsarūpavidhinaiva dāyo dada iti ṇaśābhyā siddha syāt nana yadyanubandhakṛtamapi vairūpya syāttadā vāsarūpostriyām ityatrārūpagrahaṇamanarthakam ataḥ sāmarthyātmavogagatamasārūpyamāśrayaṇīyam na ca kāṇoḥ prayogesārūpyamasti ato na bhaviṣyati vāsarūpa vidhiriti staccāpyuktam anubandhasārūpye vāsarūpavidhirmā vijñāyītyevamarthamasarūpagrahaṇa syāt igupagajñāprīkiraḥ kaḥ mūlavibhujādibhya upasakhyānamiti kaḥ pacādyac harateranudyamanec yadi hi syāt tadā nityopapadasamāsābhāvānmūlānā bhibhujośasya hara ityapi syāt asadetat mūlavibhujādibhya ityasyānarthakatvāt akārādanupapadātsopapado bhavati vipratiṣedheneti vacanācca astvantaraṅgatvānnirūpapadaḥ vāsarūpavidhinā sopapado bhaviṣyati eva tarhi kkibaṇośca śāstrakṛt śāstrakāra ityatra vāsarūpavidherabhāvāt samāveśo na syāt na kvipaḥ prayogosti aśrāvitvāt   iti śrīsīradevakṛtāyā paribhāṣāvṛttau pratyayapādaḥ   lakṣaṇapratipadoktayoḥ pratidoktasyaiva grahaṇa na tu lākṣaṇikasya   lakṣaṇa lākṣaṇikamupacārāt pratipadokta viśeṣeṇa pratipāditam tayormadhye pratipadoktasyaiva grahaṇa bhavati na tu lākṣaṇikasya khaṇḍato vyutpāditasya tadyathā īṅo ṇici krīṅjīnā ṇau ityāttve pukri ca kṛte āprūpe sampanne lyapi parato vibhāṣāpa ityanenāyādeśo na bhavati adhyāpya gata iti pratipadoktasya tvāperdhātorbhavati prāpya prāpayyeti tathā vaseḥ kvipi usiti uṣā caratītyatrārthe carati iti tṛtīyāsamarthāt ṭhaki kṛte usśabdasya lākṣaṇikatvādisusuktāntāt kaḥ iti ko na bhavati auṣikamiti pratipadoktospratyayāntādbhavati dhānuṣka iti nanveva sati hvāvāmaśca ityatra māgrahaṇena meṅo grahaṇa na syāt  na gāmādāgrahaṇaparibhāṣayā lākṣaṇikasyāpi bhavati na caiva mā māna ityasyāpi grahanamiti vācyam gāmādāgrahaṇaparibhāṣayā lugvikaranaparibhāṣābādhasyāniṣyamāṇatvāt yattu ghumāsthāgādi sūtre nyāsakāreṇa lugvikaraṇaparibhāṣāyā api bādha uktaḥ tatkeṣā cinmatamiti  yattu hvāvāmaśca ityatra maitreyeṇokta yeṣā darśana gāmādāgrahaṇeṣvaviśeṣa iti lakṣaṇapratipadoktaparibhāṣābādhanārthamida niranubandhakaparibhāṣābādhanārthamida  vā teṣā mā māna ityasya lumvikaraṇatvād grahana veditavyam  tatra yadukta lakṣaṇapratipadoktaparibhāṣābādhanārthamiti tadayuktam eva hi sānubandhakatvānmāṅmeṅoreva grahaṇa na syāt mā māna ityasyaiva niranubandhakasya syāt niranubandhakalugvikaraṇavicāre cāntaraṅgatvānniranubandhakaparibhāṣaiva pravattate anyathā vyākhyāne tvasterbhū iti śtipā nirddeśo vaicitryārtha iti yadukta tadasagata syāt asati śtipā nirddeśe lugvikaranaparibhāṣayā asukṣepaṇa ityasyaiva grahaṇaprasaṅgāt atha niranubandhakaparibhāṣāyāḥ pratyayaviṣayatvādiha dhātugrahaṇe tadvyāpārābhāvaḥ yathā na kavateryaṅi ityatra vyākhyāta nyāsakṛtā lumvikaraṇaparibhāṣayā kautairagrahaṇamiti tathāpi yadukta niranubandhakaparibhāṣābādhanārthamida ceti tadasaṅgata yato niranubandhakaparibhāṣābādhe lākṣaṇikatvānmeṅo grahaṇa na syāt māṅ māna ityasyaiva grahaṇa syāt ucyate neda rakṣitena vyavasthārthamuktam ki tarhi sarvathā lugvikaraṇaparibhāṣā gāmādāgrahaṇaparibhāṣayā na bādhyata iti pradarśanārtham tathāhi ida keṣā ciddarśana lakṣaṇaparibhāṣā bādhyate keṣā cidubhayaparibhāṣā na tu lugvikaranaparibhāṣāpīti yāvat etaccāyuktam ghumāsthāgādi sūtre nyāsakārena lugvikaraṇaparibhāṣābādhasyāpyuktatvāt eva tarhi niranubandhakaparibhāṣābādhanārtha veti nāya vāśabdaḥ pakṣāntare ki tarhi samuccaye tadayamarthaḥ gāmādāgrahaṇaparibhāṣā lakṣanaparibhāṣā bādhate niranubandhakaparibhāṣāmapīti samuccayepi vā śabdo dṛśyata eva yathā sagrahaśabdasya vyutpattau nyāsakṛtokta samyak samantādveti asyāyamarthaḥ samyaksamantācceti khaṇḍaśo vyutpanna hi lākṣaṇikamiti na sarvasamatam  tena vibhāṣā diksamāse bahuvrīhau ityatra sarvanāmavidhau pratipadoktasya diṅgāmānyantarāla iti bahuvrīhergrahaṇa dakṣiṇapūrvasyai dehīti na tvanekamanyapadārtha ityatrasya yā pūrvā sottarāsyonmugdhasya tasmai purvottarāyeti tathā ca ṝta iddhātoḥ ityatra ṝvarṇagrahaṇepīyamuktā jñāpaka cātra karttari bhuvaḥ khiṣṇuc khukañau ityatra khiṣṇuca ikārāditvam taduktam udāttatvādbhuvaḥ sidvamikārāditvamiṣṇucaḥ nañastu svarasiddhyarthamikārāditvamiṣyate anityā ceya paribhāṣā taccānityatva yāvatpurānipātayoḥ iti viśeṣaṇādavasitam tena dādhāghvadāp ityatra ghāgrahaṇena dheṭopi grahaṇa bhavati etattvapiditi karttavyedābiti yat kṛta tallakṣaṇaparibhāṣāyā abhāve heturiti tata eva siddham ida tu vaktavyam adhyāpayatītyatra lākṣaṇikasyākārasya pugiti   ekadeśavikṛtamananyavat   tenābhavadityatretaśca itīkāralope kṛte tiṅāśrayā sārvadhātukasajñā padasajñā ca tathā kariṣīṣṭetyatra syasicsīyuṭ iti soyuḍgrahaṇena sīmātrasya grahaṇam grahiṇotītyatra tvacaḥ parasmin ityādina syānivadbhāvenāpi hinumīnā iti ṇatva sidhyati nyāyasiddheyam tathāhi karṇacchedepi śvā śvaiva nāśvo nāpi garddabha iti jñāpakamapyāhuḥ āḍhyādi sūtrettvāviti pratiṣedhaḥ   kva cidvikṛtirapi prakṛti gṛhṇāti   tena nisamupavibhyo hvaḥ iti hvādhātorātmanepadamucyamāna prakṛtibhūtādapi bhavati nihvayate sahvayate jñāpakañcātra na vyo liṭi iti vikṛtasya vyeñitvasya nirddeśena vyeña āttvaniṣedhavidhānam atrāhuḥ na vyo liṭi ityatra nisamupavibhyo hvaḥ ityatra caikārāntāyā eva prakṛterupādānam vikṛtistu lakṣaṇagatenāttvena tasmāddādhāghvadāp ityatra dādhāgrahaṇe prakṛtibhūtayorapi deṅdhergrahaṇam praṇidayate praṇidhayatīti   bahuvrīhau tadguṇasavijñānamapi   guṇo viśeṣaṇamupalakṣaṇam citragavādiḥ sa guṇo yasyāsti sa tadguṇaḥ bahuvrīhisamāse viśeṣaṇasahitasyaiva śāstre savijñānam tadyathā sarvādīni sarvanāmānīti sarvasyāpi sajñā siddhyati sarvasmāyiti tasau matvarthe ityatra tūdaśvittvānityacopalakṣye matvarthe matupontarbhāvāttaddvāreṇaiva matupi sajñākārya siddham na tatreyamapekṣyate yathā kākebhyo dadhi rakṣyatāmityatropalakṣanāt kākādapi rakṣyate sūtrepiśabdāt kva cidatadguṇasavijñānamapi veditavyam tadukta siddha gadguṇāguṇābhyā pāṇineryathā loka iti loke hi tadguṇetadguṇe ca bahuvrīhirdṛśyate yathā lambakaramānaya citragumānayeti jñāpaka cātrāḍhyādi sūtre cvyartheṣvityutkācvāviti niṣedhavacanam yuktirapyatra vidyate tathāhi sarva ādiryeṣāmiti na viśvādayonyapadārthāḥ na hi teṣāmavayavaḥ sarvaśabdo bhavati tasyānārambhakatvāt na ca samīpārthe bahuvrīhirasti anabhidhānāt na hi lambakarṇa ityanena yasya samīpau lambau karṇau sobhidhīyate ki tarhi yasyāvayavau sa eva tasmāt samudāya evānyapadārthaḥ na ca samudāyasyaikatvāt sarvādīni ityatra bahuvacanānupapattiḥ udriktāvayavabhedaḥ samudāyonyapadārtha ityāśrayaṇāt ato bahuvacana yuktameva tadeva samudāye sarvaśabdontarbhūta iti tasyāpi sajñā bhavati   tācchīlikeṣu vāsarūpavidhirnāsti   tadyathālaṅkṛñ itīṣṇucālaṅkariṣṇurityeva bhavati na vāsarūpa vidhinālaṅkāraka iti jñāpaka cātra tṛjbādhanārtha nindahisādi sūtra vuño vidhānam yadi hi vāsarūpa vidhinā ṇvulādayastācchīlikeṣu bhaveyuḥ tadā ṇvultṛcau iti ṇvuli kṛte nindako hisaka ityādayaḥ siddhāḥ ki vuño vidhānena tatkṛta jñāpayati tācchīlikeṣu vasarūpa vidhinā tṛjādayo na bhavantīti tadeva tācchīlikānāmatācchīlikaurvāsurūpa vidhirnnāstīti jñāpitam idānī tu tācchīlikanā tācchīlikaireva vāsarūpa vidhirnnāstīti jñāpyate jucaṅkramyadanndramyasūgṛdhijvalaśucalaṣapatapada ityatra paderdhātīryujartha padagrahaṇamanarthakam anudāttetaśca halādeḥ ityanenaiva yu cā padana ityasya siddhatvāt eva tarhi laṣapatapada iti padyateryuco bādhaka ukañ syāt  na vāsarūpa vidhinā yujapi bhaviṣyati tadeva yujvidhāna jñāpayati tācchīlikanā tācchīlikairvāsarūpa vidhirnnāstīti tenālapūrvātkarotestṛnna bhavati alakattati prāyika caitatat sūdadīpadīkṣaśca iti dīpo yucpratiṣedhena jñāpitam yadi tācchīlikeṣu vāsarūpa vidhirnnāstyeva tadā namikampismyajasakamahisadīpo raḥ iti rapratyayenaiva viśeṣavihitena yuj bādhiṣyate ki pratiṣedhena tat kurvan jñāpayati kva cidasti samāveśa iti kamrā kamanā yavatiriti rayucoḥ samāveśaḥ siddhaḥ gantākhilaḥ gāmuka iti tṛjukañorvikatthī vikatthana iti ghinuṇyucoḥ samāveśaḥ siddhaḥ   iti paribhāṣāvṛttau karmaṇipādaḥ   purastādapavādā anantarān vidhīn bādhante nottarān   pūrvasthā apavādā anantarān samīpasthānevotsargān bādhante nottarān vyavahitārthotrottaraśabdaḥ tadyathā hvāvāmaśca ityapavādaḥ samīpamevānupasarge ka bādhate na vyavahita tācchīlikaṇini svargahvāyīti bādhyaviśeṣacintāyā caiṣā paribhāṣā pravarttate na samudāyāpekṣayetīko jhal ityatra nyāsakṛtoktam tena niṣṭhāyā seṭi ityanena ṇilopena yathā bhakṣitamityatreyaṅ bādhyate tathā kāritamityatrairanekācosayogapūrvasya iti yaṇādeśaśceti jñāpaka cātra parimāṇākhāyā sarvebhya ityatra sarvagrahanam taddhi dvau kārau trayaḥ kārā ityatrāpo bādhanārtham anyathā purastādapavādanyāyena samīpasyairac ityasyaiva bādhaka syāditi anantarasya vidhirvā bhavati pratiṣedho vetyetsvarūpayānayaiva ca paribhāṣayā votāpyoḥ ityatra sūtre nyāse yaduktam yadyatrāṅo nirddeśastadā vautāpyo iti prāpnoti pareṇa saha guṇe kṛte pūrveṇa saha vṛddhyā bhavitavyam sautratvādadoṣa iti tadupapadyate tathā hyomāṅośca ityanena pararūpatvena samīpabhūtamakaḥ savarṇe dīrghatva bādhyate na tu vṛddhireci ityapi  anyathā hyomāṅośca ityanena vṛddhidīrghayorapavādena pararūpatvena votāpyoḥ itinirddeśasya siddhatvānnirddeśādasya siddhirityayuktamukta syāt etaccāsamyak sarvaṇadīrghabādhane u omāṅośca iti pararūpavidhānavaiyarthyāt naitat achāchādanamityādau pararūpatvenānunāsikākāranivṛtteḥ prayojanatvāt anyathā savarnadīrghatvenātra pakṣenunāsikopyākāraḥ syāt tadevamomāṅośca ityatra yanmaitreyeṇoktam āṅa saha yatraikādeśo nāsti tatra pararūpatvena sarvanadīrghatvena viśeṣa ityekādeśa udāhriyate āūḍhā oḍhā adyoḍheti taccintyam  tadetadanantaroktanyāsasamarthanamayuktam tatra vṛttikārādibhiḥ pararūpatvasya sarvāpavādatvena vyākhyātatvāt ata evādyoḍhetyudāhṛta vṛttau iti paribhāṣāvṛttau bahulapādaḥ   nānubandhakṛtamanejantatvam   tena dādhā ghvadāp ityatra dādhāgrahaṇena deṅdheṭorapi grahaṇam anyathā gatepyanubandha upadeśa ejantatvābhāvāccetā stotetivadāttvābhāvāttayorgrahaṇa na syāt etaccāyuktam syasicsīyuṭtāsiṣu ityatrājgrahana kṛtvā yad graherupādana karoti tenopadeśāśrayakāryaviṣayenubandho nāśrīyata ityasya jñāpitatvāt yathā piṣlṛdhātau pranipeṣṭetyatra śeṣe vibhāṣā kakhādāvaṣanta upadeśe iti pratiṣedhāṇatva na bhavati tathātrāpyanubandhe gatepyejantāśrayeṇāttvena bhavitavyameva ida tūdāharaṇam adābiti dāpgrahaṇe daipopi ghusajñāpratiṣedhaḥ siddhaḥ avadāta mukhamiti bhāṣye punarddivādau dāp śodhana iti paṭhitavyamityuktam nanvetadyadi prayojana tadā dādhā ghvapiditi kriyatām eva hi daipopi pitvād ghusajñāpratiṣedhaḥ siddhyati lāghavañca bhavati nānubandhakṛtaparibhāṣāpi nāśrayitavyā bhavati ucyate dādhā dhvapiditi kṛte lakṣaṇaparibhāṣātra na pravarttata ityatrārthe pramāṇa na syāt adāviti tu kṛte yathā pratiṣedhe lākṣaṇikasyāpi daipo grahaṇam tathā vidhāvapi dādhāgrahaṇena lākṣaṇikasyāpi grahaṇamupapadyate tathā codīcā māṅo vyatīhāre ityatra rakṣitenokta jñāpakaphalamida dādhā ghvapidityanena yadyapi sidhyati tathāpi tathā nirddeśo na kṛta iti tatraiva pratipāditamiti  ki tvapāviti dvivacanena nirddeśe kṛtevidyamānaḥ pakāro yayostāvapāviti pratiṣedhe dābdaiporgrahaṇasāmarthyādvidhāvapi dādhāvapi dādhāgrahaṇe  lakṣanaparibhāṣātikramaḥ śakyata eva vyākhyātum  tathā tu na kṛta praṇidāpayatītryatrāpi puki kṛtepāviti pratiṣedhāśaṅkāprasaṅgāt apitāviti tu kṛte yadyapyetatparihriyate tathāpi tathā na kṛta vaicitryārthatvāt jñāpaka cātrodīcā māṅo vyatīhāre iti kṛtāttvasya nirddeśaḥ anejantatve hi sa na syāt na ca māṅ māna ityasyaiva nirddeśastasya vyatīhāre vṛttyasabhavāt   cānukṛṣṭa nottaratra   cakāreṇānukṛṣṭamuttaratra nābhisambadhyate tena vadaḥ supi kyap ca iti cakāreṇānukṛṣṭasya yato bhuvo bhāva ityatrānuvṛttirnna bhavati kyapastu bhavati brahmabhūyamiti yatra svaritatvenānuvṛttau siddhāyā cakāreṇānukarṣaṇa kriyate tatrāsyā vyāpāraḥ yatra tu pratiyogina dṛṣṭvā nivṛttau prāptāyā cakāreṇānuvarttana tatreya nopatiṣṭhate tenāntarāntareṇayukte ityatra dvitīyānuvarttate maitreyaḥ punaḥ sāmānyenaitā manyate yadāha iko jhal ityatra cānukṛṣṭatvādityapi siddhānta iti  jñāpaka cātrāvyayeyathābhipretākhyāne kṛñaḥ tkvāṇamūlau ityatra ṇamuladhikāreṇa ṇamulvacana yadi cānukṛṣṭamapyanuvarttate tadā tkvā cetyovocyate anityā ceyam taccānityatva prātipadikāntanumvibhaktiṣu ca iti cānukṛṣṭamapi vikalpa nivarttayitumekājuttarapadeṇa iti punargrahaṇādavasīyate   iti sambandhapādaḥ   iti tṛtīyodhyāyaḥ   madhyepavādāḥ pūrvān vidhīn bādhante nottarān   tadyathā kṛño hetutācchīlyānulomyeṣu iti pūrvamaṇa bādhayte vidyā yaśaskarī na para tācchīlikaṇini śrāddhakārīti evamiṇo yaṇ iti pūrvamiyaṅa bādhate na parau vṛddhiguṇau āyakamayanamiti  na saprasāraṇe saprasāraṇam ityatra saprasāraṇagrahaṇānuvṛttau yat saprasāraṇagrahaṇa tatsāmarthyāduttarasyāpi śvayuvamaghonāmataddhita  ityetasya pratiṣedho bhavati  yūnaḥ paśya yūnā yūnā iti  ata eva saprasāranagrahaṇasāmarthyāt saprasāraṇapratiṣedhe karttavyeca parasmin iti sthānivadbhāvopi na pravarttate sthānivatkṛta vyavadhāna  vā nāśrīyate  nanu tatra vyatho liṭi iti yatsaprasāraṇamavyadhāne prāpnoti tadbādhanārtha saprasāraṇagrahaṇa syādvivyatha iti naitat yadyetāvatprayojana syāttadā saprasāraṇagrahaṇamakṛtvā vyatha ityeva kuryāt vyathaśca saprasāraṇe saprasārana na bhavatīti siddha vivyatha iti vyatho liṭi ityatraiva vā vyatho yo liṭoti kuryāditi jñāpaka cātra bahuvrīherūdhaso ṅīṣ ityatra svaritatvāsañjana vṛttinyāsapratipāditam taddhyana upadhālopinonyatarasyām ityatra svaritatvādanuvarttate tenāna upadhālopinonyatarasyām iti paratvād bhaviṣyanta ṅīpa bādhitvā bahuvrīherūpadhaso ṅīṣ iti ṅīṣeva bhavati ghaṭodhnīti anyathā ṅoṣ madhyepavādatvātpūrvayoreva ḍāppratiṣedhayorbādhakaḥ syāt ṅīṣṅīpośca svare bhedaḥ svaropi bhedako bhavati yadāhuḥ tridhā śabdo bhidyate rūpatorthataḥ svarataśceti tathā ca taddhitā ityatra maitreyaḥ pratipāditavān yadi stryadhikārāt pūrvamida syād tadā dūṣaṇāntaram īhā ceṣṭeti yasyeti ceti lope kṛte ekādeśa udāttenodātta ityudātto na syāt atra codayanti  īhā ceṣṭetyatrākāralope kṛte yadyapyekādeśa udāttenodātta ityudāttatva nāsti tathāpyanudāttasya ca yatrodāttalopa ityanenodāttatva vidyata  eveti  na cānayorudāttayorviśeṣosti astītyucyate tathāhi  yadaikādeśa udāttenodātta ityanenāsiddhādhikārīyeṇodāttatva kriyate tadā pūrvatrāsiddham iti tasyāsiddhatvādudāttasvaritaparasya sannatara  ityanenekāraikārau sanatarau na bhavataḥ sannataronudāttatara ityarthaḥ  yadā tvanudāttasya ca yatrodāttalopa ityanena kriyate tadā tasya siddhatvādudāttasvaritaparasya sannatara sati sannataraḥ syāt ekādeśasvarasyāsiddhatvepyakārapratyayasyodāttatvamāśritya sannatareṇa bhavitavyameveti na vācyam yata ekādeśena pratyayasya nivarttitatvāt kutastasyādyudāttatvam asiddhatva tvekādeśasvarasya na tvekādeśasya nanvevamapyekādeśasvarontaraṅgasiddho vaktavya ityanenaikādeśasvarasya siddhatvāt sannatareṇa bhavitavyameva ucyate tatra hi parigaṇanamasti ayavāyāvaikādeśaśatṛsvaraikānudāttasarvānuḍhāttārtha iti nanvevamapi svaritaparatvāt sannatareṇa bhavitavyameva ekādeśasvarasyāsiddhatvādudāttānudāttayorekadeśa āntaratamyāt svaritaḥ naitat antaratamasvarasyodāttatvena bādhitatvāt atha tasyāsiddhatvāt kutastena bādheti cet  na parihṛtyāpavādaviṣayamutsargaḥ pravarttata iti svarita udāttaviṣaye na pravarttate nanvasiddhatvāt kutastasya viṣayoyamucyate ucyate asiddhatvena tatkāla udāttatvasya pravṛttirnirākriyate na tvaviṣayatva kriyate viṣaye ca pravarttamānopavāda utsarga bādhata eva dadatītyatrādādeśo yathā evañcātrāpi svaritasyodāttatvena bādhā karttavyā nanvevamapi sannatarotrānivāryya eva īhaceṣṭibhyā gurośca hala ityakārapratyaye kṛte ṭabutpatteḥ prāgeva sannatareṇa bhavitavyamantaraṅgatvāt tasmādboddhavyoya rakṣitaḥ boddhavyāśca vistarā eva rakṣitagranthā vidyante tathāhi ṅyāp sūtre ābanteṣvapi ḍāpcābantayoḥ pūrvoktāt kāraṇāditi tathā tatraiveha cenaḥ striyām itīnnantādbahudaṇḍinīkā ceti vibhāṣā kabvidhiriti tathā ṛnnebhyo ṅīp ityatra kartrī hartrīti gherṅiti iti na guṇaḥ supi ca ityanuvṛtteḥ supi ṅiti tadvidhānāditi na krīḍādibahuca ityatra tathā kroḍāśabdāt strīliṅgāt pratiṣedha uktastathā pulliṅgādbhavativyameveti lakṣyata iti   anantarasya vidhirvā bhavati pratiṣedho vā   vidhirvā prateṣedho vānantarasyaiva bhavati yathā vā cchandasi ityanena serhyapicca ityanantaramapittva vikalpyate na tu vyavahito hirādeśaḥ yuyuhi yuyohi tathā neṭi iti vṛddhipraṣedhonantarasyaiva vadavrajahalantasyācaḥ ityasya bhavati adevīditi na sici vṛddhernāpi mṛjervṛddhiḥ ityasya alāvīdamārjjīditi kva cittu svaritatvapratijñānasāmarthyādvyavahitasyāpi vidhiniṣedhau bhavataḥ yathā ṭiḍḍhāṇañ iti ḍāpā vyavahitasyāpi ṅīpo vidhiḥ tathā kālādhvanoratyantasayoge iti dvitīyā vyavahitāpi vidhīyate tathā na ṣaṭsvasrādibhya iti dvayorapi ṭāpṅīpoḥ pratiṣedhaḥ aya cārthaḥ prattyāsattinyāyalabdhaḥ padvyate jñāpakamapyāhuḥ sakhyāvyayādeḥ iti ṅībvacanam taddhi bahuvrīherūdhaso ṅīṣ iti ṅīṣā vyavahito ṅībiti punaḥ kriyate pratiṣedhopyanantarasyaiva bhavatītyatra na ktici dīrghaśca iti dīrghagrahaṇa jñāpakam tadapyanayā paribhāṣayā yantiḥ santirityatrānantarasyānudāttopadeśa ityasyaiva pratiṣedhaḥ syāt na vyavahitasya kkijhaloḥ kṅiti ityasyetyevamartha kriyata iti   akṛtavyuhāḥ pāṇinīyāḥ   kṛtamapi śāstra nivarttayanti   viśiṣṭa ūho niścayo vyūhaḥ viśeṣaṇākṛtaniścayāḥ pāṇinīyāḥ kṛtamapi lakṣaṇa vyabhicārayantītyarthaḥ tena papuṣaḥ paśyetyatra yadyapi papivasśabdācchas vihitastathāpyakṛtavyūhā iti vacanāt papāvas asiti sthite saprasāraṇa saprasāraṇāśraya ca kārya balīyo bhavatītīḍāgama bādhitvā saprasāraṇam tato valāditvābhāvādiṇ na bhavati atrahuḥ astviṭ usyapadāntāt iti pararūpatve siddha papuṣa iti etaccāyuktam usyapadāntāt itya trādityanuvṛtteḥ nanu tathāpīṭo yaṇādeśe kṛte bahiraṅgaparibhāṣayā saprasāraṇasyāsiddhatvādvali lopena siddham asāhitikatvādvali lopasyācoranānantaryyevidhānānnājanantarya ityatra nāsti na ca bahiraṅgaparibhāṣayā yaṇādeśa eva na prāpnotīti vācyam nājānantaryya iti vacanāt atrocyate antaraṅge vali lope karttavye bahiraṅgasya yaṇādeśasyāsiddhatvādyaṇeva nāsti kuto vali lopa iti bahiraṅgatva tu yaṇādeśasya sahitāpekṣatvāt ki tveva varttate varddhete ityatrāto ṅitaḥ iti bahiraṅgasyaikādeśasyāsiddhatvādvali lopo durghaṭaḥ anye tu prayojanamida nimittāpāyaparibhāṣayā siddhamityācakṣate na cāsiddhaparibhāṣayā nimittasadbhāvostīti vācyam  asiddhavadatrāmāt iti bhādhikārīyāyā paribhāṣāyā karmavyāyā bahiraṅgasya bhādhikārīyasya saprasāranasyāsiddhatvādaṅgavaikalyena paribhāṣāyā  vyāpārābhāvāt  nanu ca vyāśrayatvāt kathamasiddhavadatrābhāt ityasya vyāpāraḥ ucyate paribhāṣāyā yannimitta bahiraṅga saprasāraṇādi tasya yannimitta svādi tadvasoḥ saprasāraṇam ityasyāpi paramparayāpi yannimitta tadapi paribhāṣāyā nimittamāśrīyate bhādhikārīyakāryametadarthameva siddhādhikāra iṣyate atīstyeva samānanimittatvamiti avaśya caitat papuṣaḥ paśyetyādāvāto lopa iṭi ca iti lopārtha vyākhyeyam na cātrosyapadāntāt ityastitatkarttavyatāyā saprasāranasyāddhatvāt etaccāsamyak acorānantarye sahitādhikārīya usyapadāntāt iti karttavye nājānantarya ityanayā asiddhaparibhāsāpratiṣedhāt eva tarhyusyapadāntāt ityatra pratipadoktasyoso grahaṇe papuṣa ityatra lākṣaṇika usi pararūpatva nāsti ata evāsiddhavadatrābhāt ityatra nyāsakṛtokta pratipadoktasya hyustatra grahaṇamiti nanūsyapadāntāt ityatra lākṣaṇikaparibhāṣābādhāt sāmānyagrahaṇamuktam ucyate eva manyate lakṣaṇaparibhāṣābādho na karttavyaḥ prayojanābhāvāt astu lakṣaṇaparibhāṣā  na caiva papuṣaḥ paśyetyatra chāndasodāharaṇe sārvadhātukasajñāpakṣe āto lopa iṭi ca ityasyābhāllākṣaṇika usyusyapadāntāt ityasyābhāvādākāraśrutirdūṣanam śnābhyastayorāt ityākāralopaśchāndasatvāt yat evāsiddhaparibhāṣā nāsti tata evāpṛkta ekālpratyaya ityatra rakṣitenoktam vopṛktasyetyucyamāne na doṣo darvirityādāvapṛktatvepīti na vācyam tathā ca rājakṛtvānamācaṣṭe rājakṛtvayatītyatrāpi prasañga iti tathā janasanakhanakramagamo viṭ ityatra rakṣitenoktam ikāro verapṛktasya iti viśeṣaṇārtha iti asati tasmin paralokadṛśvayatītyatra ṇici ṭilope kṛte vakāralopaḥ syāt tasmādikāro viśeṣaṇārtha iti etadasiddha bahiraṅgamantaraṅga ityasya ṭilopasyādiddhavadatrābhāt ityasiddhatvenāpravarttanādupapadyate  yadyeva yuvoranākau ityatra yadukta rakṣitenāṅgasajñānimittayoryakāravakārayorgrahaṇenunāsikayoryakāravakārayorgrahaṇamanarthakameveti tadayuktam pūrvoktakrameṇa rājakṛtvayati paralokadṛśvayatītyatrādeśaprasaṅgāt ucyate bhādhikārātprāgya asiddhādhikāramāhuḥ tanmatena vāha uṭhaṭilopayorābhācchāstrīyatvannāsti atosiddhaparibhāṣāyā karttavyāyāmasiddhavadatrābhāt ityasyāpravṛttirityadoṣaḥ jñāpaka cātra samarthānā prathamādvā ityatra samarthagrahaṇam tathāhi yadyeṣā na syāt tadā samarthitasarvakāryāttaddhito yatha syādityemartha samarthagrahaṇamanarthaka syāt gorataddhitaluki ityatrātaddhitagrahana ke cidāhuḥ taddhi subluki mābhūdityevamartha kriyate rajagavīyatīti atra ca prāgeva niṣpannaṣṭac taduttarakāla kyaci subluki yadā pravṛttopi ṭac nivarttate tadā bhavati   iti sīradevakṛtāyā paribhāṣāvṛttau ṅyāppādaḥ niranubandhakagrahaṇe na sānubandhakasya   ekānubandhakagrahaṇe na dvyanubandhakasya   tena sadavyayatavya iti ṣaṣṭhīsamāsaniṣedhe niranubhandhakasyaiva tavyasya grahaṇa na tavyataḥ tathā diva ut ityatra divdhātoruttva na bhavati akṣadyūriti yato nāva ityatraikānubandhakasya yato grahaṇa na dvyanubandhakasya ṇyataḥ jñāpaka cātra vāmadevāḍ ḍyaḍḍyau iti ḍyaḍyatorḍitvam tacca na karttavyam yasyeti ca iti lopenaiva vāmadevyasya siddhatvāt tatkṛtamanayorastitva jñāpayati taduktam siddha yasyetilopena kimartha yayatau ḍitau grahaṇa mā tadarthe bhūdvāmadevyasya nañsvara iti ke citpratyayaviṣayā niranubandhakaparibhāṣāmāhuḥ etattu jṛvraścyoḥ tkvi ityatrānunyāsakāreṇoktam  tathā na ca kavateryaṅi ityatra nyāsakāreṇa lugvikaraṇaparibhāṣayādādikasya kauteragrahaṇe siddhe kavateriti śtipā nirddeśastaudādikasya  kuvartergrahaṇanirāsārtha iti yadukta tadupapadyate  anyathāntarañgāyā niranubandhakaparibhāṣāyā viṣaye lugvikaraṇaparibhāṣā kathamabhidhīyate antaraṅgatva tu niranubandhakaparibhāṣāyā upadeśa eva itsajñāpravarttanātlumvikaraṇaparibhāṣāyāstu bahiraṅgatvamuktarakāla vikaraṇaluko vidhānāt gaṇapāṭhaviśeṣaparijñānācca anye tu sāmānyena niranubandhakaparibhāṣāmāhuḥ ata evāsterbhūrityatra śtipā nirddeśo vaicitryārtha ukto nyākṛtā na tvasu kṣepeṇa ityasya nirāsārtha iti tannirāsasya niranubandhakaparibhāṣayā siddhatvāt iya ca ekānubandhakaparibhāṣā vasoḥ saprasāranam ityatra nopatiṣṭhate vasurugitkaranasāmarthyāt tena vasugrahaṇe kvasuvasvorubhayorgrahaṇa bhavati nanu cāsati vasurugittve vasaḥ saprasāraṇamityucyamāne vasa ācchādana ityasya varmmavasaḥ paśyetyatrāpi saprasāraṇa prāpnoti naitat vasa ācchādana ityasya sānubandhakatvāt na ca vasa nivāsa ityasya niranubandhakasya grahaṇamāśaṅkanīyam tatra kvibāśrayasyaiva saprasāraṇasya siddhatvāt  nanu vasīrugittva vidvānivācaratīti kvibantāt tkvāpratyaye vidvasitvetyatrodito vā iti vikalpeneḍāgamārtha kasmānna bhavati pratyayanubandho  hyeṣa samudāyānubandha eva  ucyate anabhidhānāt kvibatra nāstīti na tadarthamugittvamiti videḥ śaturvasuḥ ityatra rakṣitaḥ bhāṣye tu vasorapi dvyanubandhakatvamuktam tathā ca videḥ śaturvasuḥ ityatra bhāṣyam vasuriti dvisakārako nirddeśa iti tatraikaḥ śrutyarthoparastu dvyanubandhakatvārtha iti anye tvāhuḥ anubandhasya sthānivadbhāvena vasurapi naikānubandha iti naitat sthānivadbhāvena hyanubandhakāryāṇāmatideśo nanubandhasyaiva syādetadekānubandhakagrahaṇe na dvyanubandhakasyeti pratiṣedhānna hyatra ki cidekānubandhakamastīti vasoḥ saprasāraṇam ityatra rakṣitaḥ  yadyeva yadvyākhyātamauṅa āpaḥ ityatra rakṣitena na hi sthānivadbhāvenānubandho bhavatyapi tu kārya sthanivadbhāvaśāstrasya sthānikāryārthatvādanubandhāśca  kāryārthā na tu kāryāṇīti  tadayuktam yatastatrāpi pūrvoktakrameṇa dvyanubandhakapratiṣedhādauṭsthānikasyauṅo grahaṇa na syāt etannyāyānusāreṇaiva gaṅkuṭādisūtre kai gai śabda ityasyaiva grahaṇa syādityavadhāraṇa yujyate tathā hīṇsthāniko yo gādeśaḥ sthānivadbhāvena sānubandhaka iti tasyāpyagrahaṇam na caiva vācyameva hi gāṅādeśaṅakāro na karttavyaḥ sthānivadbhāveneṇdhātoriveṅādeśagāśabdasyāpyagrahaṇāt yatosati ṅakāre niranubandhakaparibhāṣāyā ihāvyāpāre pramāṇa na syāt  nanvasyā paribhāṣāyā satyāmutkarādibhyaśchaḥ naḍādīnā kuk ca iti naḍakīya ityādāveva niranubandhakatvādāyannādi sūtreṇeyādeśaḥ prāpnoti  na tu chaṇādau sānubandhakatvāttauttirīyamiti  ucyate āyannādi sūtre na pratyayagrahaṇamapi tu varṇagrahanam nanu naḍakīyādisiddhyartha naḍādīnā kuk ca ityanena kimartha chapratyaya kṛtvā kugāgamaḥ kriyate na naḍādibhyaḥ kuṭ cetyevocyeta eva hi naḍādibhya iti pañcamīnirddeśena lāghava bhavati takṣṇo nalopaśceti gaṇasūtra na karttavya bhavati padasajñayaiva lopasya siddhatvāt tathā ca tatra rakṣitaḥ parādau kuṭi kṛte takṣṇī nalopaśceti vacanamarthakam pratyayādestu vidhīyamāna īyādeśo na syāditi atrocyate nanu parādau kuṭi kṛte svādiṣu iti padasajñayāvagrahaḥ prāpnoti yathoktamekādākiniccāsahāya ityatrākinici karttavya ākinico vidhānamavagrahanirāsārthamiti ucyate ayasmayādipāṭhāt bhasajñā manyate maitreyaḥ nanu ceda na chandaḥ ucyate tatra pāṭhabalādbhāṣāyāmapi bhasajñā bhaviṣyati ata eva ṭāṅasiṅasāminātsyā ityatra nādeśe karttavye inādeśavidhānamatijarasineti siddhyartha nyāse vyākhyātam nanu tathāpīyādeśo na syāditi katha yāvatā pratyayopadeśakāla ekyodeśena bhavitavyam naitat gṛhītāgamā evāgamina upajāyanta iti kakārāditva syāditi nanu yadīyādeśena na bhavitavyam tadā kuḍāgamamakṛtvā chapratyayameva kuryāt naḍādibhyaścha iti tasmākuṭyapi kṛte īyādeśena bhavitavyam ucyate evahi pratipattigaurava syāt   tadanubandhakagrahaṇe nātadanubandhakasya   sa evānubandho yasya sa tadanubandhakaḥ tasya grahaṇenyasya tacchūnyasya grahaṇa na bhavati tena caṅi iti cakārānubandhe dvirvacana kriyamāṇa tacchūnyeṅi na bhavati adarśaditi anubandhoccāraṇasāmarthyalabdhoyamartha iti sonubandho yasya tasya grahaṇe sa yatra nāsti tasya grahaṇa na bhavatītyaparosyārtha ityāhuḥ tathā ca svādiṣvasarvanāmasthāne ityatrānayā prathamaikavacanagrahanamukta bhavati rakṣitena   iti sīradevakṛtāyā paribhāṣāvṛttau raktapādaḥ svaravidhau vyañjanamavidyamānavat   udāttādisvaravidhau vyañjanamavidyamānavat syāt tena tavyapratyayādestakārasyāvidyamanatvāt pratyayāderakārasyodāttatva bhavati karttavyamiti rājadṛṣadityatra halantatvepi samāsasya ca ityantodāttatvam udaśvitvānityatra hrasvanuḍbhyā matup ityanena takāreṇa vyavadhānāddhrasvātparo matub na bhavatīti tasyodāttatva na bhavati anayā tu paribhāṣayā prāpnoti tatrāsyā lakṣyasthityānāśrayaṇena vṛttikṛtā samāhitam samāsasya ityatra tu bhāṣyepyetaddoṣaparihārārtha halsvaraprāptāvityuktam atrocyate acaḥ svaravidhānāddhalsvaraprāptireva nāsti tatkimucyate halsvaraprāptāviti tatroktam uccairudātta ityādāvaca iti ṣaṣṭhīnirddiṣṭa nivṛttamiti codyañca yadatrāpadyate tattatraiva parihṛtamiti  jñāpaka cātrānudāttādeḥ ityasyāño bādhanārtha bilvādibhyoṇ iti vacana yadi vyañjana vidyamāna syāttadā bilvādayonudāttādayo na bhaveyuḥ anudāttasyājdharmatvāditi prāptireva nāsti mayaṭo bādhanārtha tu na vācyam mayaḍbādhanārthe hyasminbilvādibhyoṇ ityaṇgrahaṇamanarthaka syāt tasya hīda prayojanam pāṭaliputraśabdotra paṭhyate tasmādaṇ yathā syāt yathāprāptābhyanujñānenudāttādeśca ityañ mābhūditi añaśca halāditvādaprāptirityuktam imanijādīnāñca citkaranamasyā liṅgamupapadyate anyathemanico halantatvādetadantasya svarāprāpteścittvamanarthaka syāt udāharaṇāntara cāsyāḥ paurvārddhika dākṣiṇārddhikamityatra ṭhañi ñnityādinniratyam ityanena asyārthaḥ dikpūrva padādarddhaśabdāṭṭhañbhavati cakārādyacceti yadyeva pūrvapadagrahanamiha na kriyatādiśaṣṭhañityeva vaktavyam aya cārthaḥ diśa uttarasmādarddhaśabdāṭṭhañ bhavatīti  na diśaṣṭhañityucyamāne diśaḥ svarūpagrahaṇa syāt pūrvapadagrahaṇe tu kṛte digityarthagrahaṇam tarhi pūrvagrahanameva kriyatām ata evārthagrahaṇa bhaviṣyati  yathā parāvarādhamottamapūrvācca ityatra parāvarādhamottamebhya iti karttavye pūrvagrahaṇa parārddhyamityatra ṭhaño bhādhanārthamiti vṛttāvuktam naitat padagrahaṇe sati pūrvagrahaṇādarthagrahaṇe vyavasthāpite bahupūrvārddhyamiti bahupūrvādarddhaśabdādapi ṭhañ syāt atrāpi dikpūrvasyārddhaśabdasya vidyamanatvāt na hi pūrvagrahaṇenārthagrahaṇa bahupūrvādibhyaḥ pratyayasya nirākaraṇa cobhaya śakyate karttum padagrahaṇe tu kṛte pūrvādiśabdebhya eva bhavati tatraiva diśaḥ pūrvapadasya vidyamānatvāt bahucpūrvādarddha śabdāttu na bhavati tasyāpūrvapadatvāt tasmātpūrvagrahaṇa padagrahaṇa cobhayamapi karttavyamiti eva ca sati dikpūrvapadāṭṭhañ ityatra yanmaitreyeṇoktam yathā pūrvasūtre pūrvagrahaṇasya prayojana vyākhyātam tathātrāsatyapi padagrahaṇe pūrvagrahaṇādeva svarūpagrahaṇannirastamiti tanna śobhanam   yuṣmaṭpādaḥ samāptaḥ   kriyāviśeṣaṇānā karmatva napusakaliṅgatā ca   tadyathā mṛdu paṭhati śobhana pacati nanu kimartha napusakatva karmatva cobhayamāśrīyate na napusakatvamevāstu tata eva mṛdu pacatītyādi siddhyati satyam  ki tva sati karmatve mṛdvādīnā prathamāntatvāt sapūrvāyāḥ prathamāyā vibhāṣā ityanena grāme mṛdu te pacatītyādau vikalpena temayādividhayaḥ  syuḥ  dvitīyāntatve tu mṛdvādīnā temayādividhayo nityā bhavanti atha ki na bhavitavyameva grāme mṛdu te pacati grāme mṛdu tava pacatīti rūpadvayenabhavitavyamevānanvādeśesarva eva vānnāvādayonanvādeśe vibhāṣā vaktavyā iti vacanāt  anvādeśe tvatho grāme mṛdu te pacatītyeva nitya bhavati tadyadi mṛdvādīnā prathamāntatva syāt tadānvādeśepi sapūrvāyāḥ prathamāyā vibhāṣā  ityanena vikalpaḥ syāt  yathā atho grāme kambalaste svam atho grāme kambalastava svamiti tasmāt karmatva napusakatva cobhaya karttavyam aya cārtho nyāsiddha ityāhuḥ tathāhi mṛdu pacatītyatra pākakriyāyāḥ prārthanādhyavasānādikriyayā vyāpyatvāt karmatvam tathāhi kaścitphalamīpsuḥ phala paśyati etasyā etatphalamiti dṛṣṭvā prārthayate tatastā karttumadhyavasyati gamyamanā ca kriyā kārakāṇā nimittamiti gamyamānāyāḥ prārthanādikriyāyāḥ pākakriyā karma bhavatiatastadviśeṣana karmaiva kriyāyāścāsattvabhūtatvāttadviśeṣaṇa sāmānyena liṅgena napusakenaiva nirddeṣṭu yujyata iti nanu kriyānimittasya karmmatvamukta nimitta ca siddhasvabhāvam kriyā ca sādhyasvabhāvā tatkatha karmatva syāt tarhi tatpratyanupūrvamīpalomakūlam iti kriyāviśeṣaṇakarmadvitīyāntāṭṭhāmvidhāna jñāpayati sādhyasvabhāvāpi kriyā prārthanādhyavasānādikriyā prati sādhanatvenāśrīyate   iti paribhāṣāvṛttau ṭhakpādaḥ   iti caturthodhyāyaḥ   grahaṇavatā prātipadikena tadantavidhirnnāsti   vyapadeśivadbhāvoprātipadikena   grahaṇavatyuccāravatā prātipadikena tadantavidhiḥ pratiṣiddhyate tena naḍādibhyaḥ phak iti kevalādeva bhavati nāḍāyana iti na tadantāt sautranāḍiriti vyapadeśivadbhāvaśca prātipadikena na bhavati kratūkthādisūtrāntāṭṭhak itīhaiva bhavati sagrahasūtramadhīte sāgrahasūtrikaḥ vyapadeśivadbhāvena kevalānna bhavati sūtramadhīte sautra iti jñāpite ete paribhāṣe yenavidhiḥ iti sūtre bhāṣyakṛtā pūrvādiniḥ ityasyānantara sapūrvācca ityanena taduktam kimartha sapūrvādinirvidhīyate pūrvaśabdena prātipadike viśeṣite tadantavidhinā sapūrvādapi bhaviṣyati kevalācca vyapadeśivadbhāveneti nārthonena tat kṛta jñāpanārtham etacca jñāpayati ete paribhāṣe grahaṇavatetyādike sta iti  ata eva pratyayavidhau jñāpitatvādgrahanavatetyādiparibhāṣādvaya pratyayavidhiviṣayamākhyāya gostriyorupasarjanasya ityatra tadantavidhinā  gośabdāntagrahaṇa vyacakṣate  anye ca sāmānyena pratyayavidhau cāpratyayavidhau ca paribhāṣāmāhuḥ tathā ca śeṣo ghyasakhi iti pratiṣedhaḥ kevala eva na tadante atisakherāgacchatīti punaścaitayorbhāṣye pratyākhyānamuktam taduktam ādyāyāstāvatsiddha viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāva prati yatheṣṭatvādviśeṣaṇena hi tadantavidhirbhavati na viśeṣyeṇa tatra samāsavidhau dvitīyāśrita ityādau yatsupsupeti prakṛta na tacchritādibhirviśeṣyateapi tu tenaiva śritādayo viśeṣyante śritādibhiḥ subantairititena tadantavidhyabhāvānna bhavati kaṣṭa paramaśrita ityatra samāsaḥ  pratyayavidhau naḍādibhyaḥ phak ityatra yatprātipadikāditi prakṛta tenaiva naḍāḍhyo viśeṣyante naḍādibhyaḥ prātipadikebhya iti teneha na bhavati  sūtranaḍasyāpatya sautranāḍiriti  yatra tu gṛhyamāṇena prakṛta viśeṣyate tatra bhavatyeva tadantavidhiḥ yathopapada prakṛta bhayagrahaṇenāḍhyādibhiśca viśeṣyate atastadantavidhinābhayakaronāḍhya bhaviṣṇuritisvagrahaṇānuvṛttyā vyapadeśivadbhāvācca kevalepi bhavati bhayaṅkara ityāḍhyaṅkaraṇa iti ca kratṛvasthādisattrāntāṭṭhak ityatra tadantavidhinaiva tadantatve labdhentagrahaṇa kevalānmābhūdityevamartham anyathā svamityasyānuvṛtyā kevalādapi syāt ata eva vyapadeśivadbhāvo na pravarttate  ki tveva gokulamityatra svagrahaṇānuvṛttyā vyapadeśivadbhāvāccopasarjanahrasvatva prāpnoti tatra tadantagrahaṇasāmarthyādvyapadeśivadbhāvo  na bhavatīti bhāgavṛttikṛtā gostriyorupasarjanasya ityatra samāhitam  svagrahaṇānuvṛttiśca na sarveṣā matā   samāsapratyayavidhau tadantavidhiniṣedha ugidvarṇagrahaṇavarjam   tena śritādīnā subantaviśeṣaṇatvepi tadantavidherabhāvākaṣṭa paramaśrita ityatra samāso na bhavati tathā pratyayavidhau sautranāḍirityatra phagna bhavati ugidvarṇagrahaṇavarjamiti vacanāttaḍhantavidhinātibhavatīti dākṣiriti bhavati anyathā viṣṇuvācinośabdātsyāt yenavidhi sūtre vārttikamida paribhāṣārūpeṇa kaiścitpadyate siddha tu viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvayoryatheṣṭatvāt   itiparibhāṣāvṛttau dhānyapādaḥ samāptaḥ   svārthikāḥ prakṛtito liṅgavacanānyativarttantepi   tena kuṭira ityatra liṅgātikramaḥ apkalpamityatra ca liṅgavacanayorubhayorapi pacatorūpa pacantirūpamityatra vacanātikramaḥ apiśabdānnāpyativarttante kutsitośvośvaka iti jñāpaka cātra ṇacaḥ striyāmañ ityatra striyāmiti vacanam liṅgānatikrame hi striyamiti na karttavyam karmavyatihāre ṇac striyām iti ṇacaḥ striyāmeva vidhānāt striyāmañapi siddha iti etasyā udāharaṇāntaram dvipadikā dviśatiketi pustvanapusakatvayoratikramaḥ atra hi dvaudvau pādau dadāti dvedve śate dadātīti pādaśatasya sakhyādervīpsāyā vun lopaśca iti vunpratyayontyākāralopaśca atra codayanti nanu kimarthamanena vunvidhīyate kanneva vidhīyatām tenāpi hi dviśatiketi siddhyati eva ca sthūlādibhyaḥ prakāre kan iti kangrahaṇa karttavya na bhavati etadeva hyanuvarttiṣyate ucyate yadi kan vidhīyetāntyalope kṛte dviśatiketi na syāt tathā kani bhasajñābhāvāddvipadiketi bhasajñānibandhanaḥ pādaḥ pat iti padbhāvo na syāt athāstu padbhāvastathāpi dvipadiketi na syāt padbhāvasya halantatvād dvipatketi syāt eva ca yattatra rakṣitenoktam kanvidhānepi siddhyati dviśatiketi sthūlādibhyaḥ prakāre kan ityekatkarttavya na bhavati dvipadiketi tu bhasajñānimittapadādeśābhāvād rūpa ca na siddhyatīti tadayuktamkanpratyayentyalope ca kṛte dviśatiketyetadapi na siddhyati tatkathamucyate kanvidhānepi siddhyati dviśatiketi atha lopagrahaṇamapi na karttavya tarhi bhasajñānimittapadādeśābhāvād rūpa ca na siddhyatīti yadukta tadasaṅgata syāt tathāhi yathā bhasajñā nāsti tathā dakārāntaḥ pācchabdopi nāsti katha vā tadrūpañca na siddhyatītyucyate yāvatāntyalope kṛte padādeśe cābhyupagate satyantyo yokārastasyettve sati dvipadiketi siddhyatyeva ki cottaraphakkikāyā lopagrahaṇa pratyākhyātavyameva adhunā tatpratyākhyānamayuktam ucyate rūpa ca na siddhyatīti yadukta tadubhayatra veditavyam tatoyamarthaḥ dviśatiketi na siddhyati dvipadiketi ca na siddhyati anye tvāhuriha duravagamau maitreyābhiprāyaḥ na kevalamihaivāpi tvanyatrāpi tathāhi vibhaktipāde adhunā ityatra sūtre rakṣitenoktam yadyayamadhunā pratyayaḥ syāttadā pūrvasūtra evādhunā pratyaya vidadhyāt nādbhāvanipātanārthamida vaktavyam idama iś itīśādeśe kṛte yasyeti lope satyadhunetyasya siddhatvāt tasmādasāvanipātanārtha yatpṛthagyoga karoti tatonumīyate nāyamadhunāpratyayaḥtarhi dhunaiva sve ca viśeṣo vṛttikṛtobhipretaḥ bhāṣye punaradhunāpratyaya evāya yasmādādisūtre kathitaḥ strī adhuneti pratyudāharaṇenatathā tu yogavibhāgonarthakaḥ asminkāle vastunīti vivakṣāyāmikoci iti nummābhūditi   śatapādaḥ samāptaḥ   iti pañcamodhyāyaḥ   saprasāraṇa saprasāraṇāśraya ca kārya balīyo bhavati   tena juhāvayiṣatītyatra hvaḥ saprasāranam iti śācchāsāhvāvyā iti yuka badhitvā saprasāranam juhūṣatītyatrābhyastasya iti dvirvacanātprāk saprasāraṇamjuhuvaturitya trākāralopa bādhitvā saparmāranapūrvarūpatve eva bhavataḥ tenāci śnudhātu ityādinovaṅ sidhyati anyathāto lopa iṭi ca ityākāralope sati tasyāsiddhavadatrābhāt ityasiddhatvāduvaṅna syāt katha tarhi brahmaśabda upapade jināterddhātorātonupasarge ka iti ke kṛte brahmajya iti syāt yāvatatrāpi juhuvaturjuhavurityuvaṅādeśavadiyaṅā bhavitavyam na cātrairanekācosayogapūrvasya iti yaṇādeśo vācyaḥ aṅgasyakāctvāt tathā ca brahmajiya ityaniṣṭa rūpa syāt ucyate sarvatra saprasāraṇibhyo ḍo vaktavya iti ḍapratyayena bhavitavyamiti yathāhvaḥ prahva ityatroktam atha vā kva cideṣā na sarvatreti ata eva sahivahorodavarnasya ityatra nyāsakṛtoktam kva cideṣā na sarvatreti tena brahmajyaḥ āhvaḥ prahva iti kapratyaye saprasāraṇapūrvarūpa bādhitvā ikāralopastasyāsiddhatvādiyaṅuvaṅau na bhavataḥ tathā ceko yaṇaci iti kṛte siddha brahmajya ityādi jñāpaka cāsyā bhāṣye liṭyabhyāsasyobhayeṣām ityatrobhayeṣā vacanamuktam  taddhi vavraścetyādau halādiḥ śeṣaḥ bādhitvā saprasāraṇa yathā syādityevamartha kṛta tena kāryāntara bādhitvā saprasāraṇasya pravarttanādasyā  astitva gamayati  punaścāsyā bhāṣye pratyākhyānamuktam juhuvaturityādau pūrvavipratiṣedhena saprasāraṇasya saprasāraṇāśrayasya ca siddhiḥ  ki tu vyākhyānāt paribhāṣāśrayaṇameva laghviti nyāsakāreṇa punariya sahivahorodavarṇasya ityatrāvarṇagrahaṇena jñāpitā tasyaitat prayojanamūḍha  ūḍhavānityatra saprasāraṇe pūrvarūpatve cokārasyautva mābhūditi  etaccāprayojanam  dhatvaḍhatvaḍhalopesu saprasāraṇapūrvarūpatvābhyā paratvādakārasyautve kṛte saprasāraṇapūrvarūpatva ca kariṣyāma iti na ki cidaniṣṭamāpadyate tadevamavarṇagrahaṇamasyā jñāpakamiti atha juhūṣatītyatrādeśapratyayayoḥ iti katha mūrddhanyaḥ yāvatā sthānedvirvacanapakṣe hūso dvirvacane kṛte juhūsādeśasya śabdāntaratvāt prakṛtipratyayavibhāgo nāsti na ca mūrddhanyasyaiva dvirvacanam pūrvatrāsiddham ityasiddhatvāt pūrvatrāsiddhīyamadvirvacana iti tu prāyikam ubhau sābhyāsasya iti vacanāt ucyate tattvādhyavasāyena kāryakāraṇāt pratyayāśraya ṣatva bhavati tathaikāc sūtre rakṣitaḥ  tatrāya sādhāraṇaśca parihāraḥ sicprabhṛtīnā ṣopadeśasya sāmarthyāt stautiṇyoreva iti stautigrahaṇāt sico yaṅi iti pratiṣedhāccaiva jñāpyate  śrutyabhedāttattvādhyavasāyena sthāne dvirvacanepi kāryāṇi kriyante  anyathā kaḥ prasaṅgaḥ ṣatvasya syāditi atrocyate nanu katha sico yaṅi ityasya jñāpakatvamuktam yāvatopasargāt sunīti ityādinā ṣatve prāpte tanniṣedhārtha tat syāt paritosicyata iti etacca sico yaṅi ityatra vṛttāvuktam  upasargāt sunoti iti yā prāptiḥ sā padādilakṣanameva ṣatvapratiṣedhamanantaratvād bādhate na sico yaṅi iti tasmādaya pratiṣedhaḥ sarvatreti ucyate sātpadādyoḥ iti pratiṣedhe prāpta upasargādi sūtreṇa ṣatva vidhīyate sātpadādyoḥ ityanena cādeśapratyayayoḥ ityasyaiva pratiṣedhaḥ ādeśapratyayayoḥ ityanena ca ṣatvasyāprāptiḥ sakārasyānādeśatvāt naitat sthite tathāvidhosyārthaḥ idānī punaraprāptamevopasargādi sūtreṇa ṣatva vidhāsyate atastatpratiṣedhārthameva sico yaṅi iti syāt na ca vācya sātpadādyoḥ ityādeśapratyayayoḥ ityasyāpavādaḥ tatsāhacaryātsico yaṅi ityapyādeśalakṣaṇaṣatvāpavādaḥ yata ubhayasambhave sāhacaryamucyate aya cādeśalakṣanaṣatvāpavādo na sambhavatītyanupapanna sāhacaryam ucyate  sthānedvirvacanapakṣe parisesicyata ityatrāpi yakāravataḥ sicyabhāgasya dvirvacane sesicyādeśasya sijvyapadeśābhāvātkathamupasargādi sūtreṇa  sijdvārikā mūrddhanyasya prāptiryanniṣedhārtha sicoyaṅi iti syāt  atha vā yadyatra sicoyaṅi iti kriyatām  aya cārthaḥ yaṅpratyaya varjayitvopasargāt sicaḥ ṣatvamiti tataḥ parisesicyata iti siddhe yatsico yaṅi iti kṛta tadādeśapratyayayoḥ ityasyāpi  pratiṣedhārthamiti  etasminpāde omāṅośca ityatra raksite pūrvapakṣo bahulapāde purastādapavādaparibhāṣāyāmuktaḥ   ubhayata āśraye nāntādivat    ekaḥ pūrvaparayoḥ ityataḥ pūrvagrahaṇānuvṛtyāntādivacca ityanenaikādeśaḥ pūrvasya kārya pratyantavat parasya kārya pratyādivatkriyate tatra  yathā śakyeta vidhiḥ karttumiti pūrvasyāntavattvenāmū ityatrādasoserdādu do ma iti bhavati tathā parasyādivattvenāgnī vṛkṣāvityatra pragṛhyatve  bhavataḥ  yatra tvekādeśa ubhayamāśrayati pūrva para ca tatrobhayata āśraye nāntavattva nāpyādivattvamiti vākyārthaḥ tena vṛkṣamityatraikādeśasya pūrvagrahaṇenāgrahaṇānnaṅgasyākārāntatva paragaraṇenāgrahaṇānmakārasya na suptvamiti dīrghatvābhāvaḥ tathā prohyata ityatropasargāḍvrasva ūhateḥh iti na bhavati atreda na vaktavyam ekādeśasya pūrvagrahaṇena grahaṇe kṛte ekadeśavikṛtadvāreṇa makāramātrasya suptvamāśritya dīrghatvena bhavitavyamiti yadyatraikadeśaparibhāṣā syādubhayatāśrayaparibhāṣā nirviṣayā syāt iya ca paribhāṣāntādivacca ityatra bhāṣyakāreṇa paṭhitā tatrokto laukiko nyāyaḥ yathobhayostulyabalayorekaḥ preṣyo bhavati avirodhārthī ubhayorapi kāryena pravarttata iti   varṇāśraye vidhau nāntādivattvam   tena khaṭvābhirmālābhirityatra pūrva pratyantavattvābhāvādato bhisa es ityaisna bhavati taparakaraṇa tu somapābhirityatra kritārtham tathā hvayaterjuhāvetyatra saprasāraṇapūrvarūpasyānādivattvādāta au ṇala iti na bhavati tathā asyai aśvaḥ asyā aśva iti āṭaśca iti na vṛddhiḥ iya ca paribhāṣāntādivacca ityatra bhāṣye paṭhitā jñāpaka cāsyāḥ ṣatvatukorasiddha iti tugvidhāṣasiddhavacana kaiyaṭenoktam tathāhi yadyeṣā na syāttadādhītyetyatra savarṇadīrghasya paragrahaṇena grahaṇe kṛte hrasvāśrayastuk siddhastukyasiddhavacanamanarthaka syāt  nanvasyā satyā kṣīrapeṇetyatra pūrva pratyanantavattvenaikājuttarapadeṇa iti ṇatva na prāpnotyekājāśrayeṇa varṇāśrayatvāttatra pratiṣedha  eva yuktaḥ  śriyāmityatra para pratyādivattvābhāvādiyaṅna syāt yāveva pūrvaparau varṇāvāśrityaikādeśaḥ pravarttate tadvarṇāśrayentādivadbhāvo neṣyate atideśasya tatraiva vyāpārāttatraiva pratiṣedho yuktaḥ iha tvekādeśa eva kṛte yo varṇa ekājuttara ākāraśca tadāśrayau ṇatveyaṅvidhī na tau nivartyete tathā cāhuḥ ihādyantaśabdayoravayavavacanatvāttadavayavakaraṇesyātideśasya vyāpāro na tu tatkaraṇa iti tadeva khaṭvābhirityādau pūrva pratyantavattvepi tadekadeśatā labhyate na tu tadrūpateti tatkuta aisprasaṅga iti etadeva nyāsakṛtoktamatādrūpyoyamatideśa iti   ekācpādaḥ samāptaḥ   kṛdgrahaṇe gatikārakapūrvasyāpi grahaṇam   iya ca pratyayagrahaṇaparibhāṣāyā apavādaḥ yatra sajñayā svarūpeṇa vā kṛto grahana bhavati tatra gatikārakapūrvamapi gṛhyate na tu yataḥ pratyayastadādyeva tadyathā kṣepa iti ktāntena samāsaḥ sagatinā sakārakeṇa ca bhavati udakeviśīrṇamavataptekulasthitamiti aṇinuṇa itīnuṇantātsagateraṇ bhavati sārāviṇa iti jñāpaka cāsyā gatiranantara ityanantaragrahaṇam tena ktānta uttarapade pūrvasyānantarasya gatisvaro vidhīyate udbhatamavadhūtamiti na hi vyavahitasyābhyuddhūtamiti  tatra yadīya paribhāṣā na bhavet tadā pratyayagrahaṇaparibhāṣyaivoddhūtaśabde saghāte saktānte prāptireva nāstīti kimetannivṛttyarthenānantaragrahaṇena  tatkṛta jñāpayatyastīya paribhāṣeti  liṅgamātrañcedam kātyāyanabhāṣyakārābhyupagamādeva siddheyam anyathā kārakapūrvagrahaṇasya grahaṇe ki jñāpaka syāt  anayā paribhāṣayā kṛttaddhitasamāsāśca ityatrāpi kṛdgrahaṇe gatikārakapūrvasyāpi grahaṇa prāpnoti tatra yat samādhāna ca tadgatikārakopapadānā  kṛdbhiḥ samāsavacanamityasyā paribhāṣāyāmuktam  lakṣyavaśādiya na pravarttata ityapīti tena prajñāsukaraḥ kaṭa ityatra khityanavyayasya iti hrasvorurdviṣadajantasya iti ca mumna bhavati kūlamudraja itivat   samāsānto vidhiranityaḥ   tena bhuvāraṇyāśasādhṛtadhanuṣayāhūya tṛṇavaḍhityatra dhanuṣaśca ityanaṅna bhavati tathā bahvāmpi taḍāgānītyatra ṛkpūrabdhūḥ ityakāro na bhavati jñāpaka cāsyāḥ sphigapūtavīṇāñjodhvakukṣisīranāmanāma ca ityatrādhvagrahaṇam taddhyapācca ityatopādityanuvṛttāvapāduttarasyādhvanontodāttatva yathā syāditi kriyate yadi ca nityaḥ samāsāntaḥ syāttadopasargādadhvana iti samāsānteci kṛte cittvādevāntodāttatva siddhamiti tatrādhvagrahaṇa na kuryāt kṛta cāto jñāpayatyastīya paribhāṣeti tathā bhāṣye dvitribhyā pāddanmūrddhasu bahuvrīhau ityatra sūtrekritasamāsāntasya mūrddhaśabdasyopādāna liṅgam  nitye hi samāsānte yathā pāditi daditi ca pādasya lopohastyādibhya iti vayasi dantasya datṛ iti kṛtasamāsantau nirddiṣṭau tathā mūrddhaśabdopi  dvitribhyā ṣa mūrddhna iti kṛtasamāsānto nirddiṣṭaḥ syāt  tataśca mūrddheṣviti nirddeśaḥ syāttasmāttathā cākṛtasamāsāntanirddeśaḥ samāsāntavidheranityatva jñāpayati tena dvimūrddhā trimūrddhetyatrāpyudāttatva bhavati yataśca jñāpiteya paribhāṣā bhāṣye tato yaduktam yasmātpratyayavidhi sūtre bhāgavṛttikṛtā samāsānto vidhiranitya iti naiṣā paribhāṣā bhāṣye jñāpakābhāvāditi tadayuktam nanu lāghavārtha samāsāntanirdeśo na kṛtonyathā mūrddheṣviti gaurava syāt yadyeva mūrddhapāddatsviti kuryāt eva ca samāsāntakramo na laṅghito bhavatīti jñāpitam   bahuvrīhipādaḥ samāptaḥ   sannipātalakṣaṇo vidhiranimitta tadvighātasya   ānantaryalakṣaṇo vidhistadvighātasya nimittanna bhavati yasyānantaryeṇa yo vihitastadānantaryamasau na viruṇaddhītyarthaḥ tadyathā grāmaṇi brāhmaṇakulamityatra hrasvatve kṛte tugna bhavati naitatprayojanam asiddha bahiraṅgamantaraṅga ityanenaiva siddhatvāt vṛttau paddhatāvityatra tarhyacca gheḥ ityadādeśe kṛte ṭab mābhūditi prayojanam etadapi na adādeśasya taparatvāt tasyaitatprayojana vāmanenokta ṭāb mābhūditi ida tarhi prayojanam śatāni sahasrāṇīti vibhaktisanipātena numi kṛte tasya vibhaktiluka pratyanimittatvāt ṣṇāntā ṣaṭ iti ṣaṭsajñā na bhavati yadi syātṣaḍbhyo luk iti luksyāt tathā kumbhakārebhya ityatraitve kṛte kṛnmejanta iti na bhavati iya ca paribhāṣā kṛnmejanta ityatra bhāṣyakāreṇa paṭhitā jñāpakamasyā na tisṛcatasṛ iti dīrghapratiṣedhavacanam  taddhi satyāmasyā vibhaktinimittayostricaturoḥ striyā tisṛcatasṛ iti ṛkārāntaorvyavadhānakāriṇa ṅīpa pratyanimittatvāddīrghaprāptau pratiṣedhavacanamupapadyate anyathā tu ṅīpā vyavahitatvānnāmi dīrghatvāprāpteḥ pratiṣedhavacanamanarthaka syāt ṅīpaśca dīrghādīrghābhyāmaviśeṣāt anityā ceya kaṣṭāya kramaṇa iti nirddeśekārāntanimitte ṅerya iti ye kṛte yādau supi ca iti dīrghakaraṇādāhuḥ tena dākṣirityatra yasya iti lopaḥ siddhyati tathā yā sā ityatra ṭāppratyayaḥ nanu katha kaṣṭāya iti jñāpaka yāvatāto dīrgho yañīti yakāreṇa pratyāhārasāmarthyāt kaṣṭāya ityatra supi ca ipi dīrghatva siddhyati ucyate  pvādīnā hrasva ityatrāgaṇāntāḥ pvādaya iti darśane jānātītyatra jñājanorjā iti jādeśe kṛte hrasvatva prāpnoti tanmābhūdityevamartha dīrghāntādeśavidhānamuktam anyathā yadi jānātītyatrapvādīnā hrasva iti hrasvatvena bhavitavyam tadā hrasvameva kriyāt jñājanorja iti nanu jayata ityatra dīrghaśrutyartha dīrghāntajādeśavidhāna syāt naitat jabhāvepi kṛteto dīrgho yañi iti dīrghatvamiti na śakyate vaktum yadi punarāgaṇāntāḥ pvādayo na bhavantīti darśanam tadā jānātītyatra pvādīnām iti nāsti aṅgavṛttaparibhāṣayā vā hrasvābhāvobhidhīyate kṛte vā hrasvatve tu punarato dīrgho yaṅi iti dīrghatvam tadā yakāreṇa pratyāhāragrahaṇasāmarthyād dīrghatva śakyata eva vaktumiti nānityatve jñāpakam anityatve tvetadeva jñāpakam nalopaḥ supsvarasajñātugvidhiṣu kṛti iti tuggrahaṇam yadīya nityā syāt tadā vṛtrahabhyāmityatrānayaiva tag na bhaviṣyatīti tuggrahanamanarthakam   aninasmangrahaṇānyarthavatā cānarthakena ca tadantavidhi prayojayanti   tenāllopona iti yathā sārthakasya bhavati rājño rājñeti tathā nirarthakasya dadhno dadhneti tathenhanpūṣāryamṇā śau iti yathā bahudaṇḍīni brāhmaṇakulānītyatra bhavati tathā bahuvāgmīnītyatrāpi syāt tathātvasantasya cādhātoḥ iti yathā supayā iti tathā nirgatastato nistatā ityatrāpi bhavati tṛntṛcorbhedenopādānādāhuḥ tṛntṛcorbhedenopādānamarvaṇastrasāvanaña ityarvādeśatṛśabdaparihārārtham yadi tvarthavarparibhāṣā nityā syāttardārthavatparibhāṣayaivārvādeśasya tṛśabdasya nirāse siddhe syāt yato nityatvānnumi kṛte upadhāyā vihitatvāddīrthatva na bhaviṣyati ucyate vā ṣapūrvasya nigama ityataḥ pūrvagrahaṇānuvṛtternumaḥ prāg dīrghatvameva bhaviṣyatīti manyate etaccāvaśya vaktavyam anyathā bahvāmpi taḍāgānītyatrāpi numi kṛte dīrghatva na syāt anyastvāha tṛntṛcorbhedenopādāna sāmānyepi nirddeśe kvacidviśeṣo gṛhyata iti jñāpanārtham tena na kopadhāyā ityatra sāmānyoktāvapi vidyamānatvamiti eva ca vidherabhāvādasavarṇagrahaṇamanarthakameva ucyate nātra sthānivadbhāvostyādiṣṭādacaḥ pūrvatvādabhyāsasya tathāhi paratvādguṇe kṛte dvirvacaneci iti sthānivadbhāvād dvirvacanam dvirvacane kṛte sthānivadbhāvavidhau dvirvacana evetyavadhāraṇādguṇaḥ pūrvarūpeṇāvatiṣṭhate na punardvirvacanāduttarakāla punaḥ kriyate tenācaḥ parasmin itīyaṅuvaṅoḥ karttavyayoḥ sthānivadbhāvo na hyanādiṣṭādacaḥ purvastasya vidhi prati sthānivat   yo hyacaḥ parasmin iti sthānivadbhāvaḥ sonādiṣṭādacaḥ pūrvasya kārye bhavati tena paṭayatītyatra ṭāśabdākārādanādiṣṭādacaḥ pūrvo yaḥ iti sthānivadbhāvānna dīrgha iti tadupapadyate  aya cārthoaḥ parasminpūrvavidhāvityasyārthaḥ paribhāṣārūpeṇa paṭhyate tatrājapekṣamādeśāpekṣa nimittāpekṣa vā pūrvatvamāśrīyata ityuktam tatra yadājapekṣa pūrvatva tadāyamarthaḥ ajādeśaḥ paranimittakaḥ pūrvasya vidhau sthānivat kutaḥ pūrvasya vidhau sthānivattvamacaḥ tadevamajaprekṣapūrvatvamasyā mūlam jñāpaka cāhuḥ abhyāsasyāvarṇa prakṛtigrahaṇe yaṅlugantasyāpi grahaṇam   tena vido laṭo vā iti ṇalādyādeśavikalpo yaṅlugantasyāpi bhavati veveda vevidatuḥ veviduḥ vevetti vevittaḥ vevidatīti nyāyasiddhatvamasyā niṣṭhā śīṅādi sūtre nyāsakṛtā darśitam tathāhi sthānedvirvacanapakṣe sthānivadbhāvātprakṛtivyapadeśaḥ dviḥ prayoge ca sa eva dvirāvarttyata iti yukta prakṛtigrahaṇe yaṅlugantasyāpi grahaṇamiti jñāpakamapyāhuḥ ūdupadhāyā goha ityatropadhāgrahaṇam ūdorgoha iti lāghavārtha vaktavye yadupadhāgrahaṇa karoti tadyaṅluki jogṛhatītyatra yobhāsasyaukārastasya mābhūdityevamartha kriyate etacca tadā syāt yadi prakṛtigrahaṇe yaṅlugantasyāpi grahaṇa bhavatīti nanu cottarārthamupadhāgrahaṇa gamahanajanakhanaghasām iti anyathālontyasya lopaḥ syāt ucyate jñāpakavādino mate tatrāta iti nīstha prtipādayitavyaḥ śtipā nirddeśe caiṣā nopatiṣṭhate tathā ca smṛtiḥ śtipā śapānubandhena nirddiṣṭa yadgaṇena ca yaccaikājgrahaṇa tatra pañcaitāni na yaṅluki śtipā nirddeśa indhibhavatibhyā ca iti śapā bharajñapisanām ityatra bhara iti anubandhena śīṅo ruṭ iti gaṇena vatatitanotyādīnām iti ekājgrahaṇena ekāca upadeśenudāttāt iti śryukaḥ kiti itīṭpratiṣedhaḥ atra śloke ki ciditi śeṣaḥ yatrakājgrahaṇena dhāturviśeṣyate
