samprasāraṇasyāsiddhatvādvalakṣaṇo vasvekājādbhasām itīṇ na bhavati atra cāsyāḥ pravarttanābhāva upāyāntaramakṛtavyūhā ityatroktam   nājānantarye bahiṣṭvapraklṛtptiḥ   pūrvāpavādoya yogaḥ acorānantarye bahiraṅgaparibhāṣā nāsti tena bahava ityādāvecoyavāyāva iti bhavati tathākṣadyūrityatreko yaṇaci iti yūno maghona ityatrākaḥ savarṇādguṇau yadyeva pacāvedamityatrāpyeta aiprāpnoti atrāpyacorānantarye bahiraṅgasyādguṇasya pravṛttatvād siddha bahiraṅgamantaraṅga ityasyāḥ pratiṣedho yuktaḥ naitat acorānantarye sati yatrobhayamantaraṅga bahiraṅgañca tatreya pratiṣidhyate yathā bahavokṣadyūriti tathāhyatra bahiraṅge pravṛtte vidyamāna eva guṇa ūṭhi vāntaraṅgāvayaṇādeśau karttavyatayā vidyete pacāvedamityatra bahiraṅga ekādeśe kṛtecorānantarya nivṛttamityacorānantarye dvaya na vidyate tatkathamasyāḥ pratiṣedhaḥ yadyevamadhītya pretyetyatrāpyekādeśe kṛtecorānantarye dvayannāsti katha tadā ṣatvatukorasiddha ityasya jñāpakatopapattiḥ tathāhyatra pūrva dhāturupasargeṇa yujyata ityatra darśane dīrghāduttarakālamantaraṅge tuki karttavyecorānantaryannasti eva tarhi pūrva dhātuḥ sādhanena yujyata ityasmin darśanedhītya pretyetyatra nājānantarya ityucyate etaddarśane hyekādeśāt prāg lyapi kṛtecorānantaryentaraṅga bahiraṅga ca iya vidyata eva na cāsmin darśanentaraṅgatvāttuki kṛte ṣatvatukorasiddha ityasyānarthakyam yathāntaraṅgatva tukastathā nityatva dīrghasyatadetayornnityāntaraṅgayoḥ paratvāddīrghatva syāt atha vā pūrva dhāturupasargeṇa yujyate ityatrāpyakṛtavyūhā iti pravibhajyānvākhyānecorānantaryamasti ki ca ṣatvatukīrasiddha ityatra dhātostannimittasyaiva ityatra nyāsakṛtā vyākhyātam sahitādhikārīye kārye karttavyesiddha bahiraṅgamantaraṅga iti nājānantarya ityanayā bādhyate eta ai itīda prakaraṇāntaravihita kāryamiti kutastatra karttavye pratiṣedhe ucyate etadeva cchvoḥ śūḍanunāsike ca ityatra maitreyeṇoktam acorānantarye yattad dvaya prāpnotyantaraṅga bahiraṅga ca tatreya pratiṣidhyateiha tu kṛta eva bahiraṅgecorānantarye ca nivṛttentaraṅga prāpnotīti kutastasyāḥ pratiṣedha ityādinā granthena asyāyamarthaḥ astītyadhyāhāryam tadayamarthaḥ  acorānantarye yatra dvayamasti bahiraṅga pravṛttamantaraṅga prāpnotyantaraṅga pravṛtta bahiraṅga vā tatra bahiraṅgaparibhāṣā pratiṣidhyata  iti  jñāpaka cātra ṣatvatukorasiddha iti tukyekādeśasyāsiddhavacanam  yadyacorānantaryepi bahiraṅgasyāsiddhatva syāttadādhītyetyādāvantaraṅge tuki karttavye padadvayāśritasya savarṇadīrghasyāsiddha bahiraṅgamantaraṅga  ityata evāsiddhatvādasiddhavacanamanarthaka syāt anayā cāntaraṅgaparibhāṣā na bādhyata ityantaraṅgaparibhāṣāmuktam   sajñāpūrvako vidhiranityaḥ   tena dhāma svāyambhuva yayurityatraurguṇa ityasyābhāvāduvaṅ siddhyati tathā jyogiṣamityatrāṇyādivṛddhirna bhavati pañcabāṇaḥ kṣiṇotītyatra na guṇaḥ udaśvitvānityatra śvayateḥ kvipi na samprasāraṇam jñāpaka cātra oroditi karttavye orguṇa iti guṇagrahaṇamtathoto vṛddhirluki hali ityatra auditi karttavye vṛddhigrahaṇam tena stuyādityatra vṛddhirna bhavati  eva ca kṅiti ca ityatrācinavamasunavamitisiddhyartha vṛttau yadukta yāsuṭo ṅidvacana jñāpaka lakārāśraya ṅittvamādeśānā na bhavatīti  tadupapadyate  anyathā yāsuṭo ṅidvacana stuyādityatrāniglakṣaṇavṛddhipratiṣedhārtha syāttatkuto jñāpakam nanu tathāpyasya jñāpakatvamayukta vinuyurityādau jusi ca iti pratiṣedhārthatvāt etaccāyuktam yataḥ satyapi ṅittve bhavitavyamevātra jusi ca iti guṇenakṅidviṣaya eva tasyārambhāt  na yena nāprāptinyāyena sārvadhātukamapit ityanena yan ṅittva tadevānena bādhyate na yāsuḍāśritamapi ucyate yadyetāvatprayojana syāt skasyāci ityatocītyanuvarttyājādau jusi guṇo vidheya iti yāsuṭo ṅittva jñāpakameva apiḥ padārthasambhāvanā ityatra stuyādityatra ṅicca pinna bhavatīti vacanādrakṣitena vṛddhyabho vyākhyātaḥ stuyādityakṛtsārvadhātukayoḥ iti na dīrghaḥ sārvadhātukayakāratvāt nanu cācinavamityādisiddhyartha jñāpakamabhidhīyate yāvatā picca ṅinna bhavatyanena ṅittvābhāvādguṇaḥ siddha eva ucyate bhāṣyamatamida na sūtrakṛtaḥ ata eva serhyapicca ityatra nyāsa uktam serhiṅiditi kriyamāṇe sthānivadbhāvena pittva syāditi anyathā tatrāpi ṅicca pinna bhavatīti kaḥ prasaṅgaḥ pittvasya syāditi nanu yadi sūtrakārasyānapekṣitamida ṅicca pinna bhavatīti tathā brūtādbhavānityatra pittvasya sthānivadbhāvād bruva īṭ itīṭ syāt ucyate satyapi sambhave bādhana bhavatīti tātaṅo ṅittvena tipaḥ pittva bādhanīyam eva bhindyādityatrāpi tipaḥ pittvena liṅo ṅittvasya bādhitatvāt   sanniyogaśiṣṭānāmanyatarāpāye ubyorapyapāyaḥ   tadyathā  dhīvarītyādau ṅīpsanniyogaśiṣṭo vano ra ca iti rephādeśaḥ pañcadhīvetyādau pañcabhirddhīvarībhiḥ krītetyārhīyasya ṭhakodhyarddhadvigorlugasajñāyām  iti luki kṛte luktaddhitaluki iti ṅīpo nivṛttau rephasyāpi nivṛttiḥ  ayāḥ paribhāṣāyāśchedādibhyo nityam ityatra bhāṣyakāreṇa nyāyasiddhatvamuktam taduktam laukika evāya nyāyaḥ sanniyogaśiṣṭānāmanyatarāpāye ubhayorapyapāyaḥ tadyathā devadattayajñadattābhyāmida karttavyamityukte devadattāpāye yajñadattopi na karotīti jñāpakamapyasyā bhāṣyakāreṇabilvakādibhyaśchasya luk ityatra vyākhyātam tatra hyukta vilvakādibhya iti kukā nirddeśaḥ kuk cāya naḍādīnā kukca iti chapratyayasaniyuktastaśca bilvādibhyaḥ paraścha eva sambhavatīti bilvakādibhyo lugityucyamāne bhasañjñānimittapratyaye  chasyaiva lugbhaviṣyati ki chagrahaṇena tatkṛta chasyaiva kevalasya lugyathā syāt  anyathā sanniyogaparibhāṣayā kukopi nivṛttiḥ syādityevarmartham eva cāsyāḥ paribhāṣāyā astitve jñāpakam atrocyate nanu yadi bilvakādibhyo lugityucyate sāmānyena pratyayamātrasya luksyāt tathā ca bilvakādityatra supopi luk syāt ucyate halastaddhitasya ityasmāttaddhitagrahaṇānuvṛtterna bhaviṣyati nanvevamapi bilvakasyāvayavo vikāro vā bailvaka ityatra kopadhācca ityasyāṇo luk prāpnoti eva tarhyāpatyasya ca taddhitenāti ityatastaddhita ityanuvṛttestaddhitasya bhasajñasya taddhite parato luk evamapi bilvake bhavī bailvako vailvakasyeda bailvakīyamityatra prāpnoti naitat bilvakādibhyo yo vihitastasmin lugucyate na cātra bilvakāccho vihitopi tu bailvakāditi anityā ceyam taccānityatva bhyasyāḍhe taddhita ityaḍha iti puvadbhāvapratiṣedhena jñāpitam tatra hyaḍha iti kimityutkvā śyaineyo rauhiṇeya iti prtyudāhṛtam yadi ceya nityā syāt tadā yasyeti ca iti lope kṛte sanniyogaparibhāṣayā nakārasyāpi nivṛttiḥ syāt tataśca puvadbhāveviśeṣādaḍha iti pratiṣedhonarthakaḥ syāt nanu kathamanarthako yāvatā lope satyacaḥ parasmin iti sthānivadbhāvena pratyayalakṣaṇenāsiddha paribhāṣayā vā ṅīsanniyogo vidyata eva eva ca sati sanniyogaparibhāṣāyā anupasthānānnakārādeśo na nivarttate ucyate sthānivadbhāvādinā kārya kriyate na tu luptavarṇasannidhāna na caiva sanniyogaparibhāṣāyā anupasthānam apāyamātre tatpravarttanāt jñāpakamapyasyāstādṛśameva anyathā chasya lukyapi kṛte kuko nivṛttirna prāpnoti pratyayalakṣaṇādinā tasya vidyamānatvāt   tācchīlike ṇepyaṇkṛta kārya bhavati   aṇā kṛta kāryamaṇkṛtam taṇapratyayepi bhavati tena cūrā śīlamasyā iti chatrāditvāṇapratyayāntādapi ṅībhavati caurī tāpasī tācchīlike iti kim śīlikāmibhikṣyācaribhyo ṇo vaktavyaḥ māsaśīlā māsabhikṣā prajñāśraddhārcāvṛttibhyoṇaḥ prājñā brāhmaṇīti atrāṇkṛta ṅīb na bhavati kārmastāchīlya ityatra jñāpiteyam tatra karmaśabdāttacchīlamityanuvarttamāne chatrāditvāṇapratyaye kārma iti nipātyate atrocyate tastaddhita iti ṭilopena kārma iti siddhe ṭilopārtha nipātanamayuktam na cānniti prakṛtibhāvostiaṇi tasya vidhānāt eva tarhyetaj jñāpayatyastīya paribhāṣeti atrocyate yadi tācchīlikepyaṇkṛta kārya bhavatīti kimartha tarhi tācchīlikeṣvaṇpratyaya eva na vidhīyate eva ca jñāpaka karttavya na bhavati ucyate vaicitryārtha na kṛtam   dhātoḥ kāryamucyamāna tatpratyaya eva bhavati   dhātoryatkāryamucyate taddhātupratyaya eva bhavati tena sṛjidṛśorjhalyamakiti ityam rajjusṛgbhyāmityatra kvibantānā satyapi dhātutve supi prātipadikapratyaye na bhavati tathāci vibhāṣā iti girau gira ityatra na bhavati tathodakamagbhyā prāṇanagbhyāmityatra masjinaśorjhali iti num yadyeva yathā prāṇanagbhyāmityatra na num tathā naśervā iti naśadhātvāśrita kutvamapi pakṣe na syāt ucyate padasya kutvavidhānānna dhātupratyayāśrita kutva numāgamastu dhātupratyayāśrita eva imāmeva paribhāṣāmavalambyopayaṭkāmyatītyatra kāmyacaḥ kakārasyānitsajñā śriyau śriyo bhruvau bhruva ityādau prātipadikapratyayepīyaṅuvaṅau bhavataḥ oḥ supi iti varṣābhvaśca iti sūtrārambhāt parivyavebhyaḥ kriyaḥ bhuvaḥ prabhava iti nirddeśācca vārttikakārāstvanyādṛśī paribhāṣā paṭhanti dhātoḥ svarūpagrahaṇe tatpratyaya eva kāryavijñānamiti atra hi pāṭhe dṛgbhyā dṛgbhirityatrānudāttasya cardupadhasyānyatarasyām ityatrāsvarūpadhātugrahaṇāt supyapyamāgamaḥ syāt etaccāpi vibhāṣā ityatra mjervṛddhiḥ ityatra ca rakṣitena vyākhyātam etasyāḥ paribhāṣāyā dāṇḍināyanādi sūtre bhrauṇahatyaśabde tatvanipātana liṅgam tathāhi yadyeṣā na syāt tadā hanastociṇaloḥ iti ṣyañi tatva siddhamiti nipātanamanarthaka syāt atrocyate nipātanamida kutvābhāvārtha syāt ucyate na kvādeḥ iti yogavibhāgena kutva bhaviṣyati ṭilopārthamapi ca vācyam paratvāṭṭilopa bādhitvā hanastociṇaloḥ iti tasya vidyamānatvāt upadhāvṛddhyabhāvārthamapi naādivṛddhyopadhāvṛddherbādhitatvāttvāṣṭro jāgata iti yathā ñnityādisvarabādharnārthamapi na tasyeṣyamāṇatvāt   iti sīradevakṛtāyā paribhāṣāvṛttau ṣaṣthasyāṅgapādaḥ   iti ṣaṣṭhādhyāyaḥ   tanmadhyapatitastagrahaṇena gṛhyate   yo yasya madhyapātī sa tadgrahaṇena gṛhyata ityarthaḥ tena sarvaka ityatra sākackasyāpi sarvanāmatve jasaḥ śī iti śībhāvaḥ tathā vaiyākaraṇa ityatrāpyaijāgame kṛte taddhitadvārikā prātipaḍhikasajñā laukika evāya nyāyaḥ tadyathā bhaṭṭagrāma iti tatrābhaṭṭā api bhadṛvyapadeśa samāsadayanti tathāmallā api mallavyapadeśam jñāpaka cātra nedamadasorakoḥ ityatrākoriti padam yadyeṣā na syāttademadasoḥ pratiṣedha ucyamānokaci kṛte imakairamukairityatra śabdāntaratvādeva na syāt kimakoriti pratiṣedheneti yena vidhi sūtre bhāṣyakṛtoktam yadyeva katha tarhi sa eva bhagavānnedamadasorakoḥ ityatredamadasoḥ kāditi niyama kṛtvā niṣedha pratyākhyātavān ucyate asyāyamabhiprāyaḥ mābhūdidamakoriti jñāpakam etattadoḥ sulopokoranañsamāse hali ityatra yadakoriti pada tadbhaviṣyati yuvoranākau ityatra paśyāmācaṣṭe paśyayatītyatra prastāve yad dūṣaṇādika tan ṅyāppādekṛtavyūhā ityatroktam   abādhakānyapi nipātanāni bhavanti   tena purāṇaprokteṣu iti nipātanasya nityamabādhakatvāt sāyaciraprāhṇepragevyayebhyaṣṭyuṭyulau tuṭ ca iti ṭyuṭyulau tuḍāgamopibhavati tathā ca dadhataḥ purātanamunermunitāmiti bhāraveḥpurātanīrnnadīriti ca māghasya prayoga upapadyate jñāpaka cātra trayāṇāmiti siddhaye trestraya iti sūtram yadi hi bādhakānyeva nipātanāni syustadā nijāntrayāṇām iti siddha syāt yadā tvabādhakānyapi nipātanāni bhavanti tadā trīṇāmiti prayoganivṛttyartha trestraya iti sūtramarthavadbhavati anye tvāhuḥ neya paribhāṣā nāpi bhāṣyakāravacanam bādhakānyeva nipātanānīti sarvādīni ityādisūtre vyākhyātam ata eva tatraiva sūtre bhāgavṛttiḥ purātanamunermunitāmiti purātanīrnnadīriti ca pramādapāṭhāvetau gatānugatikatayā kavayaḥ prayuñjate na teṣā lakṣaṇa cakṣuriti   aṅgādhikāre tasya taduttarapadasya ca   tenāsthidadhītyādiā priyāsthnā priyadadhnetya trāpyanaṅ bhavati grahaṇavatā prātipadikenetyasyāyamapavādaḥ jñāpaka cātra yujerasamāsa ityatrāsamāsagrahaṇam  taddhyaśvayugityatra nummābhūdityevamartha kriyate yadi cāṅgādhikāre taduttarapadasyāpi kārya na bhavati tadā yujernnumyaśvayuji kaḥ prasaṅgo  yanniṣedhārthamasamāsagrahaṇa syāditi    pratyeka vākyaparisamāptiḥ   iha śāstre pratyeka vākyāni parisamāpyante yathā vṛddhisajñā pratyekamādaicām guṇasajñā cādeṅām laukika evāya nyāya ubhe abhyastam ityatra bhāṣyakāreṇa vyākhyātaḥ taduktam devadattayajñadattaviṣṇumitrā bhojyantāmityukte na punarucyate pratyekamitiatha ca pratyeka bhojyanta iti atra śabdaśaktireva pramāṇam jñāpakamapyatra ṇaluttama ityatrottamagrahaṇa ṇalo viśeṣaṇam yadi hi pratyeka vākyasambandho na syāttadottamagrahaṇamiḍvasmasā trikeṇa sambaddhamiti ṇalaḥ kevalasya viśeṣaṇa na syāt   kva cit samudāye vākyaparisamāptiḥ   yathā halonantarāḥ sayoga iti sayogasajñāvidhānam etadartha sayoga iti mahatī sajñā kṛteti nyāsakṛtoktam laukika evāya nyāyo vṛddhirādaijityatra bhāṣye darśitaḥ gargāḥ śata daṇḍyantāmiti samudāyenārthino rājānohiraṇyena bhavantīti na cātra pratyeka daṇḍayanti atrāpi śabdaśaktireva pramāṇam ke cidatra yuktimāhuḥ śatamatra pradhāna karma gargāstu guṇakarma tadaṅgatvāt guṇabhede ca pradhānabhedo na yuktaḥ jñāpakamapyāhuḥ prathayoḥ pūrvasavarṇa ityatra prathamādvitīyayorvvacanaṣaṭkayoḥ prayukta prathamayoriti padam prathamāśabdo hi yadi supā trikasya svaujasiti samudāyasya sañjñā syāt sāmīpyāccāmauṭśasiti trikeṣu prayujyate tadā prathamayoriti nirddeśaḥ sādhīyān bhavati  yadi tu pratyeka prathamāśabdaḥ syāttadā sorekavacanasya prathamāśabdena grahaṇa syāt sāmīpyāccāma iti lāghavārtha svamorityeva kuryāt tasmātprathamayoḥ iti nirddeśena samudāyena vākye parisamāpti bodhayati yatheṣṭa ca pakṣayorāśrayaṇam ke cittu yathā vākyaparisamāptirityāhuḥ yathā gargaiḥ saha na bhoktavyamiti pratyeka na bhujyate samuditaiśceti  tena svādividhivākyasya bahuṣu bahuvacanam ityādinā karmaṇi dvitīyā ityādinā ca śāstreṇaikavākyatāpattau tatra tatrābhidhīyamānāvupayujyate  iti    abhedakā iha śāstre guṇāḥ   tena vṛddhirādaic ityudāttasvaritānāmādaicā vṛddhisañjñāsiddhiḥ loke guṇānā bhedakatvamabhedakatva ca yathaikamudakamida śītamidamuṣṇamiti guṇabhedādbhidyate  abhedakatva ca yathā devadatto gauro lohitaḥ kṛṣṇo vā vṛddho veti svāmabhikhyā na jahāti eva ca śāstra ubhayagrahaṇe prāpte niyamoyam  aya cārthaścaturanaḍuhorāmudātta ityudāttagrahaṇena jñāpitaḥ tathāsthidadhi ityatrodātta ityanenaluṅlaṅ ityatrodāttagrahaṇena ca yadi bhedakāḥ syurguṇāstadodāttaguṇayukta evākāra uccārayitavya ityudāttagrahaṇamanarthaka syāt ato jñāpakam   iti yuvapādaḥ   aupadeśikaprāyogikayoraupadeśikasyaiva grahaṇam   upadeśe bhava aupadeśikaḥ prayoge bhavaḥ prāyogikaḥ adhyātmāditvāṭṭhañ tayormadhye aupadeśikasyaiva grahaṇam tadyathā taraptamapaugha iti pratyayasyaiva tarapo ghasañjñā brāhmaṇitareti na tu taratareppratyaye kṛte yaḥ prayogastasya nadītara iti yadi tu syād gharūpa iti hrasvaḥ syāt jñāpaka cātra śvīdito niṣṭhāyām iti śvigrahaṇam  yadi prāyogikasyāpi grahaṇamabhaviṣyat tadā samprasāraṇe kṛte śūnaḥ śūnavānityatrogantatvādeva śyukaḥ kiti itīṭpratiṣedhaḥ siddha iti śvigrahaṇa  na kuryāt  etaccāyuktam ekāca upadeśe ityata upadeśagrahaṇānuvṛtteḥ śyukaḥ kiti ityanenopadeśa ugantātpratiṣedhaḥ śūna ityatra tu nopadeśa ugantatvamapi tu prayoge tathā ca śvīdito niṣṭhāyām ityatra rakṣitaḥ upadeśagrahaṇānuvṛtteḥ śyukaḥ kiti iti pratiṣedho na prāpnotīti śvigrahaṇamiti ucyate jñāpakavādinoyamabhiprāyaḥ śyukaḥ kiti ityatropadeśādhikāro na svīkriyate an caiva tīrṇamityādāviṭpratiṣedhābhāvaḥ prāpnoti śvīdito niṣṭhāyām ityatra śvigrahaṇenaupadeśikogantādiṭpratiṣedhāt nanu śvigrahaṇamiṭpratiṣedhārthamayuktam uḍḍīna ityetadudo dittvādeveḍāgamābhāvasya siddhatvāt ki ca paribhāṣāyāḥ prayojana nāsti taraptamapau ityatra tamapā sāhacaryāllakṣaṇaparibhāṣayā ca pratyayasyaiva tarapo grahaṇāt tathopadeśāvasthāyā pakārasyetsañjñālope kṛte guṇaparavelāyā pakārābhāvāttarapsamudāyo nāstīti katha nadītara ityatra ghasañjñāśañkā ki ca yadīya paribhāṣāsti tadā kimupadeśejanunāsika ityādāvupadeśagrahaṇena ucyate ādyastāvanna bhavati prapañcārthatvāt dvitīyopi na upāyasyānupāyatopālambho na rūpāya gauravamiti vacanāt tṛtīyopi na sarvatraivetsajñāyā lope kṛte bhūtapūrvagatyā pakāramāśritya sajñāvidhānāt caturthopi na paribhāsāśrayāpekṣayā prakriyālāghavārthatvāt   sarvavidhibhya iḍvidhirbalavān   tena śvayitvetyatra samprasāraṇāt pūrvamiḍāgama eva bhavati tathā na tkvā seṭ ityakittvātsamprasāraṇābhāvaḥ jñāpaka cātra sani grahaguhośca ityatrokonukarṣaṇārtha cakārakaraṇam anyathā rurūṣatīttyatreko jhal iti sanaḥ kittve śyukaḥ kiti ityeveṭpratiṣedhaḥ siddha iti kimukonukarṣaṇārthena cakāreṇapaśyati tvācāryonyatreḍvidhirbalavāniti prathamatastasminkṛte jhalāditvābhāvātkittva nāstītyukonukarṣaṇa karoti   lugvikaraṇālugvikaraṇayoralugvikaraṇasyaiva grahaṇam   tena gopoṣṭak ityalumvikaraṇasyaiva pibatergrahaṇam na tu lugvikaraṇasya pāteḥ satsūddhiṣādi sūtre vidagrahaṇa eṣā na pravarttate yujavida ityakārāntasyopādānādgaṇe yekārāntā vidadhātavo vida jñāne vida vicāraṇe vida sattāyāmiti te sarve gṛhyante tasyāścāstitve svaratisūtisūyati ityatra sūtimūyatyorvikaraṇanirddeśo jñāpakaḥ tatra hyaktam sūṅiti sāmānyanirddeśotu tata evādādikadaivādikayorgrahaṇa bhaviṣyati na sū preraṇe ityasya tatki vikaraṇanirddeśenaeva tarhi jñāpayatyastīya paribhāṣā sūṅgrahaṇe lumvikaraṇaparibhāṣayā daivādikasyaiva grahaṇa syāt nādādikasyavikaraṇenobhayornnirddeśaḥ kriyamāṇosyā jñāpako bhavati nanu ca sūtiriti śtipā nirddeśaḥ kva cit śtipi pitkārya na bhavatīti jñāpanārthaḥ tena śtipopittvān ṅittvena sūti ityatra kṅiti ca iti guṇapratiṣedhaḥ sidhyati tathā manyakarmaṇyanādare vibhāṣā ityatra manutergrahaṇa mābhūdityatra manuteriti gaṇābhāvena sidhyati ucyate sūtisūyatīti vikaraṇanirddeśaḥ pittvābhāva bodhayanneva paribhāṣāstitva jñāpayati anyathā yadi vikaraṇanirddeśasya pittvābhāvajñāpanameva kevala prayojana syāttadā sūtīti nirddeśa kṛtvā sūṅgrahaṇameva kṛta syāt svaratisūtisūṅdhūṅūdito  veti  atrāpi sūtisūṅorupādāna pittvābhāvajñāpanārtha bhaviṣyati atra tu lugvikaraṇālumviraṇayorlumvikaraṇasyaiva grahaṇamiti viparītortho na jñāpyate na hyaniṣṭārthā śāstre prakḷptiryujyata itivacanāt vettervibhāṣā ityatra vetteriti śtipā nirddeśācca tasya hyetatprayojanam lumvikaraṇaparibhāṣayā raudhādikasya vida vicāraṇe ityasya grahaṇa mābhūditi  yadi ca lumvikaraṇālumvikaraṇayorlumvikaraṇasyaiva grahaṇamiti syāttadā vida ityapi kṛte vida jñāna ityasyaiva grahaṇa bhaviṣyati ki śtipā  nirddeśena  na ca yaṅlugnivṛttyarthamiti vācyam śīṅo ruṭ ityatra śīṅoyaṅluggrahaṇena sāhacaryācca yaṅluggrahaṇābhāvasiddheḥ   vartsyatpravṛttyeha kāryāṇi kriyante   bhaviṣyantī pravṛttimāśritya kāryāṇi kriyanta ityarthaḥ yathā śadeḥ śita ityanena bhāvinā śittvena śīyata ityatrātmanepadam tathā ninyaturninyurityatra bhaviṣyadanekāctvena dvirvacanāt prāgevairanekācosayogapūrvasya iti yaṇādeśaḥ anyatheyaṅ syāt jñāpaka cātra vasvekājādghasām ityekājgrahaṇamtaddhi liṭi dvirvacanasyāvaśyakatvānna kaścidekājastīti bhaviṣyadabhyāsalopapravṛtteruttarakāla bhāvī ya ekāctadartha kṛtam tadarthatā ca tadā syādyadi vartsyatpravṛttyeha kāryāṇi syuḥ nanu dvirvacanātprāgyo dhāturekāc tadarthamekājgrahaṇa syāt tatkathamuktārthasya jñāpakam ucyate dvirvacanātprāk sarve dhātava ekāca evetyekājgrahaṇamanarthaka syāt naitat svādau cirijirī paṭhyete pratyayāntāśca yenekāco dhātavastannivṛttyarthatvāt asadetat kāsyanekāca iti vaktavyamityanekājbhyo nityamāmvidhānāt jāgarttevyāvṛttyartha tarhi syāt jāgarttertdyuṣavidajāgṛtyonyatarasyām iti vikalpenāmvidhānāt ucyate yadyetadarthamekājgrahaṇa syāttadaikājgrahaṇamapanīya na jāgurityeva brūyāt aya cārthaḥjāgarttervasoriṇna bhavati natūrṇotirapi vyāvṛtyosti naitat vācya urṇorṇuvadbhāva iti ṇuvadbhāvātideśenorṇoterekāckāryeṇa bhāvyameveti jñāpakameva dvirvacane kṛte yadaikāctva bhavati tadaiva tadarthatvāt yukta caitat anyathā ghasigrahaṇamanarthaka syāt ghasibhasorhali ca iti lopātprāk paratvādekāca ityanenaivātreḍāgamena bhavitavyam tatra hi kṛte gamahanajanakhanaghasām ityupadhālopasya dvirvacaneci iti sthānivadbhāvātsiddhañjakṣivāniti ucyate jñāpakavādinoyamabhiprāyaḥ ekājgrahaṇāttāvatkṛtadvirvacanānāmiṭā bhavitavyam sa ceṭ dvirvacanātprāg yadi kriyate tadā paratvanyāyo na laṅghito bhavati tathā ca vasvekājāt iti sūtre rakṣitaḥdvirvacanotpatteḥ prāgeva paratvādiḍāgama iti ghasigrahaṇa tu pratyākhyāyata eveti atha vāna upadhālopinonyatarasyām iti bhaviṣyadupadhālopino ṅībvīdhāna jñāpakam anyathā sati ṅīpyupadhālopaḥ satyupadhālope ca ṅībityasaṅgatiḥ syāt atha vartsyatpravṛcyeti katham yāvatā sayoge guru iti gurusajñābādhanālladhūpadhaguṇo na prāpnoti ucyate vihitaviśeṣaṇasvīkāre laghūpadhādvihita yatsārvadhātukamārddhadhātuka vā tasmin guṇa ityadoṣaḥ na caiva kuṇḍitetyatra guṇaprasaṅgaḥ dhātugrahaṇena dhātūpadeśa eva numpravṛtteḥ vihitaviśeṣaṇena tarhi ruṇaddhityatrāpi guṇaḥ syāt eva tarhi nābhyastasyāci piti sārvadhātuka ityatrājgrahaṇātsayoge guṇo bhaviṣyati anyathā hi nenektītyatra guṇabhāvārthamacītyarthaka syāt naivam anenegityatra guṇapratiṣedhābhāvārthatvādajgrahaṇasya eva tarhi prakṛtipratyayayorhalorāntarye gurusajñā na bhavati trasigṛdhidhṛṣikṣipeḥ knuḥ iti knoḥ kitkaraṇāt halantācca iti laghūpadhaguṇapratiṣedhārthāt kittvācca taduktam knusanoryatkṛta kittva jñāpaka syāllaghorguṇa iti yadyeva dṛḍhaḥ sthūlabalayoḥ ityatra tarhi nyāse yadukta tadasagatam tatra hyuktam kimartha hakāralopo nipātyate yāvatā ho ḍhaḥ iti ḍhatve kṛte ḍho ḍhe lopa ityeva siddha dṛḍha iti satya siddhyati draḍhīyānityatra tu rephādeśo na siddhyati ra ṛto halāderlaghoḥ iti karttavye ḍhalopasyāsiddhatvād gurusajñayā laghusajñābādhanāt ucyate eva manyate guṇa eva karttavye gurusajñā na pravarttate ato raphādeśe karttavye syādeva gurusajñā tathā ca kḷptaśikha ityatra guroranṛtonantyasyāpyekaikasya prācām iti gurutvāt pluto bhavatyeva etaccāyuktam ato halāderlaghīḥ ityatra pratyudāhṛtamiṭītyevāpākṣīditi tasya dvyaṅgavaikalyāt tathāhi yathā sijiḍādirnna bhavati tathā laghurakāropisayogagurutvena laghutvasya bādhanāt tarhyevammanyate draḍhīyānityatra jñāpakasiddha na sarvatreti laghusajñayā na bhavitavyam tathā kḷptaśikha ityatrāpi gurusajñaiva bhavati  atha vā yatra pratyaye prakṛtihalā sayogastasminneva pratyaye yadi laghusajñākāryaprāptistadaiva knusanoḥ kittvāj jñāpakād gurusajñā na  bhavati jñāpakasya tulyatvāt  tathāhi bhettetyādau tṛci guṇaprāptiḥ apākṣīdityatrāpi sici vṛddhiprāptiḥ parasmaipadagrahaṇa tu sico viśeṣaṇam draḍhayati draḍīyānityatra tu ṇāvīyasuni ca rephādeśo na tu kte kḷptaśikha ityatrāpi na ktāśrayaḥ plutopi tu prakṛtipratyayasayogāśrayaḥatotra gurusajñaiveti anyastvāha knoḥ kittvādgurutvena laghutva na bādhyate api tūbhayasajñāsamāveśaḥ kriyate tena bhettetyādau satyapi gurutve laghvāśrayo bhavatyeva guṇaḥ kḷptaśikha ityatrāpi gurusajñāśrayaḥ plutaḥ apākṣīdityatrāpi laghvāśrayā vṛddhiḥ syāt  ra ṛto halāderlaghoḥ ityanena tu kumbhīdhānyanyāyena laghusajñakasyaiva ṛkārasya rephādeśa ityāśaṅkānirāsārtha hakāralopanipātana nyāsakṛtoktam aya bhāvaḥ anyathā ḍhalopasyāsiddhatvādgurusajñakoyamṛkāro na ta laghusajñaka eveti rephādeśo na syāt   antaraṅgānapi vidhīn bahiraṅgo lug bādhate   antaraṅgānapi numādīn bādhitvā bahiraṅgo lugeva pravarttate tena gomān priyosya gomatpriyaḥ gomānivācarati gomatyate ityatra supo luki kṛte sarvanāmasthānābhāvānnumna pravarttate pratyayalakṣaṇa na nāsti na lumatāṅgasya iti niṣedhāt iya paribhāṣā pratyayottarapadayośca ityatra bhāṣya kāreṇa jñāpitā tatra hyuktam  tavāya tvadīyo mamāya madīya ityādau chapratyaye tava putrastvatputrī mama putrī matputra ityādau cottarapade vibhaktyāśrayatvāttvamāvekavacana  ityanenaiva tvamau bhaviṣyataḥ  samāsottarakālabhāvī lug bahiraṅgaḥ sa paścād bhaviṣyati na ca nimittāpāyaparibhāṣayā tvamāvapi nivartteta yato bahiraṅgasya lukosiddhatvādvidyata eva nimittasiddhau pūrveṇa tvamāviti ki pratyayottarapadayośca ityanena tadetkṛta jñāpayati astīya paribhāseti tena tvamau bādhitvā vibhaktiluki kṛte vibhaktyābhāvātpūrveṇa tvamau na prāpnuta iti vacanamarthavadbhavati  nanu tvattaro mattara iti tarapi tvamau yathā syātāmiti pratyayagrahaṇa syāt prātipadikamātrādeva tarabādayaḥ svārthikā vidhīyante na tu subantāt  samarthādhikāranivṛtteḥ  tathā ca samarthānā prathamāddhā ityatra vyākhyāta svārthikapratyayāvadhiścāyamadhikāra iti uttarapadagrahaṇamapi karttavyam tava putrastvatputrastubhya hita tvaddhitamityatra tavamamau ṅasi tubhyamahyau ṅayi iti bādhitvā tvamau yathā syātām  anyathā yathā tava tubhyamityatra tavabubhyau bhavatastathātrāpi syātām pratyayottarapadayośca iti sūtre tu kṛte tayorapavādau tvamāveva kriyete  iti katha jñāpakam  ucyate ādyastāvadadoṣaḥ yataḥ svārthikā api nivṛttepi samarthādhikārentaraṅgatvāt supi kṛte suvantādeva bhavantīti vyavasthitam tathā ca kutsita ityatra sūtre bhāṣyam  svārthamabhidhāya śabdo nirapekṣo dravyamāha tatsamaveta samavetasya ca liṅga sakhyā vibhaktiścābhidhāya tataḥ priyakutsanādiṣu varttatesau  vibhaktyanta iti  tasmātsubantasyaiva priyakutsanādayorthā viśeṣamiti subantādeva tarabādaya iti yuktamukta pratyayagrahaṇa jñāpakamiti  ye tu manyante tarabādiprakṛtestarabādividhau ṅyāpprātipadikasyaiva svabhāvataḥ puruṣādyathāvṛttitvamityanavakāśatvāt supa bādhitvā prātipadikādeva  tarabādibhirbhavitavyamiti tamate naiva tarabādividhau ṅyāpprātipadikādityanuvarttate iti vṛttāvuktam  tathā svādiṣvasarvanāmasthāna ityatra rājataro rājatama ityudāhṛtam tanmate pratyayagrahaṇa na jñāpakamityāhuḥ uttarapadagrahaṇameva jñāpakam dvitīyopyadoṣaḥ  tathāhi yadi tavatubhyādeśa bādhitvā pratyayottarapadayoścetyanena bhavitavya tadotsargasamānatvādapavādānām maparyantasyaiva tau bhaviṣyato  na sarvasyeti ki maparyantasyetyanukarṣaṇārthena cakāreṇeti  tavatubhyādeśabādhanayā bhavitavyam tadā cakāreṇa maparyantasyetyanukarṣaṇa yatkṛta tadanarthaka syāt tasyaitatprayojana sarvādeśārthatve tu sarvādeśaḥ syāt atastannirāsārtha cakāreṇa maparyantasyetyanukaṣaṇamupapadyate   iti paribhāṣāvṛttau sicipādaḥ   satyapi sambhave bādhana bhavati   kva ciditi śeṣaḥ tena varttamānaktena bhūtaktasya bādhātathauniniṣatītyatra dvitīyadvirvacanena prathamadvirvacanasyatathā tvāṣṭro jāgata ityatrādyajvddhyā aco ṅiti ityasyāta upadhāyā ityasya ca bādhanam laukika evāya nyāyaḥ yathā brāhmaṇebhyo dadhi dīyatā takra kauṇḍinyāyeti jñāpaka cātrānuśatikādiṣu puṣkarasacchabdapāṭhaḥ anyathā hi bhinnaviṣayatvādādyajvṛddhyopadhāvṛrddhirnna bādhitavyeti siddha pauṣkarasādirityanartha pāṭho bhavet  nanu puṣkarasadā jitamityatrārthe tena dīvyati khanati iti ṭhaki kṛte pauṣkarasādika ityatra ṭhaki vṛddhyarthaḥ pāṭhaḥ syāt kiti hyupadhāvṛddhirnāsti  ñṇiti tadvidhānāt  ucyate ṭhagevātra nāsti anabhidhānāt ke cittu vibhāṣā supo gahuc purastāt ityatra vibhāṣāgrahaṇa jñāpakamāhuḥ tanna yato vibhāṣāgrahaṇa kalpavādīnā pakṣe vidhānārtha vṛttau vyākhyātam anyathā hyasati vibhāṣāgrahaṇe nityameva bahuci sati kalpabādayo na syuḥ na ca vācyam pūrvadeśe bahuc paradeśe kalpabādayo bhaviṣyantīti yato bahuci kṛte tenaiveṣadasamāptyarthasya dyotitatvādabhihitebhidhāna nāsti kimpunardyotite dyotanamiti kalpabādayo na prapnuvantyeva etacca tatra nyāsakṛtā vyākhyātam na hyavaśya deśakṛta eva sāmānyaviśeṣarvirodho bhavati ki tvarthakṛtopi bahucaḥ kalpabādibhiḥ samānortha iti bahucā dyotitatvādabhihite punarabhidhāna nāsti ki punardyotite punardyotanamiti tasyārthetyādinā grantheneti   parjanyavadiha lakṣaṇapravṛttiḥ   iha parjanyavanmeghavallakṣaṇa pravarttate taduktam kṛtakāri khalvida śāstra meghavannākṛtakāri ḍhahanavatdahano hi dagdha na dahati tena khaṭvātakamityādau dīrghaḥ siddhyati megho hi jalepi varṣati jñāpaka cātra pravāhaṇasya ḍhe ityanena pravāhaṇasyāpatya prāvāhaṇeya iti śubhrāditvāḍ ḍhaki uttarapadavṛddhividhānam tatra pūrvapadasya praśabdasya vibhāṣottarapadasya tu vāhanasya dīrghasyāpyākārasya nitya vṛddhiḥ nanu pravāhaṇeya ityatrottarapadavṛddheḥ ki prayojanam pravāhaṇeyībhārya ityatra vṛddhinimittasya ca taddhitasyāraktavikāre iti puvadbhāvapratiṣedhaḥ prayojanamiti cet  na jāteśca ityanenaiva tatsiddheḥ jātitva cāsya gotra ca caraṇaiḥ saheti jāteśca ityatra svāṅgāccetyatomāninītyanuvṛttermānini puvadbhāvaniṣedho nāṣti pravāhaṇeyamāninī tataścātra na vṛddhinimittasya iti puvadbhāvapratiṣedhārtha vṛddhividhānadamiti  yadyeva katha tatra tarhi nyāsakṛtā vyākhyāta jāteśca iti puvadbhāvapratiṣedhe siddhe vṛddhinimittasya iti puvadbhāvapratiṣedhārtha pravāhaṇasya  ṭha iti vṛddhividhāna jāteśca ityasyānityatva jñāpayati tena hāstikamityatra jāteśca iti pavadbhāvapratiṣedho na bhavatīti ucyate vyaktau tadā jñāpaka boddhatvyam   garbhavaṭṭābādayo bhavanti   yathā madhye garbhastathāḥ strīpratyayāḥ prātipadikasvādyormmadhye bhavanti kā ke kā iti kādeśe kṛte ṭabbhavati ādigrahaṇādarvaṇastrasāvanaña iti vibhaktau cādeśe kṛte ugitaśca iti ṅīp arvatyau arvatya iti ke cidāhuḥ kroṣṭuśabdādvibhaktau striyā ca iti tṛjvadbhāve kroṣṭrībhyā kroṣṭībhirityinye jñāpaka cātra na yāsayoḥ itīttvapratiṣedhārtha vacanam yadi garbhavaṭṭābādayo na syustadā vibhaktau tyadādyatve kṛte garbhavaṭṭāpobhāvāt yakā saketi na syāt eva ca pratyayasthāt itīttvaprāpterabhāvānna yāsayoḥ ityanarthaka syāt śrīpuruṣottamadevena tu vyākhyātam jñāpaka ca na yāsayorittvapratiṣedhavacanam yadi na garbhavaṭṭāp syāttadā tyadādyatve kṛte supaḥ pareṇa syād yakā saketi na syāt eva ca pratyayasthāt itīttvaprāpterabhāvānna yāsayoḥ ityanarthaka syāt śrīpuruṣottamadevena tu vyākhyātam jñāpaka ca na yāsayorittvapratiṣedhavacanam yadi na garbhavaṭṭāp syāttadā tyadādyatve kṛte supaḥ pareṇa syād yakā saketyatra pratyayasthāt itīttvaprāptireva nāsti supaḥ paratvādāpaḥ tatki pratiṣedheneti   vidhau paribhāṣopatiṣṭhate nānuvāde   tena kṅiti ca ityatra kṅitītyasya guṇavṛddhibhyā sambandhāttasminniti nirdiṣṭa iti paribhāṣā nopatiṣṭhate tena kaṅinnimitte pratyaye niṣedhādbhinnamityatrāpi niṣedhaḥ siddhyati pradhānāpradhānanyāyalabdhoyamarthaḥ jñāpaka cātrodīcāmātaḥ sthāna ityatra sthānapratipattyartha sthānagrahaṇam avyāpikā ceya sakhyāvyayādeḥ ityatrādigrahaṇāt anyathā sakhyāvyayābhyāmityevocyeta aya cārthaḥ sakhyāvyayābhyāmuttaro ya ūdhaḥśabdastadantāntādbahuvrīherṅobiti nanveva sakhyāvyayābhyāmuttara ūdhaḥśabdānto yo bahuvrīhiriti syāttataścehaiva syāt pañcaghaṭoghṇaḥ pañcaghaṭoghnīti bhavati hyatra sakhyāvyayābhyāmuttara ūdhaḥśabdānto bahuvrīhi ucyate pratyāsattyodhaḥśabda eva sakhyāvyayayorviśeṣyo na bahuvrīhiḥtathāhi sakhyāvyayābhyāmityatrodhaśśabda eva pratyāsanno netaraḥ nanvevamapi tripade bahuvrīhau na prāpnoti tadartha yatna āstheyaḥ   prakṛtigrahaṇe ṇyadhikasyāpi grahaṇa bhavati   tena heracaṅi iti hinoterṇyantādapi sani kṛte jighāyiṣatīti kutva bhavati  abhiṣāvayati pariṣāvayatītyatra tu sunotimeva prati kriyāyogo na tu sāvayati pratītyupasargātsunoti iti ṣatvamiti vṛttavukta na tvanayā paribhāṣayeti jñāpaka cātra heracaṅi iti pratiṣedhaḥ yadi prakṛtigrahaṇe ṇyadhikasya grahaṇa na syāt tadā kevalasya hinoteraṅgasyābhysanimittapratyaye kutvamucyamāna kaḥ prasaṅgo ṇyadhike syāt yadarthamacaṅīti pratiṣedhaḥ kriyata iti avyāpikā ceyam na bhādi sūtre ṇyantānā bhādīnāmupasakhyānamiti vacanāt tenārha ityatra ṇyantasyārhatergrahaṇa na bhavatīti rakṣitenoktam   aṅgavṛtte punaraṅgavṛttāvavidhirnniṣṭhitasya   aṅgakāryasya vṛttiḥ pravṛttiraṅgavṛttistato hetornniṣṭhitasya prayogārhasyāṅgasya punaraṅgakāryapravṛttāvavidhiravidhāna bhavati aṅgavṛttāviti saptamī ṣaṣṭhyarthe punaraṅgakāryavṛtteravidhiravidhānamaniṣpattirityarthaḥ tena pibatītyatra pibādeśe kṛte laghūpadhaguṇo na bhavat iya ca paribhāṣā bhāṣye jñājanorjjā ityatra jyādādīyasa ityatra ca jñāpitā tathāhi pūrvatroktam kimartha jābhāvo vidhīyate na jabhāva eva vidhīyatām tatrāpyato dīrgho yañi ityanena siddhyatyeva jāyata iti uttaratrāpyukta jyātparasyeyasaḥ pratyayasyāttva kimarthamucyate na prakṛto lopa eva vidhīyatām tasminnapi kṛtekṛtsārvadhātukayoḥ ityanena jyāyānini siddhyatyeva tasmārpūrvatra jābhāva itaratra tvākāravidhānamubhayamapi jñāpakamastīya paribhāṣeti nyāsakāraḥ punarāha pratipattilāghavārtha dīrghāntādeśavidhāna hrasvepi hi kṛteto dīrgho yañi ityeva jānātīti siddhyati nanu cāṅgavṛttaparibhāṣayā na prāpnoti naitat niṣṭhitasyetyucyate na hi ja ityādeśe kṛte niṣṭhitamaṅga bhavati aprayogārhatvāt jyādādīyasa ityasya jñāpakatvamuktam akṛtsārvadhātukayoḥ ityatra kṅidgrahaṇānanuvṛttyā ananuvṛttiścoruyetyādau chāndasatvāddīrthābhāvasiddheḥ   iti paribhāṣāvṛttau devikapādaḥ   pūrvatrāsiddhīye na sthānivat   tena papaktiryā yaṣṭirityatra pūrvatrāsiddhādhikārīye kutve ṣatve ca karttavyeto lopasyāsthānivattvājjhalādau kutva ṣatva ca siddhyati nanu pāpaktiryā yaṣṭirityatra yaṅoci ca iti hyajjhalsamudāyasya lope kṛte halacorādeśe na sthānivaditi siddham naitat ato lopa ityakāralope kṛte yaṅoci ca iti yakāramātrameva lupyate kuta etat na padāntādi sūtre yāyāvara ityatra sthānivadbhāvapratiṣedhārthādvaregrahaṇāt samudāyalope hi sthānivattvaprāptyabhāvādvare sthānivattvapratiṣedhonarthaḥ syāt yadyeva na dhātulopa ārddhadhātuka ityanarthakam yaṅokārasya sthānivattvena loluvaḥ popuva ityādeḥ siddhatvāt eva tarhi na dhātulopa sūtrasāmarthyādaci pratyaye lopaḥ samudāyasyaiva kriyata iti jñāpyate anyatra tu pratyeka tena sanīsrasa ityādi siddhyat tathā sanīsrasako danīdhvasaka iti yadyeva niṣṭhā śīṅ ityatra yannyāsakṛtīkta śīṅo ṅitkaraṇasya prayojana yaṅluki kittvapratiṣedho mā bhūccheśyitaḥ śeśyitavāniti tadasagatam niṣṭhāyāḥ satyapyakittve yaṅokārasya sthānivattvena guṇāprasaṅgāt eva tarhyārddhadhātuka ityasya viṣayasaptamītvamāśritya tatra vyākhyātam yadi cāci lopaḥ samastasyaivānyatra tu niyamo nāṣtīti vākyārthaḥ tena pratyeka samudāyasyāpi lopaḥ ato yadā samudāyalopastadhā śeśyita ityatrākittvapratiṣedhārtha ṅitkaraṇamiti nyāsakārasyābhiprāyaḥ iya ca paribhāṣā nāglopiśāsvṛditām ityatra bhāṣye jñāpitā  tatra hyuktamacakathadityādāvajādeśasya sthānivattvādeva ṇau hrasvo na bhaviṣyati kimaglopinā neti pratiṣedhena tata ukta yatra sthānivadbhāvo  nāsti tadarthamatyararājaditi na hyatra ṭilopojādeśaḥ ki tarhi halacorādeśa iti tataḥ punarukta na tarhyaglopinā neti pratiṣedhotra prāptoti  na hyatrāgeva lupyate ki tarhyanyopi atha yotrāglupyate tadāśrayo niṣedhaḥ eva tarhi yoj lupyate tadāśrayaḥ sthānivadbhāvopi bhaviṣyatītyutkvopasahṛtam  eva tarhi yadaglopinā neti pratiṣedha śāsti tato jñāpayatyācārya iti ārabhyottaratra sthānivadbhāvo na bhavatīti tena pūrvatrāsiddhīye na  sthānivaditi vaktavyanna bhavatīti  anye tvāhuḥ halacorādeśo na sthānivaditi ata eva nāglopiśāsvṛditām ityatra rakṣitenoktam halacorādeśe na sthānivaditi yadi hi syāttadā sthūlādīnā yaṇādilopevādeśo vaktavyaḥ syāt sthavīyāniti anye ca bahavo doṣā uktāḥ tasmāddhalacorādeśe na sthānivaditi iha punaraglopigrahaṇasāmarthyāt samudāyalopepyaglopītyāśrīyate kevalāglope pratiṣedhasyānarthakyāditi bhāṣyaṭīkāyā nirūpitam nanu sthavīyānityādāvavādeśo vaktavyaḥ syāditi kathamucyate yāvatākārasya sthānivattvādavādeśaḥ syādeva ucyate halacorādeśe na sthānivadityasminnasati samudāyasya sthānivattvādavādeśo na syāt naitat acaḥ sthānivattvamucyate na samudāyasya ucyate yathātra yo hyubhayoḥ sthāne sampadyata iti vacanādajjhalādeśasyāpyajādeśavyapadeśastathānajādeśavyapadeśopyasti tadeva yadānajvyapadeśastadāvādeśo vaktavyaḥ syādityuktam yadetaduktamihāglopigrahaṇasāmarthyātsamudāyalopepyaglopītyāśrīyate kevalālope pratiṣedhasyānarthakatvāditi etaccāglope sāmānyajñāpaka tena dṛṣadamākhyadadadṛṣadityatrāganaglopepyaglopa iti pratiṣedhāddīrgho laghoḥ iti na bhavati anyathāganaglopeglopavyapadeśo na syātacakathadityatra kevalāglopeglopapratiṣedhasya caritārthatvātna ceda sthānivadbhāvena siddhyati dīrghavidhau tanniṣedhāt anityā ceyam na padāntādi sūtre dvirvacanagrahaṇāt tena vetasvānityacākāralopasya sthānivattvādasakārāntapada bhavatīti rutvābhāvaḥ tathā kuṭādītyatrākārasya sthānivatvādṛkārasyāpadāntatvena jaśtvābhāvaḥ nanvekādeśasya pūrvagrahaṇena ṭakārasya padāntatva nāsti ucyate paragrahaṇa yuktam yathā śakyate vidhiḥ karttumiti nyāyāt satyam yatra parāśrito vidhiryathā vṛkṣādityatra supaḥ paragrahaṇāt suptvātpadatva kuṭādītyatra na paragrahaṇāśrita jaśtvam na hi jaśtvamākāramapekṣate ucyate yadyapi jaśtvamākāramapekṣate ucyate yadyapi jaśtvasyākāro nimitta na bhavati tathāpi paragrahaṇe sati kuḍiti ṭakārānta pada bhavatīti jaśtvasya paragrahaṇameva nimittam nanu satyapi paragrahaṇe jaśtvannāsti ṭakārasyāpadāntatvāt akārānta hi pada tataḥ subvidhiḥ ucyate paragrahaṇe kṛte ekadeśavikāradvāreṇa ṭakārānta padam naitat antādivattva ekadeśavikārābhāvātanyathā hi vṛkṣamityatrāpyekādeśasya pūrvagrahaṇemakārasyakadeśavikāradvāreṇa suptve supi ca iti dīrghaḥ syādeva eva cobhayata āśraye nāntādivaditi vyartha syāt ucyate yatra vidhirubhayamāśrayati ekamantādivattvenāparamekadeśavikāradvāreṇa tatraikadeśavikārasvīkāro yathā vṛkṣamiti kuṭādītyatra na jaśtva paramākāramāśrayatīti yuktamekadeśavikāriṇaṣṭakārasya padāntatvamiti nanu tathāpyatra padāntavidhau jaśtve karttavye padāntavidhi prati na sthānivaditisthānivattvapratiṣedhājjaśtvena bhavitavyameva ucyate sati sthānivattvaniṣedhe padāntatva sati ca padāntatve sthānivattvaniṣedha itītaretarāśrayatvam evamapi jhalā jaśonta iti jaśtvamastyeva na cāsti sthānivattva jaśtvavidhi prati na sthānivaditi tanniṣedhāt ucyate rephāpādīye carsahacarite jhalā jaśtve karttavye sthānivattvapratiṣedha iṣyate tathā ca dhastva sagnirityudāharaṇam etacca ṭhājādāvṛddhva dvitīyādaca ityatra ṣāḍikaprastāve rakṣitenoktam   upajātanimittopyutsarga upajaniṣyamāṇanimittenāpavādena bādhyate parihṛtyāpavādaviṣayamutsargobhiniviśate   tena dadhatītyatropajātanimittopyantaraṅo jhonta ityantādeśa upajaniṣyamāṇanimittenādabhyastāt ityadādeśena bādhyate jñāpaka cātra śīṅaḥ sārvadhātuke guṇa ityatraikāre vidhātavye guṇagrahaṇam tasyaitatprayojana guṇaśrutyekaparibhāṣopasthānādika eva sthāne guṇo yathā syāditi  anyathā śete ityatra ṅakārasyetsajñā bādhitvaikāraḥ syāt tatra yadyantaraṅgastadā guṇagrahaṇamanarthaka ṅakāre luptenyathaivekārasyaikārādeśaprasaṅgāt ata eva śīṅaḥ sārvadhātuke guṇa ityapanīya sārvadhātukamapidaśīṅa iti na kṛtam na caivamadhiśayyete ityatra ṅittvapratiṣedhādāto ṅita itīyādeśo na syāditi vācyam yatośīṅa iti pañcamīnirddeśācchīṅga uttarasya pratiṣedhena bhavitavyam na cāśīṅga iti paryudāsācca sādṛśyenājantatvāccāco ṅittvena bhavitavyam paryudāsasyāgrahaṇāt atha vā na śīṅa iti pṛthageva kriyāmiti tasmātparibhāṣādvayasya jñāpakamiti upajātanimittopyutsarga upajaniṣyamāṇanimittenāpavādena bādhyata ityatrārthe ṛcchatṝtāmityatra ṛkārapraśleṣo rakṣitena jñāpaka uktaḥ yadyeṣā na syāt ṛ atusiti sthite iko re yaṇādeśe kṛte sthānivadbhāvād dvirvacane kṛteta ādeḥ iti dīghatvena siddhamāraturāruriti asyā tu satyā yaṇādeśo nāsti dvirvacane kṛte upajaniṣyamāṇanimittena sarvaṇadīrghatvena bādhitatvāt savarṇadīrghatve ca kṛte prakṛtigrahaṇena grahaṇādraturiti syāt abhyāsagrahaṇapakṣe rephalopo āto lopa iṭi ca ityākāralope cāturiti syāt ṛgatāvityasya tu grahaṇe guṇenāraturāruriti siddhyati etacca vārṇādāṅga balīya ityasyāvyāśrayatvapakṣāśrayaṇāducyate yadi tu vyāśraye vārṇādāṅga balīya iti syāt tadā savarṇadīrghatvambādhitvoradattvādika syāt ata evośca ityatra rakṣitenoktam atha vā ṛgrahaṇa tatra pratyākhyāta yata iti   ṇau kṛta sthānivat   ṇau parato yad vṛddhyādika kṛta tad dvirvacane karttavye sthānivatsyāt tena śuśāvayiṣati juhāvayiṣatītyatrābhyāsasyovarṇāntatva siddha bhavati aśūśavadityatra tu vakārasya saprasāraṇa ṇau kṛtamapi dvirvacane na sthānivadbhavati ajādeśasyaiva ṇau kṛtasya dvirvacane sthānivadityubhyupagamāt etacca dvirvacaneci ityatra bhāṣya uktam jñāpaka cātra oḥ puyaṇjyapara ityatrābhyāsaviśeṣaṇamoriti padam tena hi pavarge yaṇi jakāre cācparebhyāsasyetva vidhīyate bibhāvayiṣatītyādiṣuyadi ca ṇau kṛta vṛddhyāvādeśādikārya sthānivanna syātkathamabhyāsasyokāretva vidhīyate tulyajātīyatvājjhāpakasyāparāṇā puyuṇjā sadṛśā anyevarṇaparā eva sthānivattva bhajante tenācikīrttadityatra na sthānivadityurṛt ityatra rakṣitaḥ etattu na samyak stautiṇyoreva ṣaṇyabhyāsāt ityatra siṣedhayiṣatītyudāharaṇa ekāraparenayā sthānivattva kṛtvā dvirvacanasya pratipāditatvāt  tathaujaḍhadityatrānayā sthānivattvena dvirvacanamuktamayukta syāt tathā lopaḥ pivaterīccābhyāsasya ityatrāpīpyadityatra ṇau kṛta sthānivadbhavatīti  vṛttikṛdvacana vyāhata syāt  tasmātsāmānyena paribhāṣā jñāpakasiddha na sarvatretyacikīrttadityatra vyavasthā avaśya caitat anyathādhijigāpayiṣatītyatra kā gatiḥ anyastvāha aṅgaikadeśājādeśo ṇau kṛta sthānivaditi tenādhijigāpayiṣatītyatra sthānivattva na tacca ṇau ca saścaṅoḥ ityatra rakṣitena vyākhyātam evamapyacikorttadityatra doṣa eva   abhyāsavikāreṣvapavādā notsargānvidhīnvbādhante   abhyāsakikāreṣvapavādatvāntaraṅgatvaparatvādibhirbādhakā bādhyān vidhīnna bādhante tena mīmāsata ityatra mānvadhādinā dīrgheṇa sanyataḥ itīttva na bādhyate tathācikṣaṇadityatra sāvakāśa sanyata itīttvamacīkaradityādau dīgho laghoḥ ityanena na bādhyate jñāpaka cātra dīrghokita ityatrākiṅgrahaṇam taddhi grayamyata ityādau dīrgho mā bhūdityevamartha kriyate  yadi cābhyāsavikāreṣvapi bādhyabādhakabhāvaḥ syāttadā nugāgame kṛtenajantatvādeva dīrgho na bhaviṣyati kimakidgrahaṇena tat kṛtamuktārthasya  jñāpakamiti    iti paribhāṣāvṛttau ṇaupādaḥ   iti saptamodhyāhaḥ   pūrvatrāsiddhīyamadvirvacane   dvirvacane karttavye pūrvatrāsiddham iti na pravarttate tena drogdhādogdhā droḍhādroḍhetyatra druherjhali ghatvaḍhatvayoḥ kṛtayoḥ sarvasya dve iti dvirvacana bhavati anyathā pūrvatrāsiddham ityasiddhatvād droh tetyasya dvirvacana syāt tato vā druhamuheti ghatvavikalpaḥ tatraitanna labhyate yadā prakṛterghatva tadā dviruktasyāpīti tataśca ḍhatvamapi kadā citsyāt eva ca drogdhādroḍhetyaniṣṭa syāt nanvasiddhapāda paṭhitvā sarvasya dvepādaḥ paṭhyatā tatosiddhatva na bhaviṣyati naitat eva hi paṭhatipaṭhatitarāmityatra prakarṣapratyayātparatvena dvirvacana na syāt pūvatrāsiddhīye nāsti paratvamabhāvāduttarasyetivacanādgrāmastvekṣata ityatra ca tvāmau dvitīyāyā ityasyāsiddhatvāḍhādguṇo na syāt jñāpaka cātra sarvasya dve ityatra sarvasyeti vacanam taddhi matvarthīyākārapratyayāntam tenāyamarthaḥ sarvakāryayuktasya dvirvacana sarvakārya kṛtvā dvirvacana bhavatītyarthaḥ eva ca tadupapadyate yadyasiddhatvanna bhavatīti jñāpakam nanu sarvasyeti vacana sarvasya dvirvacanārtham anyathā parervarjana iti dvirvacanamantyasya syāt etaccāyuktam dve vidhīyeye tayoścānekāltvātsarvādeśaḥ siddha eva satyam halenteṣu paryādiṣvikārasyālontyasya syāt nanu dvāvikārau syātām tataścānekāltvādyukta sarvādeśatvam na ca dvāvikārau kṛtaikādeśāvādeśatva pratipadyete ityekāltvādādeśontyasya syāt na hyapravṛttayostayorekādeśaśāstrapravṛttirasti pravṛttikāle cānekakāltvātsarvādeśatvamiti nāstyantyasya vidhiḥ syādetat  acorddhamātre tarhi prāpnutaḥ pariśabdasyārddhamātre dve vidhīyamānelgrahaṇena cārddhamātrāyā agrahaṇādanekāltvābhesati sarvasyeti vacanentyasya  prāpnuta iti  etaccātīvāsamyak aśliṣṭasyārddhamātrādvayasyoccāraṇāyogyatvādaśakya ādeśaḥ karttum anyastvāha sarvasya dve ityatra sūtre kātyāyanavākyamida paribhāṣārūpeṇa paṭhyate pūrvatrāsiddhīyamadvirvacana iti anityā ceyam ubhau sābhyāsasya iti vacanāt tena praṇināyeti siddhyati   iti paribhāṣāvṛttau sarvasya dvepādaḥ   anityamāgamaśāsanam   tena śāka pacānasyetyāne mugna bhavati sāgara tarttumicchatītyatreḍ na bhavati jñāpaka cātrāni loṭ ityatrānītyāgamasahitasya nergrahaṇa nitye hyāgamaśāsana āṭa upādānamakṛtvā niloṭ ityeva kuryāt tathā yuvoranākau ityatra nyāse ghorlopo leṭi vā iti vāgrahaṇena jñāpitā ke cittu stoḥ ścunā ścuḥ ityakṛtanumāgamanirddeśa jñāpakamāhuḥ nanvāgamaśāsanamiti katham yāvatāmi pūrva ityekādeśasya paragrahaṇena grahaṇādantarvarttinī vibhaktimāśritya padatvānnalopena bhavitavyam ucyate acaḥ parasmin iti sthānivattvānna bhaviṣyati na cātra padāntavidhi prati na sthānivadityastiitaretarāśrayatvāt sati sthānivattvapratiṣedhe padāntatva sati ca padāntatve sthānivattvapratiṣedha iti nanvevamapi pūrvatrāsiddhīye na sthānivaditi sthānivattva na prāpnoti ucyate uttarapadatve cāpadādividhāvityuttarasya padatve karttavye pratyayalakṣaṇapratiṣedhācchāsanasya padatva nāstīti kuto nalopaḥ  yadeva ṣātpadāntāt ityatra vṛttau yadvākhyāta padentaḥ padānta iti saptamīsamāsoya teneha na bhavati susarpiṣkeṇa suyajuṣkeṇeti tadasaṅgatam tathāhi yathā susarpiṣkeṇetyatra kapratyayepade parataḥ ṣakārāntantathaivāpadāntatva ṣantasya ucyate padādividhiśabdena sātpadādyoḥ ityārabhya ye vidyayaste gṛhyante tenāpadādividhāvitivacanāduttarasya padatva bhavatyeva atra cārthe ṣātpadāntādityatra padāntagrahaṇa jñāpakam tathā ca padavyavāyepi ityatra maitreyaḥ atra ca jñāpakam ṣātpadāntādityatra padentaḥ padānta ityevamarthasya padāntagrahaṇasyopādānam na hi tadanyathā sambhavatīti atrocyate nanu yadyevamartha padāntagrahaṇa tadā tadakṛtvā ṣātsupītyeva kriyatām ṣātpada iti vā aya cārthaḥ subante parato yaḥ ṣakāraḥ pade parata iti etadevamuktārthasya jñāpaka bhaviṣyati ki caivavidhajñāpane na prayojanam ṣātpadāntāditi karttavye pratyayalakṣaṇa bhavatītyevāstu ucyate yattāvadukta supīti kriyatā pada iti vā tanna yadi tannirvahati tadā ki padāntagrahaṇasyoktārthajñāpakā vyāhanyate dvitīyamapi na  yata evavidhajñāpane druṇaso vārddhrīṇas ityādāvuttarasya naḥśabdasya padāntatvātpūrvapadātsajñāyāmaga iti ṇatva bhavati carmanāsike ṇatvābhāvaḥ anyathā mātṛbhogīṇavaccarmanāsika ityatrāpi ṇatva syāt tathā māṣakumbhavāpeneti samāsa uttarasya kumbhaśabdasya padatva bhavati tena māṣakumbhavāpenetyatra padavyavāye ṇatvapratiṣedhaḥ siddhyati anyathā pratyayalaksaṇābhāvānnimittanimittinoḥ padavyavāyo na syāt nanvatrāpi padavyāyepi itisāmarthyātpratyayalakṣaṇena padatva bhaviṣyati ucyate yadi sāmarthyādvyavasthā tadoktamprakāre niṣphalo vyāroṣaḥ nanu yadi sātpadādyoḥ ityārabhya kāryepadādividhāvitivacanāduttarasya padatva bhavati tarhi bhāvakarmaṇoḥ ityādau padāntasya iti karttavye ṇatvapratiṣedhe padatva prāpnoti tataśca padāntasya iti ṇatvapratiṣedhena bhavitavyamucyate bhāvakarmaṇoḥ iti nirddeśādadoṣaḥ nanu ca yadyuttarapadatve cāpadādividhāvityasti katha tarhi vimaladyu dinamiti yāvatātrāpyuttarapadatve cāpadādividhāvitivacanāddivaśabdasya padatva nāsti ucyate tatraiṅaḥ padāntādati ityatontagrahaṇamanuvarttate tena tadantavidhinā divaśabdāntapadasyottvamiti siddha vimaladyu dinamiti kevale tu dyubhyāmityādau vyapadeśivadbhāvāduttvam na cāsti vyapadeśivadbhāvoprādipadikeneti dyuprāgapāgudakpratīco yat ityatra nirddeśāt   nimittāpāye naimittakasyāpyapāyaḥ   nimittena nirmita naimittikam vuñchaṇādau kumudāditvāṭṭhak kāraṇāpāye tatkāryamapyapaiti tena snātītyatra mūrddhanyābhāve ṇatvamapaiti paṭubhārya ityatra ṅībnivṛttau yaṇādeśo nivarttate jñāpaka cāsyā udaḥ sthāstambhoḥ pūrvasya ityādau ṣakāranivṛttau ṭhasya thakāroccāraṇam laukikaścaiṣa savyabhicāro nyāyaḥ loke hi japākusumasannidhau sphaṭike rāgastanivṛttau nivarttatetakṣākābhāve ca prāsādostyeva tenāsyāpatyamiti prakṛterapāye pratyayo na nivarttate tathā abhūnnipa ityādau padasaskāre bhūtasāmānye luṅanadyatanāvagamavelāyā na nivarttate  etasmin pāde upasargādasamāsepi ṇopadeśasya ityatra sthāne dvirvacanapakṣepi śrutyabhedāttattvādhyavasāyena kāryāṇi pravattanta iti sopadeśānā  sicprabhṛtīnā pāṭhena sico yaṅi itipratiṣedhārthenetyādiphakkikāyā dūṣaṇa samādhana caikācpāde saprasāraṇabhāṣāyāmuktam    iti paribhāṣāvṛttau rephapādaḥ   ityaṣṭamodhyāyaḥ
